/**
 * APJ HR ABSENSI MASTER - APP-V.4.3 SECURITY LOCK & PERMISSION SYNC
 * -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 * Prinsip baru V121:
 * 1) APJ_CORE_USER adalah pusat master/pengaturan:
 *    - USER
 *    - OUTLET
 *    - ID_SHIFT
 *    - ID_JADWAL
 * 2) APJ_ABSENSI_KARYAWAN hanya untuk transaksi dan rekap:
 *    - ID_ABSENSI
 *    - REKAP_HARIAN  (rekap/laporan dari ID_ABSENSI)
 *    - REKAP_BULANAN (rekap/laporan dari ID_ABSENSI)
 * 3) Key transaksi harian: Tanggal Key + Username.
 * 4) Check In / Check Out selalu mengembalikan data final ke frontend.
 * 5) V129 membersihkan setup agar hanya memakai 3 sheet HR utama:
 *    ID_ABSENSI, REKAP_HARIAN, REKAP_BULANAN. Sheet rekap legacy tidak dibuat lagi.
 * 6) V130 mengisi REKAP_HARIAN dan REKAP_BULANAN otomatis dari ID_ABSENSI + ID_JADWAL.
 * 7) V131 membuat refresh rekap lebih aman dari error format kolom/table Google Sheets
 *    dan menambah installer trigger edit/jam untuk refresh rekap otomatis.
 * 8) V133 menambahkan endpoint Rekap Absensi dengan filter tanggal dan hak akses role.
 * 9) V142 menambahkan Export PDF Absensi per karyawan / semua karyawan ke Drive.
 * 10) V143 membuat export PDF tetap jadi walau periode belum memiliki data,
 *     sehingga owner bisa melihat template absensi kosong.
 */

// =============================================================================
// WEB APP ROUTER
// =============================================================================
function doGet(e) {
  const action = e && e.parameter && e.parameter.action;
  if (action) return routeAbsensi_(Object.assign({}, e.parameter, { action: action }));
  return json_({ sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'APJ HR Absensi Ready', version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION });
}

function doPost(e) {
  try {
    const payload = e && e.postData && e.postData.contents ? JSON.parse(e.postData.contents) : {};
    return routeAbsensi_(payload || {});
  } catch (err) {
    return json_({ sukses: false, success: false, pesan: errorMessage_(err), stack: String(err && err.stack || '') });
  }
}

      case 'refreshRekapBulananV135':
      case 'refreshRekapAbsensiV134':
      case 'refreshRekapHarianV134':
      case 'refreshRekapBulananV134':
        res = refreshRekapAbsensiV138(payload);
        break;
      case 'refreshRekapAbsensiV133':
      case 'refreshRekapHarianV133':
      case 'refreshRekapBulananV133':
        res = refreshRekapAbsensiV133(payload);
        break;
      case 'refreshRekapAbsensiV132':
      case 'refreshRekapHarianV132':
      case 'refreshRekapBulananV132':
        res = refreshRekapAbsensiV132(payload);
        break;
      case 'refreshRekapAbsensiV131':
      case 'refreshRekapHarianV131':
      case 'refreshRekapBulananV131':
      case 'refreshRekapAbsensiV130':
      case 'refreshRekapHarianV130':
      case 'refreshRekapBulananV130':
        res = refreshRekapAbsensiV131(payload);
        break;
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV147':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV147':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV146':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV146':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV145':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV145':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV144':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV144':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV138':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV138':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV137':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV137':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV136':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV136':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV135':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV135':
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV134':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV134':
        res = installAbsensiRekapTriggerV153();
        break;
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV132':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV132':
        res = installAbsensiRekapTriggerV132();
        break;
      case 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV131':
      case 'pasangTriggerRekapAbsensiV131':
        res = installAbsensiRekapTriggerV131();
        break;
      case 'hapusAbsensiRekapTriggerV132':
      case 'deleteAbsensiRekapTriggerV132':
        res = deleteAbsensiRekapTriggerV132();
        break;
      case 'hapusAbsensiRekapTriggerV131':
      case 'deleteAbsensiRekapTriggerV131':
        res = deleteAbsensiRekapTriggerV131();
        break;
      case 'listAbsensiRekapTriggerV132':
        res = listAbsensiRekapTriggerV132();
        break;
      case 'listAbsensiRekapTriggerV131':
        res = listAbsensiRekapTriggerV131();
        break;
      default:
        res = { sukses: false, success: false, pesan: 'Action tidak dikenal: ' + action, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
    }
    auditHrActionV45_(action, payload, res);
    return json_(res);
  } catch (err) {
    logServerErrorHrV45_(err, (typeof payload !== 'undefined' ? payload : {}));
    return json_({ sukses: false, success: false, pesan: errorMessage_(err), stack: String(err && err.stack || ''), version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION });
  }
}

function json_(obj) {
  return ContentService
    .createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(obj || {}))
    .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON);
}

function getHrKaryawanDataV160(payload) { return getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload || {}); }
function getHrKaryawanDataV161(payload) { return getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload || {}); }
function getHrKaryawanDataV162(payload) { return getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload || {}); }
function getHrKaryawanDataV159(payload) { return getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload || {}); }

function getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  const isAdmin = isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(currentUser);
  const usersAll = getHrKaryawanUsersV157_();
  const users = isAdmin ? usersAll : usersAll.filter(function(u) {
    return normKey_(u.username) === normKey_(currentUser.username) || normKey_(u.nama) === normKey_(currentUser.nama);
  });
  const outlets = getHrKaryawanOutletsV157_();
  const shifts = getHrKaryawanShiftsV157_();
  const jadwal = getHrKaryawanJadwalV157_(shifts);
  const activeUsers = users.filter(function(u) { return normKey_(u.status || 'AKTIF') === 'aktif'; }).length;
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    source: {
      spreadsheetId: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.CORE_SPREADSHEET_ID,
      spreadsheetName: coreSS_().getName(),
      sheets: {
        users: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.USER,
        outlets: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.OUTLET,
        shifts: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT,
        jadwal: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL
      }
    },
    scope: isAdmin ? 'ALL' : 'SELF',
    user: publicUser_(currentUser),
    summary: {
      totalKaryawan: users.length,
      karyawanAktif: activeUsers,
      totalOutlet: outlets.length,
      totalShift: shifts.length,
      totalJadwal: jadwal.length
    },
    users: users,
    karyawan: users,
    dataKaryawan: users,
    outlets: outlets,
    outlet: outlets,
    shifts: shifts,
    shift: shifts,
    idShift: shifts,
    jadwal: jadwal,
    schedules: jadwal,
    idJadwal: jadwal,
    pesan: 'Data HR Karyawan berhasil dimuat dari APJ_CORE_USER.'
  };
}

function saveHrKaryawanUserV157(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  if (!isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(currentUser)) throw new Error('Akses ditolak. Hanya OWNER/SUPERADMIN/HR/SUPERVISOR yang bisa mengubah data karyawan.');
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.USER);
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Sheet USER tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.');
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  const username = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.targetUsername, payload.usernameKaryawan, payload.username, payload.USERNAME));
  const nama = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.namaKaryawan, payload.nama, payload.name, payload.NAMA));
  if (!username && !nama) throw new Error('Username atau nama karyawan wajib diisi.');

  let rowNumber = 0;
  table.rows.some(function(row, idx) {
    const rowUsername = firstNonEmpty_(row['USERNAME'], row['Username'], row['username'], row['USER_NAME'], row['User ID'], row['USER_ID']);
    const rowNama = firstNonEmpty_(row['NAMA'], row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['NAMA LENGKAP'], row['name']);
    if ((username && normKey_(rowUsername) === normKey_(username)) || (!username && nama && normKey_(rowNama) === normKey_(nama))) {
      rowNumber = idx + 2;
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  });
  if (!rowNumber) throw new Error('Data karyawan tidak ditemukan untuk update: ' + (username || nama));

  const patchByAlias = [
    { aliases: ['NAMA','Nama','Nama Lengkap','NAMA LENGKAP','name'], value: nama },
    { aliases: ['USERNAME','Username','username','USER_NAME','User ID','USER_ID'], value: username },
    { aliases: ['LEVEL','Level','level','JABATAN','Jabatan'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.level, payload.LEVEL, payload.jabatan) },
    { aliases: ['OUTLET_UTAMA','Outlet Utama','OUTLET UTAMA','Outlet','OUTLET'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.outletUtama, payload.outlet, payload.OUTLET_UTAMA) },
    { aliases: ['OUTLET_AKSES','Outlet Akses','Akses Outlet','AKSES_OUTLET','OUTLET_ACCESS'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.outletAkses, payload.aksesOutlet, payload.OUTLET_AKSES) },
    { aliases: ['STATUS','Status','status','AKTIF'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.status, payload.STATUS) },
    { aliases: ['EMAIL','Email','email'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.email, payload.EMAIL) },
    { aliases: ['TELEPON','Telepon','telepon','NO_HP','No HP','HP'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.telepon, payload.noHp, payload.HP) }
  ];
  let changed = 0;
  patchByAlias.forEach(function(item) {
    if (item.value === undefined || item.value === null || String(item.value).trim() === '') return;
    const col = findHeaderColV157_(headers, item.aliases);
    if (col > 0) {
      sh.getRange(rowNumber, col).setValue(item.value);
      changed++;
    }
  });
  if (!changed) throw new Error('Tidak ada kolom USER yang cocok untuk diperbarui. Cek header sheet USER.');
  try {
    const updatedAtCol = findHeaderColV157_(headers, ['UPDATED_AT','Updated At','UPDATED AT','LAST_UPDATE','Last Update']);
    if (updatedAtCol > 0) sh.getRange(rowNumber, updatedAtCol).setValue(new Date());
    const updatedByCol = findHeaderColV157_(headers, ['UPDATED_BY','Updated By']);
    if (updatedByCol > 0) sh.getRange(rowNumber, updatedByCol).setValue(currentUser.username || currentUser.nama || 'APJ');
  } catch (err) {}
  clearHrMasterCache_();
  const data = getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload);
  data.pesan = 'Data karyawan berhasil diperbarui di APJ_CORE_USER.USER.';
  data.updated = true;
  data.changedColumns = changed;
  return data;
}

function saveHrShiftV177(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  if (!isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(currentUser)) throw new Error('Akses ditolak. Hanya OWNER/SUPERADMIN/HR/SUPERVISOR yang bisa mengatur shift.');
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT);
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Sheet ID_SHIFT tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.');
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  if (!headers.length) throw new Error('Header ID_SHIFT belum tersedia.');

  const nama = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.namaShift, payload.NAMA_SHIFT, payload.shift, payload.SHIFT, payload.nama, payload.NAMA));
  const outlet = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.outlet, payload.OUTLET, payload.Outlet));
  if (!nama) throw new Error('Nama shift wajib diisi.');
  if (!outlet) throw new Error('Outlet shift wajib dipilih.');

  const table = readTable_(sh);
  const targetNama = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.targetNamaShift, payload.targetNama, nama));
  const targetKode = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.targetKodeShift, payload.targetKode, payload.kodeShift, payload.KODE_SHIFT));
  let rowNumber = 0;
  table.rows.some(function(row, idx) {
    const rowKode = firstNonEmpty_(row['KODE_SHIFT'], row['Kode Shift'], row['ID_SHIFT'], row['ID Shift'], row['Kode'], row['KODE']);
    const rowNama = firstNonEmpty_(row['NAMA_SHIFT'], row['Nama Shift'], row['Nama Shift'], row['SHIFT'], row['Shift'], row['Nama'], row['NAMA']);
    const rowOutlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['OUTLET'], row['Outlet'], row['outlet']);
    const sameKode = targetKode && normKey_(rowKode) === normKey_(targetKode);
    const sameNamaOutlet = targetNama && normKey_(rowNama) === normKey_(targetNama) && (!outlet || normKey_(rowOutlet) === normKey_(outlet));
    const sameNamaOnly = targetNama && normKey_(rowNama) === normKey_(targetNama) && !rowOutlet;
    if (sameKode || sameNamaOutlet || sameNamaOnly) { rowNumber = idx + 2; return true; }
    return false;
  });

  const patch = [
    { aliases: ['NAMA_SHIFT','Nama Shift','Nama Shift','SHIFT','Shift','Nama','NAMA'], value: nama },
    { aliases: ['OUTLET','Outlet','outlet'], value: outlet },
    { aliases: ['JAM_MASUK','Jam Masuk','JAM MASUK','MASUK','Masuk'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.jamMasuk, payload.JAM_MASUK, payload.masuk) },
    { aliases: ['JAM_PULANG','Jam Pulang','JAM PULANG','JAM_KELUAR','Jam Keluar','PULANG','Pulang'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.jamPulang, payload.JAM_PULANG, payload.pulang) },
    { aliases: ['TOLERANSI_KETERLAMBATAN','Toleransi Keterlambatan','Toleransi','TOLERANSI','TOLERANSI_MENIT','Toleransi Menit'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.toleransiKeterlambatan, payload.toleransi, payload.TOLERANSI, '0 Menit') },
    { aliases: ['ISTIRAHAT','Istirahat'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.istirahat, payload.ISTIRAHAT, '0 Jam') },
    { aliases: ['HITUNG_LEMBUR_AWAL','Hitung Lembur Awal','Hitung Lembur Awal','LEMBUR_AWAL','Lembur Awal'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.hitungLemburAwal, payload.lemburAwal, payload.HITUNG_LEMBUR_AWAL, 'TIDAK') },
    { aliases: ['HITUNG_LEMBUR_AKHIR','Hitung Lembur Akhir','Hitung Lembur Akhir','LEMBUR_AKHIR','Lembur Akhir'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.hitungLemburAkhir, payload.lemburAkhir, payload.HITUNG_LEMBUR_AKHIR, 'TIDAK') },
    { aliases: ['MINIMAL_LEMBUR_MENIT','Minimal Lembur Menit','Minimal Lembur Menit','MINIMAL_LEMBUR','Minimal Lembur'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.minimalLemburMenit, payload.MINIMAL_LEMBUR_MENIT, '60 Menit') },
    { aliases: ['PEMBULATAN_LEMBUR_MENIT','Pembulatan Lembur Menit','Pembulatan Lembur Menit','PEMBULATAN_LEMBUR','Pembulatan Lembur'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.pembulatanLemburMenit, payload.PEMBULATAN_LEMBUR_MENIT, '60 Menit') },
    { aliases: ['METODE_PEMBULATAN_LEMBUR','Metode Pembulatan Lembur','Metode Pembulatan Lembur','METODE_PEMBULATAN','Metode Pembulatan'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.metodePembulatanLembur, payload.METODE_PEMBULATAN_LEMBUR, 'TURUN') },
    { aliases: ['STATUS','Status','AKTIF','Aktif'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.status, payload.STATUS, 'AKTIF') },
    { aliases: ['CATATAN','Catatan','NOTE','Note'], value: firstNonEmpty_(payload.catatan, payload.CATATAN) }
  ];
  const values = rowNumber ? null : new Array(headers.length).fill('');
  let changed = 0;
  patch.forEach(function(item) {
    if (item.value === undefined || item.value === null) return;
    const col = findHeaderColV157_(headers, item.aliases);
    if (col > 0) {
      if (rowNumber) sh.getRange(rowNumber, col).setValue(item.value);
      else values[col - 1] = item.value;
      changed++;
    }
  });
  if (!changed) throw new Error('Tidak ada kolom ID_SHIFT yang cocok untuk disimpan. Cek header sheet ID_SHIFT.');
  if (!rowNumber) {
    rowNumber = sh.getLastRow() + 1;
    sh.getRange(rowNumber, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([values]);
  }
  try {
    const updatedAtCol = findHeaderColV157_(headers, ['UPDATED_AT','Updated At','UPDATED AT','LAST_UPDATE','Last Update']);
    if (updatedAtCol > 0) sh.getRange(rowNumber, updatedAtCol).setValue(new Date());
    const updatedByCol = findHeaderColV157_(headers, ['UPDATED_BY','Updated By']);
    if (updatedByCol > 0) sh.getRange(rowNumber, updatedByCol).setValue(currentUser.username || currentUser.nama || 'APJ');
  } catch (err) {}
  clearHrMasterCache_();
  const data = getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload);
  data.pesan = 'Shift kerja berhasil disimpan ke APJ_CORE_USER.ID_SHIFT.';
  data.updated = true;
  data.rowNumber = rowNumber;
  return data;
}

  return saveHrJadwalV162(payload || {});

function saveHrJadwalV166(payload) { return saveHrJadwalV167(payload || {}); }

function cleanupHrJadwalPreviousPeriodsV167_(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const ss = coreSS_();
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL);
  if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() < 2) return { deleted: 0 };
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  if (!isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(currentUser)) throw new Error('Akses ditolak. Hanya OWNER/SUPERADMIN/HR/SUPERVISOR yang bisa mengatur jadwal.');
  const users = getHrKaryawanUsersV157_();
  const keyUsername = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.usernameKaryawan, payload.usernameUser, payload.username, payload.USERNAME));
  const keyNama = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.namaKaryawan, payload.namaUser, payload.nama, payload.NAMA));
  const user = users.find(function(u) {
    return (keyUsername && normKey_(u.username) === normKey_(keyUsername)) ||
           (!keyUsername && keyNama && normKey_(u.nama) === normKey_(keyNama));
  }) || {};
  const username = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(keyUsername, user.username));
  const nama = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(keyNama, user.nama));
  const bulan = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.bulan, payload.Bulan, payload.BULAN, monthNameId_(new Date())));
  const tahun = String(firstNonEmpty_(payload.tahun, payload.Tahun, payload.TAHUN, new Date().getFullYear()) || '').trim();
  if (!username && !nama) return { deleted: 0 };
  if (!bulan || !tahun) return { deleted: 0 };
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  const rowsToDelete = [];
  table.rows.forEach(function(row, idx) {
    const rowUsername = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['USERNAME'], row['USER_ID'], row['User ID']);
    const rowNama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama']);
    const rowBulan = firstNonEmpty_(row['Bulan'], row['BULAN']);
    const rowTahun = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Tahun'], row['TAHUN']) || '').trim();
    const sameUser = username ? normKey_(rowUsername) === normKey_(username) : normKey_(rowNama) === normKey_(nama);
    if (sameUser && !(normKey_(rowBulan) === normKey_(bulan) && rowTahun === tahun)) rowsToDelete.push(idx + 2);
  });
  rowsToDelete.sort(function(a, b) { return b - a; }).forEach(function(rowNumber) { sh.deleteRow(rowNumber); });
  if (rowsToDelete.length) clearHrMasterCache_();
  return { deleted: rowsToDelete.length };
}

function saveHrJadwalV165(payload) { return saveHrJadwalV162(payload || {}); }
function saveHrJadwalV164(payload) { return saveHrJadwalV162(payload || {}); }
function saveHrJadwalV163(payload) { return saveHrJadwalV162(payload || {}); }

function saveHrJadwalV161(payload) {
  return saveHrJadwalV162(payload || {});
}

function saveHrJadwalV162(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const segments = Array.isArray(payload.segments) ? payload.segments : [];
  if (!segments.length) return saveHrJadwalV160(payload || {});

  const saved = [];
  segments.forEach(function(seg, idx) {
    seg = seg || {};
    const rawDays = Array.isArray(seg.days) ? seg.days : (Array.isArray(seg.tanggal) ? seg.tanggal : []);
    let days = rawDays.map(function(d) { return Number(d); }).filter(function(n) { return n >= 1 && n <= 31; });
    if (!days.length) {
      const start = Number(firstNonEmpty_(seg.startDay, seg.start, seg.dari, seg.tanggalAwal));
      const end = Number(firstNonEmpty_(seg.endDay, seg.end, seg.sampai, seg.tanggalAkhir));
      if (start && end && end >= start) {
        for (let d = start; d <= end; d++) days.push(d);
      }
    }
    days = Array.from(new Set(days)).sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; });
    if (!days.length) throw new Error('Baris jadwal langsung #' + (idx + 1) + ' belum memiliki tanggal valid.');
    const shift = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(seg.shift, seg.namaShift, seg.kodeShift, payload.shift));
    const outlet = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(seg.outlet, seg.OUTLET, payload.outlet));
    if (!outlet) throw new Error('Baris jadwal langsung #' + (idx + 1) + ' belum memilih outlet.');
    if (!shift) throw new Error('Baris jadwal langsung #' + (idx + 1) + ' belum memilih shift/LIBUR/Kosongkan.');

    const sub = Object.assign({}, payload, {
      outlet: outlet,
      shift: shift,
      kodeShift: normText_(firstNonEmpty_(seg.kodeShift, seg.shift, payload.kodeShift)),
      tanggal: days,
      days: days
    });
    delete sub.segments;
    delete sub.multiSegments;
    delete sub.jadwalMap;
    delete sub.workDays;
    delete sub.liburDays;
    const res = saveHrJadwalV158(sub);
    if (res && res.savedJadwal) saved.push(res.savedJadwal);
  });

  clearHrMasterCache_();
  const data = getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload);
  data.updated = true;
  data.savedSegments = saved;
  data.pesan = 'Jadwal langsung multi shift/outlet berhasil disimpan ke APJ_CORE_USER.ID_JADWAL.';
  return data;
}

function saveHrJadwalV159(payload) {
  return saveHrJadwalV158(payload || {});
}

function saveHrJadwalV158(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  if (!isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(currentUser)) throw new Error('Akses ditolak. Hanya OWNER/SUPERADMIN/HR/SUPERVISOR yang bisa mengatur jadwal.');

  const ss = coreSS_();
  let sh = ss.getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL);
  if (!sh) sh = ss.insertSheet(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL);
  let headers = ensureHrJadwalHeadersV158_(sh);

  const users = getHrKaryawanUsersV157_();
  const keyUsername = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.usernameKaryawan, payload.usernameUser, payload.username, payload.USERNAME));
  const keyNama = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.namaKaryawan, payload.namaUser, payload.nama, payload.NAMA));
  const user = users.find(function(u) {
    return (keyUsername && normKey_(u.username) === normKey_(keyUsername)) ||
           (!keyUsername && keyNama && normKey_(u.nama) === normKey_(keyNama));
  }) || {};

  const nama = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.namaKaryawan, payload.nama, user.nama));
  const username = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.usernameKaryawan, payload.username, user.username));
  const outlet = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.outlet, payload.OUTLET, user.outlet));
  const bulan = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.bulan, payload.Bulan, payload.BULAN, monthNameId_(new Date())));
  const tahun = String(firstNonEmpty_(payload.tahun, payload.Tahun, payload.TAHUN, new Date().getFullYear()) || '').trim();
  const status = normalizeStatusV157_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.status, payload.STATUS, 'AKTIF'));
  const catatan = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.catatan, payload.CATATAN, payload.note, payload.NOTE));
  let shiftName = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.shift, payload.namaShift, payload.NAMA_SHIFT, payload.kodeShift, payload.KODE_SHIFT));
  const jadwalMap = parseJadwalMapV160_(payload);
  const hasJadwalMap = Object.keys(jadwalMap).length > 0;
  const clearMode = ['kosongkan','hapusjadwal','hapus','clear','blank'].indexOf(normKey_(shiftName)) >= 0;
  const days = hasJadwalMap ? Object.keys(jadwalMap).map(function(d) { return Number(d); }).filter(function(n) { return n >= 1 && n <= 31; }).sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; }) : parseJadwalDaysV158_(payload);

  if (!nama && !username) throw new Error('Nama karyawan wajib dipilih dari dropdown.');
  if (!outlet) throw new Error('Outlet jadwal wajib dipilih.');
  if (!bulan || !tahun) throw new Error('Bulan dan tahun jadwal wajib diisi.');
  if (!days.length) throw new Error('Pilih minimal satu tanggal jadwal.');
  if (!shiftName && !clearMode && !hasJadwalMap) throw new Error('Shift kerja wajib dipilih. Pilih LIBUR untuk hari libur atau Kosongkan untuk menghapus jadwal tanggal tertentu.');
  if (clearMode) shiftName = '';
  else if (normKey_(shiftName) === 'libur') shiftName = 'LIBUR';

  headers = ensureHrJadwalHeadersV158_(sh);
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  let rowNumber = 0;
  table.rows.some(function(row, idx) {
    const rowUsername = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['USERNAME'], row['USER_ID'], row['User ID']);
    const rowNama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama']);
    const rowOutlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET'], row['OUTLET_UTAMA'], row['Outlet Utama']);
    const rowBulan = firstNonEmpty_(row['Bulan'], row['BULAN']);
    const rowTahun = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Tahun'], row['TAHUN']) || '').trim();
    const sameUser = username ? normKey_(rowUsername) === normKey_(username) : normKey_(rowNama) === normKey_(nama);
    if (sameUser && normKey_(rowOutlet) === normKey_(outlet) && normKey_(rowBulan) === normKey_(bulan) && rowTahun === tahun) {
      rowNumber = idx + 2;
      return true;
    }
    return false;
  });

  if (!rowNumber) {
    rowNumber = Math.max(sh.getLastRow() + 1, 2);
    sh.getRange(rowNumber, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).clearContent();
  }

  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['Nama Lengkap','Nama Karyawan','NAMA','Nama'], nama || username);
  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['Username','USERNAME','USER_ID','User ID'], username);
  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['Outlet','OUTLET','OUTLET_UTAMA','Outlet Utama'], outlet);
  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['Bulan','BULAN'], bulan);
  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['Tahun','TAHUN'], tahun);
  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['Status','STATUS'], status);
  if (catatan) setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['Catatan','CATATAN','Note','NOTE'], catatan);
  days.forEach(function(day) {
    const cellValue = hasJadwalMap ? normalizeJadwalCellV160_(jadwalMap[day]) : shiftName;
    setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, [String(day), String(day).padStart(2, '0')], cellValue);
  });
  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['UPDATED_AT','Updated At','UPDATED AT','LAST_UPDATE'], new Date());
  setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, ['UPDATED_BY','Updated By','UPDATED BY'], currentUser.username || currentUser.nama || 'APJ');

  clearHrMasterCache_();
  const data = getHrKaryawanDataV157(payload);
  data.updated = true;
  data.savedJadwal = { nama: nama || username, username: username, outlet: outlet, bulan: bulan, tahun: tahun, shift: clearMode ? 'KOSONGKAN' : shiftName, tanggal: days, rowNumber: rowNumber };
  data.pesan = clearMode ? 'Tanggal jadwal berhasil dikosongkan di APJ_CORE_USER.ID_JADWAL.' : 'Jadwal karyawan berhasil disimpan ke APJ_CORE_USER.ID_JADWAL.';
  return data;
}

function ensureHrJadwalHeadersV158_(sh) {
  const base = ['Nama Lengkap','Username','Outlet','Bulan','Tahun'];
  const days = Array.from({ length: 31 }, function(_, i) { return String(i + 1); });
  const meta = ['Status','Catatan','UPDATED_AT','UPDATED_BY'];
  const target = base.concat(days).concat(meta);
  if (sh.getLastRow() < 1 || sh.getLastColumn() < 1) {
    sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, target.length).setValues([target]);
    sh.setFrozenRows(1);
    return target;
  }
  let headers = getHeaders_(sh).map(function(h) { return String(h || '').trim(); });
  if (!headers.some(function(h) { return h; })) {
    sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, target.length).setValues([target]);
    sh.setFrozenRows(1);
    return target;
  }
  const missing = [];
  function hasAny(aliases) {
    return aliases.some(function(a) { return headers.some(function(h) { return normKey_(h) === normKey_(a); }); });
  }
  [
    ['Nama Lengkap','Nama Karyawan','NAMA','Nama'],
    ['Username','USERNAME','USER_ID','User ID'],
    ['Outlet','OUTLET','OUTLET_UTAMA','Outlet Utama'],
    ['Bulan','BULAN'],
    ['Tahun','TAHUN']
  ].forEach(function(group) { if (!hasAny(group)) missing.push(group[0]); });
  days.forEach(function(day) { if (!hasAny([day, day.padStart(2, '0')])) missing.push(day); });
  [
    ['Status','STATUS'],
    ['Catatan','CATATAN','Note','NOTE'],
    ['UPDATED_AT','Updated At','UPDATED AT','LAST_UPDATE'],
    ['UPDATED_BY','Updated By','UPDATED BY']
  ].forEach(function(group) { if (!hasAny(group)) missing.push(group[0]); });
  if (missing.length) {
    sh.getRange(1, headers.length + 1, 1, missing.length).setValues([missing]);
    headers = headers.concat(missing);
  }
  try { sh.setFrozenRows(1); } catch (err) {}
  return headers;
}

function setHrJadwalCellV158_(sh, headers, rowNumber, aliases, value) {
  const col = findHeaderColV157_(headers, aliases);
  if (col > 0) sh.getRange(rowNumber, col).setValue(value);
}

function parseJadwalMapV160_(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  let raw = payload.jadwalMap || payload.mapJadwal || payload.dayMap || payload.daysMap;
  if (!raw) return {};
  if (typeof raw === 'string') {
    try { raw = JSON.parse(raw); } catch (err) { raw = {}; }
  }
  const out = {};
  if (Array.isArray(raw)) {
    raw.forEach(function(item) {
      if (!item) return;
      const day = Number(firstNonEmpty_(item.day, item.tanggal, item.TANGGAL));
      if (day >= 1 && day <= 31) out[String(day)] = normalizeJadwalCellV160_(firstNonEmpty_(item.value, item.shift, item.status, item.jadwal));
    });
    return out;
  }
  Object.keys(raw || {}).forEach(function(key) {
    const day = Number(key);
    if (day >= 1 && day <= 31) out[String(day)] = normalizeJadwalCellV160_(raw[key]);
  });
  return out;
}

function normalizeJadwalCellV160_(value) {
  const v = normText_(value);
  const k = normKey_(v);
  if (!v || ['kosongkan','hapusjadwal','hapus','clear','blank','empty','off'].indexOf(k) >= 0) return '';
  if (k === 'libur') return 'LIBUR';
  if (k === 'alpa') return 'ALPA';
  if (k === 'izin') return 'IZIN';
  return v;
}

function parseJadwalDaysV158_(payload) {
  let raw = payload.tanggal;
  if (raw === undefined || raw === null || raw === '') raw = payload.days;
  if (raw === undefined || raw === null || raw === '') raw = payload.hari;
  if (raw === undefined || raw === null || raw === '') raw = payload.TANGGAL;
  const arr = Array.isArray(raw) ? raw : String(raw || '').split(/[^0-9]+/);
  const seen = {};
  return arr.map(function(x) { return Number(x); })
    .filter(function(n) { return n >= 1 && n <= 31 && !seen[n] && (seen[n] = true); })
    .sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; });
}

function getHrKaryawanUsersV157_() {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.USER);
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Sheet USER tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.');
  const table = readTableCached_('CORE', sh);
  return table.rows.map(function(row, idx) {
    const outlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['OUTLET_UTAMA'], row['Outlet Utama'], row['OUTLET UTAMA'], row['OUTLET'], row['Outlet']);
    const akses = firstNonEmpty_(row['OUTLET_AKSES'], row['Outlet Akses'], row['Akses Outlet'], row['AKSES_OUTLET'], row['OUTLET_ACCESS'], outlet);
    const status = firstNonEmpty_(row['STATUS'], row['Status'], row['status'], row['AKTIF'], 'AKTIF');
    return {
      rowNumber: idx + 2,
      userId: firstNonEmpty_(row['USER_ID'], row['User ID'], row['ID User'], row['ID'], row['KODE_USER']),
      username: firstNonEmpty_(row['USERNAME'], row['Username'], row['username'], row['USER_NAME'], row['User ID'], row['USER_ID']),
      nama: firstNonEmpty_(row['NAMA'], row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['NAMA LENGKAP'], row['name']),
      level: firstNonEmpty_(row['LEVEL'], row['Level'], row['level'], row['JABATAN'], row['Jabatan']) || '-',
      outlet: outlet || '-',
      outletUtama: outlet || '-',
      outletAkses: akses || outlet || '',
      status: normalizeStatusV157_(status),
      email: firstNonEmpty_(row['EMAIL'], row['Email'], row['email']),
      telepon: firstNonEmpty_(row['TELEPON'], row['Telepon'], row['telepon'], row['NO_HP'], row['No HP'], row['HP']),
      raw: serializeRawRowV157_(row)
    };
  }).filter(function(u) { return u.nama || u.username; });
}

function getHrKaryawanOutletsV157_() {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.OUTLET);
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Sheet OUTLET tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.');
  const table = readTableCached_('CORE', sh);
  return table.rows.map(function(row, idx) {
    const status = firstNonEmpty_(row['STATUS'], row['Status'], row['status'], 'AKTIF');
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['NAMA_OUTLET'], row['Nama Outlet'], row['OUTLET'], row['Outlet'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama']);
    return {
      rowNumber: idx + 2,
      outletId: firstNonEmpty_(row['OUTLET_ID'], row['Outlet ID'], row['ID_OUTLET'], row['ID']),
      kodeOutlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['KODE_OUTLET'], row['Kode Outlet'], row['Kode'], row['KODE']),
      namaOutlet: nama,
      outlet: nama,
      status: normalizeStatusV157_(status),
      latitude: number_(firstNonEmpty_(row['LATITUDE'], row['Latitude'], row['LAT'])),
      longitude: number_(firstNonEmpty_(row['LONGTITUDE'], row['LONGITUDE'], row['Longitude'], row['LON'], row['LNG'])),
      radius: number_(firstNonEmpty_(row['RADIUS_METER'], row['Radius Meter'], row['Radius'])) || 0,
      raw: serializeRawRowV157_(row)
    };
  }).filter(function(o) { return o.namaOutlet && normKey_(o.status) === 'aktif'; });
}

function getHrKaryawanShiftsV157_() {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT);
  if (!sh) return [];
  const table = readTableCached_('CORE', sh);
  return table.rows.map(function(row, idx) {
    const namaShift = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Shift'], row['NAMA_SHIFT'], row['Shift'], row['SHIFT'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama']);
    const kodeShift = firstNonEmpty_(row['KODE_SHIFT'], row['Kode Shift'], row['ID_SHIFT'], row['ID Shift'], row['Kode'], row['KODE'], namaShift);
    const jamMasuk = normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Masuk'], row['JAM_MASUK'], row['Masuk'], row['MASUK']));
    const jamPulang = normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Pulang'], row['JAM_PULANG'], row['Pulang'], row['PULANG']));
    return {
      rowNumber: idx + 2,
      kodeShift: kodeShift,
      kode: kodeShift,
      namaShift: namaShift,
      nama: namaShift,
      outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET'], row['OUTLET_UTAMA'], row['Area']),
      jamMasuk: jamMasuk,
      jamPulang: jamPulang,
      masuk: jamMasuk,
      pulang: jamPulang,
      toleransi: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Toleransi Keterlambatan'], row['Tolerasi Keterlambatan'], row['Toleransi'], row['TOLERANSI'], row['Telat'])),
      toleransiMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Toleransi Keterlambatan'], row['Tolerasi Keterlambatan'], row['Toleransi'], row['TOLERANSI'], row['Telat'])),
      istirahatMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Istirahat'], row['Break'])),
      lembur: firstNonEmpty_(row['Lembur'], row['LEMBUR'], row['Mulai Lembur'], row['MULAI_LEMBUR'], row['Hitung Lembur Awal']),
      status: normalizeStatusV157_(firstNonEmpty_(row['STATUS'], row['Status'], row['status'], 'AKTIF')),
      raw: serializeRawRowV157_(row)
    };
  }).filter(function(s) { return s.namaShift || s.kodeShift; });
}

function getHrKaryawanJadwalV157_(shifts) {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL);
  if (!sh) return [];
  const table = readTableCached_('CORE', sh);
  const shiftMap = {};
  (shifts || []).forEach(function(s) {
    [s.kodeShift, s.namaShift, s.kode, s.nama].forEach(function(k) { if (k) shiftMap[normKey_(k)] = s; });
  });
  const out = [];
  table.rows.forEach(function(row, idx) {
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama'], row['User'], row['USER']);
    const username = firstNonEmpty_(row['USERNAME'], row['Username'], row['USER_ID'], row['User ID']);
    const outlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET'], row['OUTLET_UTAMA'], row['Outlet Utama']);
    const bulan = firstNonEmpty_(row['Bulan'], row['BULAN']);
    const tahun = firstNonEmpty_(row['Tahun'], row['TAHUN']);
    let hasDayValue = false;
    for (let d = 1; d <= 31; d++) {
      const shiftName = firstNonEmpty_(row[String(d)], row[String(d).padStart(2, '0')]);
      if (!shiftName) continue;
      hasDayValue = true;
      const shift = shiftMap[normKey_(shiftName)] || {};
      const jam = shift.jamMasuk || shift.jamPulang ? [shift.jamMasuk || '', shift.jamPulang || ''].filter(Boolean).join(' - ') : '';
      out.push({
        rowNumber: idx + 2,
        nama: nama,
        username: username,
        outlet: outlet || shift.outlet || '-',
        hari: [String(d), bulan, tahun].filter(Boolean).join(' '),
        tanggal: [String(d), bulan, tahun].filter(Boolean).join(' '),
        shift: shiftName,
        jam: jam,
        status: normalizeStatusV157_(firstNonEmpty_(row['STATUS'], row['Status'], row['status'], 'AKTIF')),
        catatan: firstNonEmpty_(row['Catatan'], row['CATATAN'], row['Note'], row['NOTE']) || '-',
        raw: serializeRawRowV157_(row)
      });
    }
    if (!hasDayValue) {
      const shiftName = firstNonEmpty_(row['Shift'], row['SHIFT'], row['Nama Shift'], row['NAMA_SHIFT'], row['Kode Shift'], row['KODE_SHIFT']);
      const shift = shiftMap[normKey_(shiftName)] || {};
      const jam = firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam'], row['JAM'], row['Jam Kerja'], row['JAM_KERJA']) || (shift.jamMasuk || shift.jamPulang ? [shift.jamMasuk || '', shift.jamPulang || ''].filter(Boolean).join(' - ') : '');
      if (nama || username || shiftName || outlet) {
        out.push({
          rowNumber: idx + 2,
          nama: nama,
          username: username,
          outlet: outlet || shift.outlet || '-',
          hari: firstNonEmpty_(row['Hari'], row['HARI'], row['Tanggal'], row['TANGGAL'], row['Day']) || '-',
          shift: shiftName || '-',
          jam: jam || '-',
          status: normalizeStatusV157_(firstNonEmpty_(row['STATUS'], row['Status'], row['status'], 'AKTIF')),
          catatan: firstNonEmpty_(row['Catatan'], row['CATATAN'], row['Note'], row['NOTE']) || '-',
          raw: serializeRawRowV157_(row)
        });
      }
    }
  });
  return out;
}


function exportHrJadwalPdfV167(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  if (!isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(currentUser)) throw new Error('Akses ditolak. Hanya OWNER/SUPERADMIN/HR/SUPERVISOR yang bisa export jadwal.');
  const bulan = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.bulan, payload.Bulan, payload.BULAN, monthNameId_(new Date())));
  const tahun = String(firstNonEmpty_(payload.tahun, payload.Tahun, payload.TAHUN, new Date().getFullYear()) || '').trim();
  if (!bulan || !tahun) throw new Error('Bulan dan tahun wajib diisi untuk export PDF jadwal.');
  const shifts = getHrKaryawanShiftsV157_();
  const jadwal = getHrKaryawanJadwalV157_(shifts).filter(function(r) {
    const p = parseHrJadwalDateV167_(r.hari || r.tanggal);
    return normKey_(p.bulan) === normKey_(bulan) && String(p.tahun || '') === tahun;
  });
  const groups = groupHrJadwalForPdfV167_(jadwal, bulan, tahun);
  const html = buildHrJadwalPdfHtmlV167_(groups, bulan, tahun, currentUser);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_('Jadwal & Shift - ' + bulan + ' ' + tahun + '.pdf');
  const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.JADWAL_EXPORT_FOLDER_ID);
  deleteExistingFileByNameV142_(folder, fileName);
  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(html, 'text/html', fileName.replace(/\.pdf$/i, '.html')).getAs(MimeType.PDF).setName(fileName);
  const file = folder.createFile(blob);
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    pesan: 'PDF jadwal berhasil dibuat di Drive.',
    fileId: file.getId(),
    fileName: file.getName(),
    url: file.getUrl(),
    folderId: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.JADWAL_EXPORT_FOLDER_ID,
    bulan: bulan,
    tahun: tahun,
    totalPeriode: groups.length,
    totalTanggal: jadwal.length
  };
}

function parseHrJadwalDateV167_(text) {
  const str = String(text || '').trim();
  const m = str.match(/(\d{1,2})\s+([^\s]+)\s+(\d{4})/);
  if (!m) return { day: 0, bulan: '', tahun: '' };
  return { day: Number(m[1]), bulan: m[2], tahun: m[3] };
}

function groupHrJadwalForPdfV167_(rows, bulan, tahun) {
  const map = {};
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const p = parseHrJadwalDateV167_(r.hari || r.tanggal);
    if (!p.day) return;
    const key = [r.username || r.nama, r.outlet, bulan, tahun].map(function(x) { return String(x || '').toLowerCase(); }).join('|');
    if (!map[key]) map[key] = { nama: r.nama || '-', username: r.username || '', outlet: r.outlet || '-', bulan: bulan, tahun: tahun, kerja: [], libur: [], alpa: [], izin: [], shiftDays: {} };
    const g = map[key];
    const shift = String(r.shift || '').trim() || '-';
    const up = shift.toUpperCase();
    if (up === 'LIBUR') g.libur.push(p.day);
    else if (up === 'ALPA') g.alpa.push(p.day);
    else if (up === 'IZIN') g.izin.push(p.day);
    else g.kerja.push(p.day);
    if (!g.shiftDays[shift]) g.shiftDays[shift] = [];
    g.shiftDays[shift].push(p.day);
  });
  return Object.keys(map).map(function(k) {
    const g = map[k];
    ['kerja','libur','alpa','izin'].forEach(function(f) { g[f].sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; }); });
    Object.keys(g.shiftDays).forEach(function(shift) { g.shiftDays[shift].sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; }); });
    return g;
  }).sort(function(a, b) { return String(a.outlet || '').localeCompare(String(b.outlet || '')) || String(a.nama || '').localeCompare(String(b.nama || '')); });
}

function formatDaysV167_(days) {
  days = (days || []).map(Number).filter(Boolean).sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; });
  if (!days.length) return '-';
  const ranges = [];
  let start = days[0], prev = days[0];
  for (let i = 1; i < days.length; i++) {
    if (days[i] === prev + 1) { prev = days[i]; continue; }
    ranges.push(start === prev ? String(start) : start + '-' + prev);
    start = prev = days[i];
  }
  ranges.push(start === prev ? String(start) : start + '-' + prev);
  return ranges.join(', ');
}

function renderShiftLinesV167_(g) {
  const keys = Object.keys(g.shiftDays || {}).sort(function(a, b) { return (g.shiftDays[b] || []).length - (g.shiftDays[a] || []).length; });
  if (!keys.length) return '-';
  return keys.map(function(k) {
    return '<div><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(k) + '</b>: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(formatDaysV167_(g.shiftDays[k] || [])) + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function buildHrJadwalPdfHtmlV167_(groups, bulan, tahun, currentUser) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd MMMM yyyy HH:mm');
  const rows = (groups || []).map(function(g, idx) {
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="c">' + (idx + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(g.nama || '-') + '</b></td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(g.outlet || '-') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="c">' + (g.kerja || []).length + '</td>' +
      '<td class="c">' + (g.libur || []).length + '</td>' +
      '<td class="c danger">' + (g.alpa || []).length + '</td>' +
      '<td class="c warn">' + (g.izin || []).length + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + renderShiftLinesV167_(g) + '</td>' +
    '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="8" class="empty">Belum ada jadwal untuk periode ini.</td></tr>';
  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="UTF-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 landscape;margin:10mm}body{font-family:Arial,sans-serif;color:#111827;margin:0}h1{font-size:22px;margin:0 0 4px}h2{font-size:14px;margin:0;color:#475569}.head{display:flex;justify-content:space-between;gap:20px;border-bottom:2px solid #111827;padding-bottom:10px;margin-bottom:12px}.brand{font-size:11px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.14em;color:#0f172a}.meta{text-align:right;font-size:10px;color:#475569;line-height:1.5}.summary{display:flex;gap:8px;margin:10px 0 12px}.card{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:10px;padding:8px 10px;min-width:90px}.card small{display:block;font-size:9px;color:#64748b;text-transform:uppercase;font-weight:800}.card b{font-size:18px}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed}th{background:#0f172a;color:#fff;font-size:9px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.05em;padding:7px 6px;text-align:left}td{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;padding:6px;font-size:10px;vertical-align:top;line-height:1.35}tr:nth-child(even) td{background:#f8fafc}.c{text-align:center}.danger{color:#b91c1c;font-weight:800}.warn{color:#a16207;font-weight:800}.empty{text-align:center;color:#64748b;padding:18px}.foot{margin-top:12px;font-size:9px;color:#64748b;display:flex;justify-content:space-between}' +
    '</style></head><body>' +
    '<div class="head"><div><div class="brand">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><h1>Jadwal & Shift Karyawan</h1><h2>Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(bulan + ' ' + tahun) + '</h2></div><div class="meta"><b>Dibuat</b><br>' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '<br>Oleh: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(currentUser.nama || currentUser.username || 'APJ') + '</div></div>' +
    '<div class="summary"><div class="card"><small>Periode</small><b>' + groups.length + '</b></div><div class="card"><small>Folder</small><b>Drive</b></div></div>' +
    '<table><thead><tr><th style="width:32px">No</th><th style="width:150px">Nama</th><th style="width:90px">Outlet</th><th style="width:48px">Kerja</th><th style="width:48px">Libur</th><th style="width:48px">Alpa</th><th style="width:48px">Izin</th><th>Rincian Shift / Tanggal</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rows + '</tbody></table>' +
    '<div class="foot"><span>Dokumen dibuat otomatis oleh APJ HR.</span><span>Jadwal & Shift - ' + htmlEscapeV142_(bulan + ' ' + tahun) + '</span></div>' +
    '</body></html>';
}

function isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(user) {
  if (isBypassUser_(user)) return true;
  const level = String(user && user.level || '').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/\s+/g, '');
  return ['OWNER','SUPERADMIN','SUPERVISOR','HR','HUMANRESOURCE','HUMANRESOURCES'].indexOf(level) >= 0;
}

function findHeaderColV157_(headers, aliases) {
  const keys = (headers || []).map(function(h) { return normKey_(h); });
  for (let i = 0; i < aliases.length; i++) {
    const idx = keys.indexOf(normKey_(aliases[i]));
    if (idx >= 0) return idx + 1;
  }
  return 0;
}

function normalizeStatusV157_(status) {
  const s = String(status || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!s) return 'AKTIF';
  if (['ACTIVE','AKTIF','YA','Y','TRUE','1'].indexOf(s) >= 0) return 'AKTIF';
  if (['NONAKTIF','NON AKTIF','INACTIVE','TIDAK','N','FALSE','0'].indexOf(s) >= 0) return 'NONAKTIF';
  return s;
}

function serializeRawRowV157_(row) {
  const out = {};
  Object.keys(row || {}).forEach(function(k) {
    const v = row[k];
    if (v instanceof Date) out[k] = formatDate_(v, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
    else out[k] = v;
  });
  return out;
}

// =============================================================================
// PUBLIC ACTIONS
// =============================================================================
function getAbsensiBootstrap(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  const outlets = getActiveOutlets_();
  const jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user);
  const riwayat = readAbsensiHariIni_(user);
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    user: publicUser_(user),
    outlets: outlets.map(publicOutlet_),
    jadwal: jadwal,
    riwayat: riwayat,
    data: riwayat,
    exists: !!(riwayat && riwayat.exists)
  };
}

function getAbsensiHariIni(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  const jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user);
  const riwayat = readAbsensiHariIni_(user);
  if (riwayat) riwayat.jadwal = jadwal;
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    exists: !!(riwayat && riwayat.exists),
    user: publicUser_(user),
    jadwal: jadwal,
    riwayat: riwayat,
    data: riwayat
  };
}

function checkin(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(user);

  const existing = findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, todayKey_());
  if (existing && isValidTime_(existing.record['Jam Masuk'])) {
    const data = recordToRiwayat_(existing.record);
    data.jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user);
    return { sukses: false, success: false, already: true, pesan: 'Sudah Check In hari ini.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true };
  }

  const lat = number_(payload.latitude || payload.lat);
  const lng = number_(payload.longitude || payload.lng || payload.lon);
  if (!lat || !lng) throw new Error('GPS belum terbaca. Refresh lokasi terlebih dahulu.');

  const outlets = getActiveOutlets_();
  const outlet = nearestOutlet_(lat, lng, outlets);
  if (!outlet) throw new Error('Data outlet aktif tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.OUTLET.');

  const validation = validateUserOutletRadius_(user, outlet, lat, lng, 'MASUK');
  const jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, outlet.namaOutlet);
  const now = new Date();
  const jamMasuk = formatDate_(now, 'HH:mm:ss');
  const tanggal = formatDate_(now, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
  const dateKey = formatDate_(now, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const terlambat = calculateLateMinutes_(jamMasuk, jadwal);
  const overtime = calculateWorkMetrics_(jamMasuk, '', jadwal);
  const statusMasuk = getStatusMasuk_(jadwal, terlambat);
  const fotoUrl = savePhoto_(payload.foto, user.username + '_CheckIn_' + dateKey + '_' + compactTime_(jamMasuk) + '.jpg');

  const record = {
    'ID Absensi': makeAbsensiId_(user.username, dateKey),
    'Tanggal Key': dateKey,
    'Username': user.username,
    'Level': user.level,
    'Shift': jadwal.shift || '',
    'Jadwal Masuk': jadwal.jamMasuk || '',
    'Jadwal Pulang': jadwal.jamPulang || '',
    'Status Masuk': statusMasuk,
    'Status Pulang': '',
    'Latitude Masuk': lat,
    'Longitude Masuk': lng,
    'Latitude Pulang': '',
    'Longitude Pulang': '',
    'Jarak Masuk': validation.jarak,
    'Jarak Pulang': '',
    'Radius': validation.radius,
    'Device': String(payload.device || ''),
    'Catatan': validation.bypass ? 'Bypass radius: ' + validation.reason : '',
    'Created At': now,
    'Updated At': now,
    'Tanggal': tanggal,
    'Nama': user.nama,
    'Outlet': outlet.namaOutlet,
    'Jam Masuk': jamMasuk,
    'Jam Pulang': '',
    'Foto Masuk': makePhotoLinkFormula_(fotoUrl, 'Foto Cek In'),
    'Foto Pulang': '',
    'Terlambat Menit': terlambat,
    'Lembur Awal Menit': overtime.lemburAwalMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Menit': 0,
    'Total Lembur Menit': overtime.totalLemburMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Aktual Menit': overtime.lemburAwalAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit': 0,
    'Total Lembur Aktual Menit': overtime.totalLemburAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Jam': overtime.lemburAwalJam,
    'Lembur Akhir Jam': 0,
    'Total Lembur Jam': overtime.totalLemburJam,
    'Total Kerja Menit': 0,
    'Istirahat Menit': Number(jadwal.istirahatMenit || 0),
    'Total Kerja Bersih Menit': 0,
    'Total Kerja Bersih': ''
  };

  if (existing) updateRecordByRow_(absensiSheet_(), existing.row, record);
  else appendRecord_(absensiSheet_(), APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129, record);
  try { refreshRekapAbsensiV131({ silent: true }); } catch (rekapErr) { console.log('Refresh rekap V131 gagal: ' + errorMessage_(rekapErr)); }

  const data = recordToRiwayat_(record);
  data.fotoMasuk = fotoUrl;
  data.jadwal = jadwal;
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Check In berhasil.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function checkout(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(user);

  const found = findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, todayKey_());
  if (!found || !isValidTime_(found.record['Jam Masuk'])) {
    throw new Error('Data Check In hari ini belum ditemukan.');
  }
  if (isValidTime_(found.record['Jam Pulang'])) {
    const data = recordToRiwayat_(found.record);
    data.jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, found.record['Outlet']);
    return { sukses: false, success: false, already: true, pesan: 'Sudah Check Out hari ini.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true };
  }

  const lat = number_(payload.latitude || payload.lat);
  const lng = number_(payload.longitude || payload.lng || payload.lon);
  if (!lat || !lng) throw new Error('GPS belum terbaca. Refresh lokasi terlebih dahulu.');

  const outletName = found.record['Outlet'];
  const outlet = getOutletByName_(outletName) || nearestOutlet_(lat, lng, getActiveOutlets_());
  const validation = validateUserOutletRadius_(user, outlet, lat, lng, 'PULANG');
  const jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, outletName);
  const now = new Date();
  const jamPulang = formatDate_(now, 'HH:mm:ss');
  const fotoUrl = savePhoto_(payload.foto, user.username + '_CheckOut_' + todayKey_() + '_' + compactTime_(jamPulang) + '.jpg');
  const statusPulang = getStatusPulang_(jamPulang, jadwal);
  const work = calculateWorkMetrics_(found.record['Jam Masuk'], jamPulang, jadwal);

  const patch = {
    'Status Pulang': statusPulang,
    'Latitude Pulang': lat,
    'Longitude Pulang': lng,
    'Jarak Pulang': validation.jarak,
    'Jam Pulang': jamPulang,
    'Foto Pulang': makePhotoLinkFormula_(fotoUrl, 'Foto Cek Out'),
    'Updated At': now,
    'Lembur Awal Menit': work.lemburAwalMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Menit': work.lemburAkhirMenit,
    'Total Lembur Menit': work.totalLemburMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Aktual Menit': work.lemburAwalAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit': work.lemburAkhirAktualMenit,
    'Total Lembur Aktual Menit': work.totalLemburAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Jam': work.lemburAwalJam,
    'Lembur Akhir Jam': work.lemburAkhirJam,
    'Total Lembur Jam': work.totalLemburJam,
    'Total Kerja Menit': work.totalKerjaMenit,
    'Istirahat Menit': work.istirahatMenit,
    'Total Kerja Bersih Menit': work.totalKerjaBersihMenit,
    'Total Kerja Bersih': work.totalKerjaBersih
  };
  updateRecordByRow_(absensiSheet_(), found.row, patch);
  try { refreshRekapAbsensiV131({ silent: true }); } catch (rekapErr) { console.log('Refresh rekap V131 gagal: ' + errorMessage_(rekapErr)); }

  const updated = Object.assign({}, found.record, patch);
  const data = recordToRiwayat_(updated);
  data.fotoPulang = fotoUrl;
  data.jadwal = jadwal;
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Check Out berhasil.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function setupAbsensiSheetsV129(showResult) {
  const ss = hrSS_();
  const absensi = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI);
  ensureHeaders_(absensi, APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129);
  formatAbsensiSheet_(absensi);
  const rekapHarian = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN);
  ensureHeaders_(rekapHarian, ['Tanggal', 'Nama Lengkap', 'Outlet', 'Shift', 'Jam Masuk', 'Jam Pulang', 'Terlambat', 'Total Kerja', 'Total Lembur', 'Status']);
  const rekapBulanan = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN);
  ensureHeaders_(rekapBulanan, ['Nama Lengkap', 'Bulan', 'Tahun', 'Total Hadir', 'Total Terlambat', 'Total Tidak Hadir', 'Total Libur', 'Total Lembur', 'Total Jam Kerja', 'Status']);
  const legacyHidden = hideLegacyRekapSheetsV129_(ss);
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Setup Absensi V129 selesai. Sheet HR aktif: ID_ABSENSI, REKAP_HARIAN, REKAP_BULANAN.', sheet: ss.getName(), legacyHidden: legacyHidden, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function hideLegacyRekapSheetsV129_(ss) {
  const legacyNames = [
    'REKAP_ABSENSI_KARYAWAN',
    'REKAP_ABSENSI_KARYWAN',
    'REKAP_ABSENSI_KARYAWAN_OLD',
    'REKAP_ABSENSI_KARYWAN_OLD'
  ];
  const activeNames = [APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN];
  let hidden = [];
  legacyNames.forEach(name => {
    const sh = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (sh && activeNames.indexOf(name) < 0 && ss.getSheets().length > 1) {
      try {
        sh.hideSheet();
        hidden.push(name);
      } catch (err) {
        // Jangan gagalkan setup hanya karena sheet legacy tidak bisa di-hide.
      }
    }
  });
  return hidden;
}

function formatAbsensiSheet_(sh) {
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  const lastRow = Math.max(sh.getMaxRows(), 2);
  const textHeaders = ['ID Absensi','Tanggal Key','Username','Level','Shift','Status Masuk','Status Pulang','Device','Catatan','Nama','Outlet','Foto Masuk','Foto Pulang','Total Kerja Bersih'];
  const timeHeaders = ['Jadwal Masuk','Jadwal Pulang','Jam Masuk','Jam Pulang'];
  const dateHeaders = ['Tanggal','Created At','Updated At'];
  const plainNumberHeaders = ['Latitude Masuk','Longitude Masuk','Latitude Pulang','Longitude Pulang','Jarak Masuk','Jarak Pulang','Radius'];
  const minuteHeaders = ['Terlambat Menit','Lembur Awal Menit','Lembur Akhir Menit','Total Lembur Menit','Lembur Awal Aktual Menit','Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit','Total Lembur Aktual Menit','Total Kerja Menit','Istirahat Menit','Total Kerja Bersih Menit'];
  const hourHeaders = ['Lembur Awal Jam','Lembur Akhir Jam','Total Lembur Jam'];
  textHeaders.forEach(h => { const c = headers.indexOf(h) + 1; if (c > 0) sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1).setNumberFormat('@'); });
  timeHeaders.forEach(h => { const c = headers.indexOf(h) + 1; if (c > 0) sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1).setNumberFormat('HH:mm:ss'); });
  dateHeaders.forEach(h => { const c = headers.indexOf(h) + 1; if (c > 0) sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1).setNumberFormat('dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss'); });
  plainNumberHeaders.forEach(h => { const c = headers.indexOf(h) + 1; if (c > 0) sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1).setNumberFormat('0.########'); });
  minuteHeaders.forEach(h => {
    const c = headers.indexOf(h) + 1;
    if (c > 0) sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1).setNumberFormat('0 "Menit"');
  });
  hourHeaders.forEach(h => {
    const c = headers.indexOf(h) + 1;
    if (c > 0) sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1).setNumberFormat('0.## "Jam"');
  });
}

function repairAbsensiLegacyRowsV129() {
  setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  const sh = absensiSheet_();
  const values = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (values.length < 2) return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Tidak ada data yang perlu diperbaiki.', repaired: 0 };
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  let repaired = 0;
  for (let r = 2; r <= values.length; r++) {
    const row = rowObjectFromValues_(headers, values[r - 1]);
    const patch = {};
    const username = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['User']);
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan']);
    const keyNow = inferAbsensiDateKey_(row);
    if (!row['Tanggal Key'] && keyNow) patch['Tanggal Key'] = keyNow;
    if (!row['ID Absensi']) patch['ID Absensi'] = makeAbsensiId_(username || nama || 'USER', patch['Tanggal Key'] || inferAbsensiDateKey_(row) || todayKey_());
    if (!row['Jam Masuk'] && isValidTime_(row['Masuk'])) patch['Jam Masuk'] = normalizeTime_(row['Masuk']);
    if (!row['Jam Pulang'] && isValidTime_(row['Pulang'])) patch['Jam Pulang'] = normalizeTime_(row['Pulang']);
    if (!row['Username'] && username) patch['Username'] = username;
    if (!row['Nama'] && nama) patch['Nama'] = nama;
    const rowUser = getUserByUsernameOrName_(username, nama);
    const dateObj = dateFromKey_(keyNow || patch['Tanggal Key'] || todayKey_());
    const jadwal = rowUser ? getJadwalForDate_(rowUser, dateObj, firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], patch['Outlet'])) : defaultJadwal_('User baris lama tidak ditemukan saat repair.');
    const masuk = normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(patch['Jam Masuk'], row['Jam Masuk'], row['Masuk']));
    const pulang = normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(patch['Jam Pulang'], row['Jam Pulang'], row['Pulang']));
    const late = masuk ? calculateLateMinutes_(masuk, jadwal) : normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Terlambat Menit']);
    if (String(row['Terlambat Menit'] || '') !== String(late) || row['Terlambat Menit'] instanceof Date) patch['Terlambat Menit'] = late;
    if (masuk) {
      const workMasuk = calculateWorkMetrics_(masuk, '', jadwal);
      patch['Lembur Awal Menit'] = workMasuk.lemburAwalMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Aktual Menit'] = workMasuk.lemburAwalAktualMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Menit'] = workMasuk.totalLemburMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Aktual Menit'] = workMasuk.totalLemburAktualMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Jam'] = workMasuk.lemburAwalJam;
      patch['Total Lembur Jam'] = workMasuk.totalLemburJam;
      if (!row['Shift'] && jadwal.shift) patch['Shift'] = jadwal.shift;
      if (!row['Jadwal Masuk'] && jadwal.jamMasuk) patch['Jadwal Masuk'] = jadwal.jamMasuk;
      if (!row['Jadwal Pulang'] && jadwal.jamPulang) patch['Jadwal Pulang'] = jadwal.jamPulang;
      patch['Istirahat Menit'] = Number(jadwal.istirahatMenit || 0);
    }
    if (masuk && pulang) {
      const work = calculateWorkMetrics_(masuk, pulang, jadwal);
      patch['Lembur Awal Menit'] = work.lemburAwalMenit;
      patch['Lembur Akhir Menit'] = work.lemburAkhirMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Menit'] = work.totalLemburMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Aktual Menit'] = work.lemburAwalAktualMenit;
      patch['Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit'] = work.lemburAkhirAktualMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Aktual Menit'] = work.totalLemburAktualMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Jam'] = work.lemburAwalJam;
      patch['Lembur Akhir Jam'] = work.lemburAkhirJam;
      patch['Total Lembur Jam'] = work.totalLemburJam;
      patch['Total Kerja Menit'] = work.totalKerjaMenit;
      patch['Istirahat Menit'] = work.istirahatMenit;
      patch['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] = work.totalKerjaBersihMenit;
      patch['Total Kerja Bersih'] = work.totalKerjaBersih;
    }
    if (Object.keys(patch).length) { updateRecordByRow_(sh, r, patch); repaired++; }
  }
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Repair Absensi V129 selesai.', repaired: repaired, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function cekAbsensiConfigV129(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    coreSpreadsheet: coreSS_().getName(),
    hrSpreadsheet: hrSS_().getName(),
    counts: {
      users: getActiveUsers_().length,
      outlets: getActiveOutlets_().length,
      shifts: readTable_(coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT)).rows.length,
      jadwal: readTable_(coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL)).rows.length,
      absensi: Math.max(absensiSheet_().getLastRow() - 1, 0)
    }
  };
}
