  payload = payload || {};
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  const jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, payload.outlet || '');
  return { sukses: true, success: true, user: publicUser_(user), jadwal: jadwal, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function debugAbsensiV129(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  const found = findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, todayKey_());
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    user: publicUser_(user),
    todayKey: todayKey_(),
    found: !!found,
    row: found ? found.row : null,
    record: found ? found.record : null,
    jadwal: getTodayJadwalForUser_(user),
    headers: getHeaders_(absensiSheet_())
  };
}

// =============================================================================
// MASTER READERS: APJ_CORE_USER
// =============================================================================
function getCurrentUser_(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  if (payload._auth && payload._auth.username) return payload._auth;
  return authorizeHrSession_('getCurrentUser', payload);
}

function authorizeHrSession_(action, payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const profile = getCoreProfileFromSessionHr_(payload);

  // APP-V.4.3 FIX:
  // Core User session adalah sumber utama. Jika server-to-server validation belum sinkron
  // (URL deploy/scope/token), jangan putus Absensi. Fallback ke pencarian USER lokal
  // memakai payload lama seperti APP-V.4.2 agar data absensi tetap berjalan.
  if (profile) {
    const users = getActiveUsers_(true);
    const local = users.find(function(u) { return normKey_(u.username) === normKey_(profile.username); }) ||
                  users.find(function(u) { return normKey_(u.nama) === normKey_(profile.nama); });
    const user = local ? Object.assign({}, local, {
      userId: profile.userId || local.userId,
      username: profile.username || local.username,
      nama: profile.nama || local.nama,
      level: profile.level || local.level,
      outletUtama: profile.outletUtama || local.outletUtama,
      outletAkses: profile.outletAkses || local.outletAkses,
      status: profile.status || local.status,
      permissions: profile.permissions || {},
      sessionToken: profile.sessionToken || '',
      securityMode: 'CORE_SESSION'
    }) : Object.assign({}, profile, { securityMode: 'CORE_SESSION' });
    assertUserActive_(user);
    return user;
  }

  const username = normText_(payload.username || payload.user || '');
  const nama = normText_(payload.nama || payload.name || payload.petugas || '');
  const fallback = getUserByUsernameOrName_(username, nama);
  if (!fallback) throw new Error('User tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.USER: ' + (username || nama || '(kosong)'));
  const user = Object.assign({}, fallback, { sessionToken: getSessionTokenHr_(payload), securityMode: 'COMPAT_FALLBACK_V43_FIX' });
  assertUserActive_(user);
  return user;
}

function getCoreProfileFromSessionHr_(payload) {
  const token = getSessionTokenHr_(payload || {});
  if (!token) return null;
  const cacheKey = 'APJ_HR_CORE_PROFILE_' + token;
  const cached = hrCache_().get(cacheKey);
  if (cached) {
    try { return JSON.parse(cached); } catch (err) {}
  }
  const url = normText_(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.CORE_USER_API_URL || '');
  if (!url) return null;
  try {
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      method: 'post',
      contentType: 'application/json',
      payload: JSON.stringify({ action: 'getMyProfile', sessionToken: token, token: token, appName: 'APJ_HR_ABSENSI' }),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    });
    const text = response.getContentText() || '{}';
    const res = JSON.parse(text);
    if (!res || !res.success || !res.user) return null;
    const profile = normalizeCoreProfileHr_(res.user, token);
    try { hrCache_().put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(profile), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.CACHE_SECONDS || 60); } catch (err) {}
    return profile;
  } catch (err) {
    return null;
  }
}

function normalizeCoreProfileHr_(u, token) {
  u = u || {};
  return {
    userId: firstNonEmpty_(u.userId, u.USER_ID),
    username: firstNonEmpty_(u.username, u.USERNAME),
    nama: firstNonEmpty_(u.nama, u.NAMA, u.name, u.username),
    level: firstNonEmpty_(u.level, u.LEVEL),
    outletUtama: firstNonEmpty_(u.outletUtama, u.outlet, u.OUTLET_UTAMA),
    outletAkses: firstNonEmpty_(u.outletAkses, u.OUTLET_AKSES, u.outletUtama, u.outlet),
    status: firstNonEmpty_(u.status, u.STATUS, 'AKTIF'),
    permissions: u.permissions || {},
    sessionToken: token || ''
  };
}

function getSessionTokenHr_(payload) {
  return normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.sessionToken, payload.token, payload.authToken, payload.APJ_SESSION_TOKEN, payload.apjSessionToken));
}

function getUserByUsernameOrName_(username, nama) {
  const users = getActiveUsers_(true);
  const usernameKey = normKey_(username);
  const namaKey = normKey_(nama);
  if (usernameKey) {
    const byUsername = users.find(u => normKey_(u.username) === usernameKey);
    if (byUsername) return byUsername;
  }
  if (namaKey) {
    const byName = users.find(u => normKey_(u.nama) === namaKey);
    if (byName) return byName;
  }
  return null;
}

function getActiveUsers_(includeAll) {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.USER);
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Sheet USER tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.');
  const table = readTableCached_('CORE', sh);
  return table.rows.map(row => {
    const status = firstNonEmpty_(row['STATUS'], row['Status'], row['status']);
    return {
      userId: firstNonEmpty_(row['USER_ID'], row['User ID'], row['ID User'], row['ID']),
      username: firstNonEmpty_(row['USERNAME'], row['Username'], row['username']),
      nama: firstNonEmpty_(row['NAMA'], row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['NAMA LENGKAP']),
      level: firstNonEmpty_(row['LEVEL'], row['Level'], row['level']),
      outletUtama: firstNonEmpty_(row['OUTLET_UTAMA'], row['Outlet Utama'], row['Outlet']),
      outletAkses: firstNonEmpty_(row['OUTLET_AKSES'], row['Outlet Akses'], row['Akses Outlet']),
      status: status || 'AKTIF'
    };
  }).filter(u => includeAll || normKey_(u.status) === 'aktif');
}

function getActiveOutlets_() {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.OUTLET);
  if (!sh) throw new Error('Sheet OUTLET tidak ditemukan di APJ_CORE_USER.');
  const table = readTableCached_('CORE', sh);
  return table.rows.map(row => {
    const status = firstNonEmpty_(row['STATUS'], row['Status'], row['status']);
    return {
      outletId: firstNonEmpty_(row['OUTLET_ID'], row['Outlet ID']),
      kodeOutlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['KODE_OUTLET'], row['Kode Outlet'], row['Kode']),
      namaOutlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['NAMA_OUTLET'], row['Nama Outlet'], row['OUTLET'], row['Outlet']),
      status: status || 'AKTIF',
      latitude: number_(firstNonEmpty_(row['LATITUDE'], row['Latitude'], row['LAT'])),
      longitude: number_(firstNonEmpty_(row['LONGTITUDE'], row['LONGITUDE'], row['Longitude'], row['LON'], row['LNG'])),
      radius: number_(firstNonEmpty_(row['RADIUS_METER'], row['Radius Meter'], row['Radius'])) || 100
    };
  }).filter(o => normKey_(o.status) === 'aktif' && o.namaOutlet && o.latitude && o.longitude);
}

function getOutletByName_(name) {
  const key = normKey_(name);
  if (!key) return null;
  return getActiveOutlets_().find(o => normKey_(o.namaOutlet) === key || normKey_(o.kodeOutlet) === key) || null;
}

function getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, preferredOutlet) {
  const today = new Date();
  return getJadwalForDate_(user, today, preferredOutlet);
}

function getJadwalForDate_(user, dateObj, preferredOutlet) {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL);
  if (!sh) return defaultJadwal_('Sheet ID_JADWAL belum ada di APJ_CORE_USER.');
  const table = readTableCached_('CORE', sh);
  const day = String(Number(formatDate_(dateObj, 'd')));
  const monthName = monthNameId_(dateObj);
  const year = String(dateObj.getFullYear());
  const nameKey = normKey_(user.nama);
  const outletPreferred = normKey_(preferredOutlet || user.outletUtama || '');
  const candidates = table.rows.filter(row => {
    const rowName = normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama']));
    const rowMonth = normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Bulan'], row['BULAN']));
    const rowYear = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Tahun'], row['TAHUN']) || '').trim();
    return rowName === nameKey && rowMonth === normKey_(monthName) && rowYear === year;
  });
  if (!candidates.length) return defaultJadwal_('Jadwal tidak ditemukan untuk ' + user.nama + ' ' + monthName + ' ' + year + '.');
  let row = candidates[0];
  if (outletPreferred) row = candidates.find(r => normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(r['Outlet'], r['OUTLET'])) === outletPreferred) || row;
  const shiftName = firstNonEmpty_(row[day], row[String(day).padStart(2, '0')]);
  if (!shiftName) return defaultJadwal_('Kolom tanggal ' + day + ' belum diisi.');
  if (normKey_(shiftName) === 'libur') {
    return {
      found: true,
      isLibur: true,
      shift: 'LIBUR',
      outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']) || preferredOutlet || user.outletUtama || '',
      jamMasuk: '',
      jamPulang: '',
      toleransiMenit: 0,
      istirahatMenit: 0,
      hitungLemburAwal: true,
      hitungLemburAkhir: false,
      minimalLemburMenit: 60,
      pembulatanLemburMenit: 60,
      metodePembulatanLembur: 'TURUN',
      catatan: 'Jadwal LIBUR'
    };
  }
  const shift = getShiftByName_(shiftName, firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']) || preferredOutlet || user.outletUtama || '');
  if (!shift) {
    return {
      found: true,
      isLibur: false,
      shift: shiftName,
      outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']) || '',
      jamMasuk: '',
      jamPulang: '',
      toleransiMenit: 0,
      istirahatMenit: 0,
      hitungLemburAwal: true,
      hitungLemburAkhir: false,
      minimalLemburMenit: 60,
      pembulatanLemburMenit: 60,
      metodePembulatanLembur: 'TURUN',
      catatan: 'Shift tidak ditemukan di ID_SHIFT: ' + shiftName
    };
  }
  return {
    found: true,
    isLibur: false,
    shift: shift.namaShift,
    outlet: shift.outlet,
    jamMasuk: shift.jamMasuk,
    jamPulang: shift.jamPulang,
    toleransiMenit: shift.toleransiMenit,
    istirahatMenit: shift.istirahatMenit,
    hitungLemburAwal: shift.hitungLemburAwal,
    hitungLemburAkhir: shift.hitungLemburAkhir,
    minimalLemburMenit: shift.minimalLemburMenit,
    pembulatanLemburMenit: shift.pembulatanLemburMenit,
    metodePembulatanLembur: shift.metodePembulatanLembur,
    catatan: ''
  };
}

function getShiftByName_(shiftName, outlet) {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT);
  if (!sh) return null;
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  const shiftKey = normKey_(shiftName);
  const outletKey = normKey_(outlet);
  const rows = table.rows.map(row => ({
    namaShift: firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Shift'], row['Shift'], row['SHIFT']),
    outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']),
    jamMasuk: normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Masuk'], row['Masuk'])),
    jamPulang: normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Pulang'], row['Pulang'])),
    toleransiMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Toleransi Keterlambatan'], row['Tolerasi Keterlambatan'], row['Toleransi'], row['Telat'])),
    istirahatMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Istirahat'], row['Break'])),
    hitungLemburAwal: parseBool_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Hitung Lembur Awal'], row['Lembur Awal'], row['Auto Lembur Awal']), true),
    hitungLemburAkhir: parseBool_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Hitung Lembur Akhir'], row['Lembur Akhir'], row['Auto Lembur Akhir']), false),
    minimalLemburMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Minimal Lembur Menit'], row['Minimal Lembur'], row['Minimum Lembur'])) || 60,
    pembulatanLemburMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Pembulatan Lembur Menit'], row['Pembulatan Lembur'], row['Kelipatan Lembur'])) || 60,
    metodePembulatanLembur: String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Metode Pembulatan Lembur'], row['Metode Lembur'], row['Pembulatan']) || 'TURUN').trim().toUpperCase()
  })).filter(s => normKey_(s.namaShift) === shiftKey);
  if (!rows.length) return null;
  return rows.find(s => normKey_(s.outlet) === outletKey) || rows[0];
}

function defaultJadwal_(catatan) {
  return { found: false, isLibur: false, shift: '', outlet: '', jamMasuk: '', jamPulang: '', toleransiMenit: 0, istirahatMenit: 0, hitungLemburAwal: true, hitungLemburAkhir: false, minimalLemburMenit: 60, pembulatanLemburMenit: 60, metodePembulatanLembur: 'TURUN', catatan: catatan || '' };
}

// =============================================================================
// ABSENSI SHEET READ/WRITE
// =============================================================================
function readAbsensiHariIni_(user) {
  const found = findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, todayKey_());
  if (!found) {
    return {
      exists: false,
      tanggal: formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
      jamMasuk: '',
      jamPulang: '',
      status: 'Belum Absen',
      statusMasuk: '',
      statusPulang: '',
      terlambatMenit: 0
    };
  }
  return recordToRiwayat_(found.record);
}

function findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, dateKey) {
  const sh = absensiSheet_();
  const values = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (values.length < 2) return null;
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  const usernameKey = normKey_(user && user.username);
  const namaKey = normKey_(user && user.nama);
  for (let r = values.length; r >= 2; r--) {
    const record = rowObjectFromValues_(headers, values[r - 1]);
    const rowDateKey = inferAbsensiDateKey_(record);
    if (rowDateKey !== dateKey) continue;
    const rowUserKey = normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(record['Username'], record['User']));
    const rowNameKey = normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(record['Nama'], record['Nama Lengkap'], record['Nama Karyawan']));
    const sameUser = (usernameKey && rowUserKey === usernameKey) || (namaKey && rowNameKey === namaKey);
    if (sameUser) return { row: r, record: record };
  }
  return null;
}

function findAbsensiRow_(username, dateKey) {
  return findAbsensiRowForUser_({ username: username, nama: '' }, dateKey);
}

function inferAbsensiDateKey_(record) {
  return inferDateKey_(firstNonEmpty_(record && record['Tanggal Key'], record && record['Tanggal'], record && record['Created At'], record && record['Updated At']));
}

function recordToRiwayat_(record) {
  const masuk = normalizeTime_(record['Jam Masuk']);
  const pulang = normalizeTime_(record['Jam Pulang']);
  const statusMasuk = String(record['Status Masuk'] || '').trim();
  const statusPulang = String(record['Status Pulang'] || '').trim();
  let status = 'Belum Absen';
  if (masuk && pulang) status = statusPulang || 'Selesai';
  else if (masuk) status = statusMasuk || 'Sudah Check In';
  return {
    exists: !!masuk,
    idAbsensi: record['ID Absensi'] || '',
    tanggalKey: record['Tanggal Key'] || '',
    tanggal: displayDate_(record['Tanggal'] || record['Created At'] || new Date()),
    username: record['Username'] || '',
    nama: record['Nama'] || '',
    level: record['Level'] || '',
    outlet: record['Outlet'] || '',
    shift: record['Shift'] || '',
    jadwalMasuk: normalizeTime_(record['Jadwal Masuk']),
    jadwalPulang: normalizeTime_(record['Jadwal Pulang']),
    jamMasuk: masuk,
    masuk: masuk,
    jamPulang: pulang,
    pulang: pulang,
    status: status,
    statusMasuk: statusMasuk,
    statusPulang: statusPulang,
    terlambatMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Terlambat Menit']),
    terlambat: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Terlambat Menit']),
    lemburAwalMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Lembur Awal Menit']),
    lemburAkhirMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Lembur Akhir Menit']),
    totalLemburMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Total Lembur Menit']),
    lemburAwalAktualMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Lembur Awal Aktual Menit']),
    lemburAkhirAktualMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit']),
    totalLemburAktualMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Total Lembur Aktual Menit']),
    lemburAwalJam: number_(record['Lembur Awal Jam']),
    lemburAkhirJam: number_(record['Lembur Akhir Jam']),
    totalLemburJam: number_(record['Total Lembur Jam']),
    totalLemburLabel: hoursToText_(number_(record['Total Lembur Jam'])),
    totalKerjaMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Total Kerja Menit']),
    istirahatMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Istirahat Menit']),
    totalKerjaBersihMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Total Kerja Bersih Menit']),
    totalKerjaBersih: record['Total Kerja Bersih'] || minutesToDurationText_(normalizeLateMinutes_(record['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'])),
    fotoMasuk: photoValueToUrl_(record['Foto Masuk']),
    fotoPulang: photoValueToUrl_(record['Foto Pulang'])
  };
}

function appendRecord_(sh, headers, record) {
  ensureHeaders_(sh, headers);
  const finalHeaders = getHeaders_(sh);
  const row = finalHeaders.map(h => record[h] !== undefined ? record[h] : '');
  sh.appendRow(row);
}

function updateRecordByRow_(sh, rowNumber, patch) {
  ensureHeaders_(sh, APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129);
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  Object.keys(patch || {}).forEach(key => {
    const col = headers.indexOf(key) + 1;
    if (col > 0) sh.getRange(rowNumber, col).setValue(patch[key]);
  });
}

// =============================================================================
// VALIDATION / CALCULATION
// =============================================================================
function validateUserOutletRadius_(user, outlet, lat, lng, mode) {
  if (!outlet) throw new Error('Outlet tidak ditemukan.');
  const jarak = Math.round(distanceMeters_(lat, lng, outlet.latitude, outlet.longitude));
  const radius = Number(outlet.radius || 100);
  const bypass = isBypassUser_(user);
  if (bypass) return { ok: true, bypass: true, reason: user.level || user.username, jarak: jarak, radius: radius };
  if (!userHasOutletAccess_(user, outlet)) throw new Error('Outlet tidak sesuai akses user. User: ' + user.nama + ', Outlet GPS: ' + outlet.namaOutlet);
  if (jarak > radius) throw new Error('Di luar radius outlet ' + outlet.namaOutlet + '. Jarak: ' + jarak + ' meter, Radius: ' + radius + ' meter.');
  return { ok: true, bypass: false, reason: '', jarak: jarak, radius: radius };
}

function userHasOutletAccess_(user, outlet) {
  const tokens = String(user.outletAkses || user.outletUtama || '').split(/[;,|]/).map(normKey_).filter(Boolean);
  if (!tokens.length) return false;
  if (tokens.indexOf('all') >= 0 || tokens.indexOf('semua') >= 0 || tokens.indexOf('semuaoutlet') >= 0) return true;
  const aliases = [outlet.namaOutlet, outlet.kodeOutlet].map(normKey_).filter(Boolean);
  return tokens.some(t => aliases.indexOf(t) >= 0);
}

function isBypassUser_(user) {
  const username = normKey_(user.username);
  const level = String(user.level || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  return APJ_HR_ABSENSI.OWNER_USERNAMES.map(normKey_).indexOf(username) >= 0 || APJ_HR_ABSENSI.OWNER_LEVELS.indexOf(level) >= 0;
}

function getStatusMasuk_(jadwal, terlambat) {
  if (jadwal && jadwal.isLibur) return 'MASUK HARI LIBUR';
  if (terlambat > 0) return 'TERLAMBAT';
  return 'TEPAT WAKTU';
}

function getStatusPulang_(jamPulang, jadwal) {
  if (jadwal && jadwal.isLibur) return 'PULANG HARI LIBUR';
  if (jadwal && jadwal.jamPulang) {
    const actual = timeToMinutes_(jamPulang);
    const scheduled = timeToMinutes_(jadwal.jamPulang);
    if (actual < scheduled) return 'PULANG CEPAT';
  }
  return 'PULANG';
}

function calculateLateMinutes_(jamMasuk, jadwal) {
  if (!jadwal || jadwal.isLibur || !jadwal.jamMasuk) return 0;
  const actual = timeToMinutes_(jamMasuk);
  const scheduled = timeToMinutes_(jadwal.jamMasuk) + Number(jadwal.toleransiMenit || 0);
  return Math.max(0, actual - scheduled);
}

function calculateLemburAwalMinutes_(jamMasuk, jadwal) {
  if (!jadwal || jadwal.isLibur || !jadwal.jamMasuk) return 0;
  const actual = timeToMinutes_(jamMasuk);
  const scheduled = timeToMinutes_(jadwal.jamMasuk);
  return Math.max(0, scheduled - actual);
}

function calculateLemburAkhirMinutes_(jamPulang, jadwal) {
  if (!jadwal || jadwal.isLibur || !jadwal.jamPulang) return 0;
  let actual = timeToMinutes_(jamPulang);
  const scheduledIn = jadwal.jamMasuk ? timeToMinutes_(jadwal.jamMasuk) : 0;
  let scheduledOut = timeToMinutes_(jadwal.jamPulang);
  // Jaga-jaga untuk shift lintas hari. Tidak mengubah shift di sheet, hanya cara hitung.
  if (jadwal.jamMasuk && scheduledOut < scheduledIn) scheduledOut += 24 * 60;
  if (jadwal.jamMasuk && actual < scheduledIn) actual += 24 * 60;
  return Math.max(0, actual - scheduledOut);
}

function calculateWorkMetrics_(jamMasuk, jamPulang, jadwal) {
  const hasMasuk = isValidTime_(jamMasuk);
  const hasPulang = isValidTime_(jamPulang);
  const masuk = hasMasuk ? timeToMinutes_(jamMasuk) : 0;
  let pulang = hasPulang ? timeToMinutes_(jamPulang) : 0;
  if (hasMasuk && hasPulang && pulang < masuk) pulang += 24 * 60;

  const totalKerjaMenit = hasMasuk && hasPulang ? Math.max(0, pulang - masuk) : 0;
  const istirahatMenit = Math.max(0, Number(jadwal && jadwal.istirahatMenit || 0));
  const totalKerjaBersihMenit = Math.max(0, totalKerjaMenit - istirahatMenit);

  let lemburAwalAktualMenit = hasMasuk ? calculateLemburAwalMinutes_(jamMasuk, jadwal) : 0;
  let lemburAkhirAktualMenit = hasPulang ? calculateLemburAkhirMinutes_(jamPulang, jadwal) : 0;

  // Owner-safe default:
  // - Lembur awal otomatis dihitung karena datang lebih awal biasanya memang bantuan operasional.
  // - Lembur akhir default TIDAK otomatis dihitung untuk menghindari kasus sudah selesai kerja tapi lupa checkout.
  //   Jika butuh, tambah kolom ID_SHIFT: Hitung Lembur Akhir = YA.
  if (jadwal && jadwal.hitungLemburAwal === false) lemburAwalAktualMenit = 0;
  if (!jadwal || jadwal.hitungLemburAkhir !== true) lemburAkhirAktualMenit = 0;

  let lemburAwalMenit = roundOvertimePayableMinutes_(lemburAwalAktualMenit, jadwal);
  let lemburAkhirMenit = roundOvertimePayableMinutes_(lemburAkhirAktualMenit, jadwal);
  let totalLemburAktualMenit = lemburAwalAktualMenit + lemburAkhirAktualMenit;
  let totalLemburMenit = lemburAwalMenit + lemburAkhirMenit;

  if (jadwal && jadwal.isLibur) {
    lemburAwalAktualMenit = 0;
    lemburAkhirAktualMenit = 0;
    totalLemburAktualMenit = totalKerjaBersihMenit;
    totalLemburMenit = roundOvertimePayableMinutes_(totalKerjaBersihMenit, jadwal);
    lemburAwalMenit = 0;
    lemburAkhirMenit = 0;
  }

  const lemburAwalJam = minutesToHours_(lemburAwalMenit);
  const lemburAkhirJam = minutesToHours_(lemburAkhirMenit);
  const totalLemburJam = minutesToHours_(totalLemburMenit);

  return {
    lemburAwalMenit: lemburAwalMenit,
    lemburAkhirMenit: lemburAkhirMenit,
    totalLemburMenit: totalLemburMenit,
    lemburAwalAktualMenit: lemburAwalAktualMenit,
    lemburAkhirAktualMenit: lemburAkhirAktualMenit,
    totalLemburAktualMenit: totalLemburAktualMenit,
    lemburAwalJam: lemburAwalJam,
    lemburAkhirJam: lemburAkhirJam,
    totalLemburJam: totalLemburJam,
    totalKerjaMenit: totalKerjaMenit,
    istirahatMenit: istirahatMenit,
    totalKerjaBersihMenit: totalKerjaBersihMenit,
    totalKerjaBersih: minutesToDurationText_(totalKerjaBersihMenit)
  };
}

function roundOvertimePayableMinutes_(mins, jadwal) {
  mins = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(mins || 0)));
  const minimal = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(jadwal && jadwal.minimalLemburMenit || 60)));
  const step = Math.max(1, Math.round(Number(jadwal && jadwal.pembulatanLemburMenit || 60)));
  const method = normKey_(jadwal && jadwal.metodePembulatanLembur || 'TURUN');
  if (mins < minimal) return 0;
  if (method === 'naik' || method === 'ceil' || method === 'up') return Math.ceil(mins / step) * step;
  if (method === 'terdekat' || method === 'nearest' || method === 'round') return Math.round(mins / step) * step;
  // Default paling aman untuk owner: dibulatkan turun ke blok penuh.
  return Math.floor(mins / step) * step;
}

function minutesToHours_(mins) {
  return Math.round((Math.max(0, Number(mins || 0)) / 60) * 100) / 100;
}

function hoursToText_(hours) {
  hours = Math.max(0, Number(hours || 0));
  if (!hours) return '';
  const rounded = Math.round(hours * 100) / 100;
  if (Math.abs(rounded - Math.round(rounded)) < 0.001) return Math.round(rounded) + ' jam';
  return String(rounded).replace('.', ',') + ' jam';
}

function parseBool_(value, defaultValue) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null || String(value).trim() === '') return !!defaultValue;
  const s = normKey_(value);
  if (['ya','y','yes','true','aktif','1','iya'].indexOf(s) >= 0) return true;
  if (['tidak','tdk','no','false','nonaktif','0','n'].indexOf(s) >= 0) return false;
  return !!defaultValue;
}

function minutesToDurationText_(mins) {
  mins = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(mins || 0)));
  const h = Math.floor(mins / 60);
  const m = mins % 60;
  // V128: Total kerja selalu tampil jam + menit agar konsisten untuk laporan,
  // contoh 2 menit => 0 jam 2 menit, 13 jam => 13 jam 0 menit.
  return h + ' jam ' + m + ' menit';
}

function nearestOutlet_(lat, lng, outlets) {
  let best = null;
  let bestDistance = Infinity;
  (outlets || []).forEach(o => {
    const d = distanceMeters_(lat, lng, o.latitude, o.longitude);
    if (d < bestDistance) { bestDistance = d; best = Object.assign({}, o, { jarak: Math.round(d) }); }
  });
  return best;
}

function distanceMeters_(lat1, lon1, lat2, lon2) {
  const R = 6371000;
  const dLat = (lat2 - lat1) * Math.PI / 180;
  const dLon = (lon2 - lon1) * Math.PI / 180;
  const a = Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
    Math.cos(lat1 * Math.PI / 180) * Math.cos(lat2 * Math.PI / 180) *
    Math.sin(dLon / 2) * Math.sin(dLon / 2);
  return R * 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));
}

// =============================================================================
// PHOTO DRIVE
// =============================================================================
function savePhoto_(fotoBase64, fileName) {
  if (!fotoBase64 || String(fotoBase64).indexOf('base64,') < 0) return '';
  const root = DriveApp.getFolderById(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.FOTO_FOLDER_ID);
  const now = new Date();
  const bulan = monthNameId_(now) + ' ' + now.getFullYear();
  const tanggal = String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0') + ' ' + bulan;
  const monthFolder = getOrCreateFolder_(root, bulan);
  const dayFolder = getOrCreateFolder_(monthFolder, tanggal);
  const cleanName = String(fileName || ('absensi_' + now.getTime() + '.jpg')).replace(/[\\/:*?"<>|]+/g, '_');
  const bytes = Utilities.base64Decode(String(fotoBase64).split('base64,')[1]);
  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(bytes, 'image/jpeg', cleanName);
  const file = dayFolder.createFile(blob);
  return file.getUrl();
}


function makePhotoLinkFormula_(url, label) {
  url = String(url || '').trim();
  label = String(label || 'Foto').trim();
  if (!url) return '';
  return '=HYPERLINK("' + url.replace(/"/g, '""') + '","' + label.replace(/"/g, '""') + '")';
}

function photoValueToUrl_(value) {
  if (!value) return '';
  const s = String(value || '').trim();
  const m = s.match(/^=HYPERLINK\("([^"]+)"\s*[,;]\s*"[^"]*"\)/i);
  if (m) return m[1];
  if (/^https?:\/\//i.test(s)) return s;
  return s;
}

function getOrCreateFolder_(parent, name) {
  const folders = parent.getFoldersByName(name);
  return folders.hasNext() ? folders.next() : parent.createFolder(name);
}

// =============================================================================
// SPREADSHEET UTILS
// =============================================================================
function coreSS_() { return SpreadsheetApp.openById(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.CORE_SPREADSHEET_ID); }
function hrSS_() { return SpreadsheetApp.openById(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.HR_SPREADSHEET_ID); }
function inventorySS_() { return SpreadsheetApp.openById(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.INVENTORY_SPREADSHEET_ID); }
function absensiSheet_() { return getOrCreateSheet_(hrSS_(), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI); }
function hrCache_() { return CacheService.getScriptCache(); }
function hrTableCacheKey_(scope, sheetName) { return 'APJ_HR_TABLE_' + scope + '_' + sheetName; }
function clearHrSheetCache_(scope, sheetName) {
  try { hrCache_().remove(hrTableCacheKey_(scope, sheetName)); } catch (err) {}
}
function clearHrMasterCache_() {
  const keys = [
    hrTableCacheKey_('CORE', APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.USER),
    hrTableCacheKey_('CORE', APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.OUTLET),
    hrTableCacheKey_('CORE', APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT),
    hrTableCacheKey_('CORE', APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL)
  ];
  try { hrCache_().removeAll(keys); } catch (err) {}
}

function getOrCreateSheet_(ss, name) {
  return ss.getSheetByName(name) || ss.insertSheet(name);
}

function ensureHeaders_(sh, headers) {
  if (sh.getLastRow() < 1) sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  let existing = getHeaders_(sh);
  if (!existing.length || existing.every(h => !h)) {
    sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
    existing = headers.slice();
  }
  const missing = headers.filter(h => existing.indexOf(h) < 0);
  if (missing.length) {
    sh.getRange(1, existing.length + 1, 1, missing.length).setValues([missing]);
  }
  sh.setFrozenRows(1);
}

function getHeaders_(sh) {
  const lastCol = Math.max(sh.getLastColumn(), 1);
  return sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0].map(v => String(v || '').trim());
}

function readTable_(sh) {
  if (!sh) return { headers: [], rows: [] };
  const range = sh.getDataRange();
  const values = range.getValues();
  if (!values.length) return { headers: [], rows: [] };
  const headers = values[0].map(v => String(v || '').trim());
  let formulas = null;
  try { formulas = range.getFormulas(); } catch (err) { formulas = null; }
  const fotoCols = {};
  headers.forEach((h, i) => { if (h === 'Foto Masuk' || h === 'Foto Pulang') fotoCols[i] = true; });
  const rows = values.slice(1).filter(row => row.some(v => String(v || '').trim() !== '')).map((row, idx) => {
    const safeRow = row.slice();
    Object.keys(fotoCols).forEach(k => {
      const c = Number(k);
      if (formulas && formulas[idx + 1] && formulas[idx + 1][c]) safeRow[c] = formulas[idx + 1][c];
    });
    return rowObjectFromValues_(headers, safeRow);
  });
  return { headers: headers, rows: rows };
}

function readTableCached_(scope, sh) {
  if (!sh) return { headers: [], rows: [] };
  const key = hrTableCacheKey_(scope || 'GEN', sh.getName());
  const cached = hrCache_().get(key);
  if (cached) {
    try { return JSON.parse(cached); } catch (err) {}
  }
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  try {
    const text = JSON.stringify(table);
    if (text.length < 90000) hrCache_().put(key, text, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.CACHE_SECONDS || 60);
  } catch (err) {}
  return table;
}

function rowObjectFromValues_(headers, row) {
  const obj = {};
  headers.forEach((h, i) => { if (h) obj[h] = row[i]; });
  return obj;
}

// =============================================================================
// FORMAT / PARSE UTILS
// =============================================================================
function publicUser_(u) {
  return {
    userId: u.userId || '',
    username: u.username || '',
    nama: u.nama || '',
    level: u.level || '',
    outlet: u.outletUtama || '',
    outletAkses: u.outletAkses || '',
    status: u.status || ''
  };
}

function publicOutlet_(o) {
  return { outlet: o.namaOutlet, kodeOutlet: o.kodeOutlet, latitude: o.latitude, longitude: o.longitude, radius: o.radius };
}

function assertUserActive_(user) {
  if (!user) throw new Error('User tidak ditemukan.');
  if (normKey_(user.status || 'AKTIF') !== 'aktif') throw new Error('User tidak aktif.');
}

function firstNonEmpty_() {
  for (let i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++) {
    const v = arguments[i];
    if (v !== undefined && v !== null && String(v).trim() !== '') return v;
  }
  return '';
}

function normText_(v) { return String(v || '').trim(); }
function normKey_(v) { return String(v || '').trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '').replace(/[_-]+/g, ''); }
function number_(v) {
  if (v instanceof Date) return 0;
  const n = Number(String(v || '').replace(',', '.'));
  return isNaN(n) ? 0 : n;
}

function todayKey_() { return formatDate_(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd'); }
function dateFromKey_(key) {
  const k = inferDateKey_(key) || todayKey_();
  const p = String(k).split('-').map(Number);
  return new Date(p[0] || new Date().getFullYear(), (p[1] || 1) - 1, p[2] || 1);
}
function formatDate_(date, pattern) { return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(date), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.TIMEZONE, pattern); }
function displayDate_(value) {
  if (!value) return formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy');
  if (value instanceof Date) return formatDate_(value, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
  return String(value);
}

function inferDateKey_(value) {
  if (!value) return '';
  if (value instanceof Date) return formatDate_(value, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const s = String(value).trim();
  const m1 = s.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{1,2})-(\d{1,2})/);
  if (m1) return m1[1] + '-' + m1[2].padStart(2, '0') + '-' + m1[3].padStart(2, '0');
  const m2 = s.match(/^(\d{1,2})\/(\d{1,2})\/(\d{4})/);
  if (m2) return m2[3] + '-' + m2[2].padStart(2, '0') + '-' + m2[1].padStart(2, '0');
  return '';
}

function monthNameId_(date) {
  return ['Januari','Februari','Maret','April','Mei','Juni','Juli','Agustus','September','Oktober','November','Desember'][new Date(date).getMonth()];
}

function normalizeTime_(value) {
  if (!value) return '';
  if (value instanceof Date) return formatDate_(value, 'HH:mm:ss');
  const s = String(value).trim();
  if (!s || s === '-' || s.toLowerCase() === 'null' || s.toLowerCase() === 'undefined') return '';
  const m = s.match(/(\d{1,2})[:.](\d{2})(?:[:.](\d{2}))?/);
  if (m) return m[1].padStart(2, '0') + ':' + m[2].padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(m[3] || '00').padStart(2, '0');
  return s;
}

function isValidTime_(value) { return !!normalizeTime_(value); }
function compactTime_(time) { return String(time || '').replace(/\D+/g, ''); }

function timeToMinutes_(value) {
  const t = normalizeTime_(value);
  if (!t) return 0;
  const p = t.split(':').map(Number);
  return (p[0] || 0) * 60 + (p[1] || 0);
}

function parseDurationMinutes_(value) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null || value === '') return 0;
  if (typeof value === 'number') return value;
  const s = String(value).trim().toLowerCase();
  const n = Number((s.match(/-?\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?/) || ['0'])[0].replace(',', '.'));
  if (s.indexOf('jam') >= 0 || s.indexOf('hour') >= 0) return Math.round(n * 60);
  return Math.round(n);
}

function normalizeLateMinutes_(value) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null || value === '') return 0;
  if (value instanceof Date) {
    // Google Sheets bisa mengubah menit jadi Date serial 30/12/1899 00:mm.
    return Math.max(0, Math.round(value.getHours() * 60 + value.getMinutes() + (value.getSeconds() >= 30 ? 1 : 0)));
  }
  if (typeof value === 'number') {
    // Kalau angka kecil pecahan hari (format time), ubah ke menit. Kalau angka biasa, tetap menit.
    if (value > 0 && value < 1) return Math.round(value * 24 * 60);
    return Math.max(0, Math.round(value));
  }
  const s = String(value).trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!s || s === '-' || s === 'null' || s === 'undefined') return 0;
  const n = Number((s.match(/-?\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?/) || ['0'])[0].replace(',', '.'));
  if (s.indexOf('jam') >= 0 || s.indexOf('hour') >= 0) return Math.round(n * 60);
  return Math.max(0, Math.round(n));
}


function makeAbsensiId_(username, dateKey) {
  const base = String(username || 'USER').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 12) || 'USER';
  return 'ABS-' + String(dateKey || todayKey_()).replace(/-/g, '') + '-' + base;
}

function errorMessage_(err) {
  const msg = err && err.message ? err.message : String(err || 'Terjadi error');
  return msg.replace(/^Exception:\s*/i, '');
}

const APJ_REKAP_HARIAN_HEADERS_V131 = [
  'ID Absensi',
  'Tanggal Key',
  'Tanggal',
  'Username',
  'Nama Lengkap',
  'Outlet',
  'Shift',
  'Jadwal Masuk',
  'Jadwal Pulang',
  'Jam Masuk',
  'Jam Pulang',
  'Status Masuk',
  'Status Pulang',
  'Terlambat Menit',
  'Total Kerja',
  'Total Kerja Menit',
  'Total Lembur',
  'Total Lembur Jam',
  'Foto Masuk',
  'Foto Pulang',
  'Update Terakhir'
];

const APJ_REKAP_BULANAN_HEADERS_V131 = [
  'Nama Lengkap',
  'Bulan',
  'Tahun',
  'Outlet',
  'Total Hari',
  'Total Hadir',
  'Total Terlambat',
  'Total Tidak Hadir',
  'Total Libur',
  'Tidak Checkout',
  'Total Lembur',
  'Total Lembur Jam',
  'Total Jam Kerja',
  'Total Jam Kerja Menit',
  'Status',
  'Update Terakhir'
];

function setupAbsensiSheetsV131(showResult) {
  const ss = hrSS_();
  const absensi = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI);
  ensureHeaders_(absensi, APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129);
  formatAbsensiSheet_(absensi);

  const rekapHarian = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN);
  ensureHeaders_(rekapHarian, APJ_REKAP_HARIAN_HEADERS_V131);
  formatRekapHarianSheetV131_(rekapHarian);

  const rekapBulanan = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN);
  ensureHeaders_(rekapBulanan, APJ_REKAP_BULANAN_HEADERS_V131);
  formatRekapBulananSheetV131_(rekapBulanan);

  const legacyHidden = hideLegacyRekapSheetsV129_(ss);
  const rekap = showResult === false ? null : refreshRekapAbsensiV131({ silent: true });
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Setup Absensi V131 selesai. Rekap aman dari error format kolom dan siap trigger otomatis.',
    sheet: ss.getName(),
    legacyHidden: legacyHidden,
    rekap: rekap,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function repairAbsensiLegacyRowsV131() {
  const repaired = repairAbsensiLegacyRowsV129();
  const rekap = refreshRekapAbsensiV131({ silent: true });
  return Object.assign({}, repaired || {}, {
    pesan: 'Repair Absensi V131 selesai dan rekap sudah diperbarui.',
    rekap: rekap,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  });
}

function cekAbsensiConfigV131(payload) {
  const base = cekAbsensiConfigV129(payload || {});
  const ss = hrSS_();
  return Object.assign({}, base, {
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    rekap: {
      harianRows: Math.max((ss.getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN) || { getLastRow: function(){ return 1; } }).getLastRow() - 1, 0),
      bulananRows: Math.max((ss.getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN) || { getLastRow: function(){ return 1; } }).getLastRow() - 1, 0)
    }
  });
}

function cekJadwalShiftV131(payload) { return cekJadwalShiftV129(payload || {}); }
function debugAbsensiV131(payload) {
  const base = debugAbsensiV129(payload || {});
  const rekap = refreshRekapAbsensiV131({ silent: true });
  return Object.assign({}, base, { version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION, rekap: rekap });
}

function refreshRekapAbsensiV131(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const useLock = payload.noLock !== true;
  const lock = useLock ? LockService.getScriptLock() : null;
  let locked = false;
  try {
    if (lock) {
      locked = lock.tryLock(30000);
      if (!locked) {
        return {
          sukses: false,
          success: false,
          pesan: 'Rekap sedang diproses oleh trigger/proses lain. Coba lagi beberapa detik.',
          version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
        };
      }
    }
    const ss = hrSS_();
    const harian = rebuildRekapHarianV131_(ss);
    const bulanan = rebuildRekapBulananV131_(ss);
    return {
      sukses: true,
      success: true,
      pesan: 'Rekap Absensi V131 selesai diperbarui.',
      harian: harian,
      bulanan: bulanan,
      version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
    };
  } finally {
    if (lock && locked) {
      try { lock.releaseLock(); } catch (err) {}
    }
  }
}

function rebuildRekapHarianV131_(ss) {
  const sh = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN);
  resetSheetWithHeadersV131_(sh, APJ_REKAP_HARIAN_HEADERS_V131);
  const rows = readTable_(absensiSheet_()).rows;
  const data = rows
    .filter(row => isValidTime_(row['Jam Masuk']) || isValidTime_(row['Jam Pulang']))
    .map(row => {
      const riwayat = recordToRiwayat_(row);
      const tanggalKey = inferAbsensiDateKey_(row) || riwayat.tanggalKey || '';
      const totalLemburJam = number_(row['Total Lembur Jam']);
      return [
        row['ID Absensi'] || '',
        tanggalKey,
        riwayat.tanggal || '',
        row['Username'] || '',
        row['Nama'] || row['Nama Lengkap'] || '',
        row['Outlet'] || '',
        row['Shift'] || '',
        normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Masuk']),
        normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Pulang']),
        normalizeTime_(row['Jam Masuk']),
        normalizeTime_(row['Jam Pulang']),
        row['Status Masuk'] || '',
        row['Status Pulang'] || '',
        normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Terlambat Menit']),
        row['Total Kerja Bersih'] || minutesToDurationText_(normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'])),
        normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit']),
        hoursToTextZeroV131_(totalLemburJam),
        totalLemburJam,
        row['Foto Masuk'] || '',
        row['Foto Pulang'] || '',
        row['Updated At'] || row['Created At'] || ''
      ];
    })
    .sort((a, b) => String(a[1]).localeCompare(String(b[1])) || String(a[4]).localeCompare(String(b[4])));
  if (data.length) sh.getRange(2, 1, data.length, APJ_REKAP_HARIAN_HEADERS_V131.length).setValues(data);
  formatRekapHarianSheetV131_(sh);
  return { rows: data.length };
}

function rebuildRekapBulananV131_(ss) {
  const sh = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN);
  resetSheetWithHeadersV131_(sh, APJ_REKAP_BULANAN_HEADERS_V131);
  const groups = buildMonthlyScheduleGroupsV131_();
  const absRows = readTable_(absensiSheet_()).rows;

  absRows.forEach(row => {
    const tanggalKey = inferAbsensiDateKey_(row);
    if (!tanggalKey) return;
    const dateObj = dateFromKey_(tanggalKey);
    const bulan = monthNameId_(dateObj);
    const tahun = String(dateObj.getFullYear());
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan']);
    const outlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], '');
    if (!nama) return;
    const key = monthlyGroupKeyV131_(nama, bulan, tahun, outlet);
    if (!groups[key]) groups[key] = newMonthlyGroupV131_(nama, bulan, tahun, outlet);
    const g = groups[key];
    const dayKey = tanggalKey;
    if (isValidTime_(row['Jam Masuk']) && !g.hadirDates[dayKey]) {
      g.hadirDates[dayKey] = true;
      g.totalHadir += 1;
    }
    if (normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Terlambat Menit']) > 0 && !g.terlambatDates[dayKey]) {
      g.terlambatDates[dayKey] = true;
      g.totalTerlambat += 1;
    }
    if (isValidTime_(row['Jam Masuk']) && !isValidTime_(row['Jam Pulang']) && !g.tidakCheckoutDates[dayKey]) {
      g.tidakCheckoutDates[dayKey] = true;
      g.tidakCheckout += 1;
    }
    g.totalLemburJam += number_(row['Total Lembur Jam']);
    g.totalJamKerjaMenit += normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit']);
    const upd = row['Updated At'] || row['Created At'] || '';
    if (upd) g.updateTerakhir = upd;
  });

  const data = Object.keys(groups).map(key => {
    const g = groups[key];
    const kerjaSampaiHariIni = Math.max(0, Number(g.totalHari || 0) - Number(g.totalLibur || 0));
    const totalTidakHadir = Math.max(0, kerjaSampaiHariIni - Number(g.totalHadir || 0));
    const status = g.tidakCheckout > 0 ? 'PERLU CEK CHECKOUT' : (totalTidakHadir > 0 ? 'PERLU CEK HADIR' : 'AMAN');
    return [
      g.nama,
      g.bulan,
      g.tahun,
      g.outlet,
      g.totalHari,
      g.totalHadir,
      g.totalTerlambat,
      totalTidakHadir,
      g.totalLibur,
      g.tidakCheckout,
      hoursToTextZeroV131_(g.totalLemburJam),
      Math.round(g.totalLemburJam * 100) / 100,
      minutesToDurationText_(g.totalJamKerjaMenit),
      g.totalJamKerjaMenit,
      status,
      g.updateTerakhir || ''
    ];
  }).sort((a, b) => String(a[2]).localeCompare(String(b[2])) || monthIndexV131_(a[1]) - monthIndexV131_(b[1]) || String(a[0]).localeCompare(String(b[0])));

  if (data.length) sh.getRange(2, 1, data.length, APJ_REKAP_BULANAN_HEADERS_V131.length).setValues(data);
  formatRekapBulananSheetV131_(sh);
  return { rows: data.length };
}

function buildMonthlyScheduleGroupsV131_() {
  const groups = {};
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL);
  if (!sh) return groups;
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  table.rows.forEach(row => {
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama']);
    const outlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']);
    const bulan = firstNonEmpty_(row['Bulan'], row['BULAN']);
    const tahun = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Tahun'], row['TAHUN']) || '').trim();
    if (!nama || !bulan || !tahun) return;
    const key = monthlyGroupKeyV131_(nama, bulan, tahun, outlet);
    const g = groups[key] || newMonthlyGroupV131_(nama, bulan, tahun, outlet);
    const effectiveDays = effectiveDaysInMonthV131_(bulan, tahun);
    for (let d = 1; d <= effectiveDays; d++) {
      const val = firstNonEmpty_(row[String(d)], row[String(d).padStart(2, '0')]);
      if (!val) continue;
      g.totalHari += 1;
      if (normKey_(val) === 'libur') g.totalLibur += 1;
    }
    groups[key] = g;
  });
  return groups;
}

function newMonthlyGroupV131_(nama, bulan, tahun, outlet) {
  return {
    nama: String(nama || '').trim(),
    bulan: String(bulan || '').trim(),
    tahun: String(tahun || '').trim(),
    outlet: String(outlet || '').trim(),
    totalHari: 0,
    totalHadir: 0,
    totalTerlambat: 0,
    totalLibur: 0,
    tidakCheckout: 0,
    totalLemburJam: 0,
    totalJamKerjaMenit: 0,
    updateTerakhir: '',
    hadirDates: {},
    terlambatDates: {},
    tidakCheckoutDates: {}
  };
}

function monthlyGroupKeyV131_(nama, bulan, tahun, outlet) {
  return [normKey_(nama), normKey_(bulan), String(tahun || '').trim(), normKey_(outlet)].join('|');
}

function effectiveDaysInMonthV131_(bulan, tahun) {
  const monthIdx = monthIndexV131_(bulan);
  const y = Number(tahun || 0);
  if (monthIdx < 0 || !y) return 31;
  const days = new Date(y, monthIdx + 1, 0).getDate();
  const now = new Date();
  if (y === now.getFullYear() && monthIdx === now.getMonth()) return Math.min(days, now.getDate());
  const monthStart = new Date(y, monthIdx, 1);
  if (monthStart > now) return 0;
  return days;
}

function monthIndexV131_(bulan) {
  const names = ['januari','februari','maret','april','mei','juni','juli','agustus','september','oktober','november','desember'];
  return names.indexOf(String(bulan || '').trim().toLowerCase());
}

function resetSheetWithHeadersV131_(sh, headers) {
  // V131: jangan reset format/table Google Sheets saat refresh rekap.
  // Error yang pernah muncul: "tidak dapat menetapkan format nomor sel di kolom yang sedang diketik".
  // Jadi refresh hanya menulis header dan membersihkan ISI baris data, bukan format kolom.
  safeSetValuesV131_(sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length), [headers], 'set header ' + sh.getName());
  try { sh.setFrozenRows(1); } catch (err) {}
  clearDataRowsOnlyV131_(sh, headers.length);
}

function clearDataRowsOnlyV131_(sh, colCount) {
  const rowsToClear = Math.max(sh.getMaxRows() - 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 0);
  if (!rowsToClear) return;
  try {
    sh.getRange(2, 1, rowsToClear, Math.max(1, colCount)).clearContent();
  } catch (err) {
    console.log('clearDataRowsOnlyV131_ dilewati untuk ' + sh.getName() + ': ' + errorMessage_(err));
  }
}

function safeSetValuesV131_(range, values, label) {
  try {
    range.setValues(values);
  } catch (err) {
    throw new Error((label || 'setValues') + ' gagal: ' + errorMessage_(err));
  }
}

function safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, headerName, format) {
  const c = headers.indexOf(headerName) + 1;
  if (c <= 0) return false;
  const lastRow = Math.max(sh.getMaxRows(), 2);
  try {
    sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1).setNumberFormat(format);
    return true;
  } catch (err) {
    console.log('Format kolom ' + sh.getName() + '.' + headerName + ' dilewati: ' + errorMessage_(err));
    return false;
  }
}

function formatRekapHarianSheetV131_(sh) {
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  const textHeaders = ['ID Absensi','Tanggal Key','Username','Nama Lengkap','Outlet','Shift','Status Masuk','Status Pulang','Total Kerja','Total Lembur','Foto Masuk','Foto Pulang'];
  const timeHeaders = ['Jadwal Masuk','Jadwal Pulang','Jam Masuk','Jam Pulang'];
  const dateHeaders = ['Tanggal','Update Terakhir'];
  const minuteHeaders = ['Terlambat Menit','Total Kerja Menit'];
  const hourHeaders = ['Total Lembur Jam'];
  textHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, '@'));
  timeHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, 'HH:mm:ss'));
  dateHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss'));
  minuteHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, '0 "Menit"'));
  hourHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, '0.## "Jam"'));
  autoResizeSafeV131_(sh, headers.length);
}

function formatRekapBulananSheetV131_(sh) {
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  const textHeaders = ['Nama Lengkap','Bulan','Outlet','Total Lembur','Total Jam Kerja','Status'];
  const numberHeaders = ['Tahun','Total Hari','Total Hadir','Total Terlambat','Total Tidak Hadir','Total Libur','Tidak Checkout','Total Jam Kerja Menit'];
  const hourHeaders = ['Total Lembur Jam'];
  const dateHeaders = ['Update Terakhir'];
  textHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, '@'));
  numberHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, '0'));
  hourHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, '0.## "Jam"'));
  dateHeaders.forEach(h => safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, h, 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss'));
  autoResizeSafeV131_(sh, headers.length);
}

function autoResizeSafeV131_(sh, cols) {
  try { sh.autoResizeColumns(1, Math.max(1, cols)); } catch (err) {}
}

function hoursToTextZeroV131_(hours) {
  hours = Math.max(0, Number(hours || 0));
  if (!hours) return '0 jam';
  return hoursToText_(hours);
}

// =============================================================================
// V131 Trigger installer & spreadsheet menu
// =============================================================================
function installAbsensiRekapTriggerV131() {
  const deleted = deleteAbsensiRekapTriggerV131(true);
  const created = [];
  const core = coreSS_();
  const hr = hrSS_();

  try {
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('onEditAbsensiRekapV131').forSpreadsheet(core).onEdit().create();
    created.push('onEdit APJ_CORE_USER');
  } catch (err) {
    created.push('GAGAL onEdit APJ_CORE_USER: ' + errorMessage_(err));
  }

  try {
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('onEditAbsensiRekapV131').forSpreadsheet(hr).onEdit().create();
    created.push('onEdit APJ_ABSENSI_KARYAWAN');
  } catch (err) {
    created.push('GAGAL onEdit APJ_ABSENSI_KARYAWAN: ' + errorMessage_(err));
  }

  try {
    ScriptApp.newTrigger('refreshRekapAbsensiV131TimeTrigger').timeBased().everyHours(1).create();
    created.push('time trigger setiap 1 jam');
  } catch (err) {
    created.push('GAGAL time trigger: ' + errorMessage_(err));
  }

  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Trigger rekap Absensi V131 selesai dipasang.',
    deleted: deleted,
    created: created,
    triggers: listAbsensiRekapTriggerV131(),
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function deleteAbsensiRekapTriggerV131(silent) {
  const handlers = ['onEditAbsensiRekapV131', 'refreshRekapAbsensiV131TimeTrigger'];
  const deleted = [];
  ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers().forEach(t => {
    if (handlers.indexOf(t.getHandlerFunction()) >= 0) {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(t);
      deleted.push(t.getHandlerFunction());
    }
  });
  const res = {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Trigger rekap Absensi V131 lama sudah dibersihkan.',
    deleted: deleted,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
  return silent ? deleted : res;
}

function listAbsensiRekapTriggerV131() {
  const list = ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers()
    .filter(t => ['onEditAbsensiRekapV131', 'refreshRekapAbsensiV131TimeTrigger'].indexOf(t.getHandlerFunction()) >= 0)
    .map(t => ({ handler: t.getHandlerFunction(), eventType: String(t.getEventType && t.getEventType() || '') }));
  return { sukses: true, success: true, triggers: list, count: list.length, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function onEditAbsensiRekapV131(e) {
  try {
    const sh = e && e.range && e.range.getSheet ? e.range.getSheet() : null;
    const sheetName = sh ? sh.getName() : '';
    const watched = [
      APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI,
      APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL,
      APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT
    ];
    if (watched.indexOf(sheetName) < 0) return;
    refreshRekapAbsensiV131({ silent: true, trigger: 'onEdit', sheetName: sheetName });
  } catch (err) {
    console.log('onEditAbsensiRekapV131 gagal: ' + errorMessage_(err));
  }
}

function refreshRekapAbsensiV131TimeTrigger() {
  try {
    return refreshRekapAbsensiV131({ silent: true, trigger: 'time' });
  } catch (err) {
    console.log('refreshRekapAbsensiV131TimeTrigger gagal: ' + errorMessage_(err));
  }
}

function onOpen(e) {
  try {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi()
      .createMenu('APJ Absensi')
      .addItem('Refresh Rekap Absensi', 'refreshRekapAbsensiV131')
      .addItem('Pasang Trigger Rekap', 'installAbsensiRekapTriggerV131')
      .addItem('Cek Trigger Rekap', 'listAbsensiRekapTriggerV131')
      .addToUi();
  } catch (err) {}
}

// =============================================================================
// V132 - SETUP FORMAT SAFE FIX
// =============================================================================
// Catatan:
// Google Sheets kadang menolak setNumberFormat/setValues saat user sedang mengetik
// atau sheet memakai fitur Table. V132 membuat setup/repair aman: header tetap dicek,
// format kolom tidak boleh menggagalkan proses, dan rekap tetap bisa refresh.

function safeRangeSetValuesV132_(range, values, label) {
  try {
    range.setValues(values);
    return true;
  } catch (err) {
    console.log((label || 'setValues') + ' dilewati: ' + errorMessage_(err));
    return false;
  }
}

function safeRangeSetNumberFormatV132_(range, format, label) {
  try {
    range.setNumberFormat(format);
    return true;
  } catch (err) {
    console.log((label || 'setNumberFormat') + ' dilewati: ' + errorMessage_(err));
    return false;
  }
}

// Override util lama agar format/header gagal tidak membuat setup/repair berhenti.
function ensureHeaders_(sh, headers) {
  if (!sh) return;
  headers = headers || [];
  if (!headers.length) return;

  let existing = [];
  try { existing = getHeaders_(sh); } catch (err) { existing = []; }

  if (!existing.length || existing.every(h => !h)) {
    safeRangeSetValuesV132_(sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length), [headers], 'header awal ' + sh.getName());
    try { sh.setFrozenRows(1); } catch (err) {}
    return;
  }

  const missing = headers.filter(h => existing.indexOf(h) < 0);
  if (missing.length) {
    safeRangeSetValuesV132_(sh.getRange(1, existing.length + 1, 1, missing.length), [missing], 'header tambahan ' + sh.getName());
  }
  try { sh.setFrozenRows(1); } catch (err) {}
}

function formatAbsensiSheet_(sh) {
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  const lastRow = Math.max(sh.getMaxRows(), 2);
  const textHeaders = ['ID Absensi','Tanggal Key','Username','Level','Shift','Status Masuk','Status Pulang','Device','Catatan','Nama','Outlet','Foto Masuk','Foto Pulang','Total Kerja Bersih'];
  const timeHeaders = ['Jadwal Masuk','Jadwal Pulang','Jam Masuk','Jam Pulang'];
  const dateHeaders = ['Tanggal','Created At','Updated At'];
  const plainNumberHeaders = ['Latitude Masuk','Longitude Masuk','Latitude Pulang','Longitude Pulang','Jarak Masuk','Jarak Pulang','Radius'];
  const minuteHeaders = ['Terlambat Menit','Lembur Awal Menit','Lembur Akhir Menit','Total Lembur Menit','Lembur Awal Aktual Menit','Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit','Total Lembur Aktual Menit','Total Kerja Menit','Istirahat Menit','Total Kerja Bersih Menit'];
  const hourHeaders = ['Lembur Awal Jam','Lembur Akhir Jam','Total Lembur Jam'];

  function fmt(headerName, format) {
    const c = headers.indexOf(headerName) + 1;
    if (c <= 0) return;
    safeRangeSetNumberFormatV132_(sh.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1), format, 'format ' + sh.getName() + '.' + headerName);
  }

  textHeaders.forEach(h => fmt(h, '@'));
  timeHeaders.forEach(h => fmt(h, 'HH:mm:ss'));
  dateHeaders.forEach(h => fmt(h, 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss'));
  plainNumberHeaders.forEach(h => fmt(h, '0.########'));
  minuteHeaders.forEach(h => fmt(h, '0 "Menit"'));
  hourHeaders.forEach(h => fmt(h, '0.## "Jam"'));
}

function resetSheetWithHeadersV131_(sh, headers) {
  // Override V132: jangan gagal jika Google Sheets sedang mengunci format/header.
  safeRangeSetValuesV132_(sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length), [headers], 'set header ' + sh.getName());
  try { sh.setFrozenRows(1); } catch (err) {}
  clearDataRowsOnlyV131_(sh, headers.length);
}

function safeSetValuesV131_(range, values, label) {
  // Untuk data rekap, tetap coba tulis. Kalau gagal, return false agar caller tidak crash.
  return safeRangeSetValuesV132_(range, values, label || 'setValues');
}

function setupAbsensiSheetsV132(showResult) {
  const ss = hrSS_();
  const absensi = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI);
  ensureHeaders_(absensi, APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129);
  formatAbsensiSheet_(absensi);

  const rekapHarian = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN);
  ensureHeaders_(rekapHarian, APJ_REKAP_HARIAN_HEADERS_V131);
  formatRekapHarianSheetV131_(rekapHarian);

  const rekapBulanan = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN);
  ensureHeaders_(rekapBulanan, APJ_REKAP_BULANAN_HEADERS_V131);
  formatRekapBulananSheetV131_(rekapBulanan);

  const legacyHidden = hideLegacyRekapSheetsV129_(ss);
  const rekap = showResult === false ? null : refreshRekapAbsensiV132({ silent: true });
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Setup Absensi V132 selesai. Header/format dibuat safe dan rekap siap trigger otomatis.',
    sheet: ss.getName(),
    legacyHidden: legacyHidden,
    rekap: rekap,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function refreshRekapAbsensiV132(payload) {
  return refreshRekapAbsensiV131(payload || {});
}

function repairAbsensiLegacyRowsV132() {
  setupAbsensiSheetsV132(false);
  const sh = absensiSheet_();
  const values = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (values.length < 2) {
    return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Tidak ada data yang perlu diperbaiki.', repaired: 0, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
  }
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  let repaired = 0;
  for (let r = 2; r <= values.length; r++) {
    const row = rowObjectFromValues_(headers, values[r - 1]);
    const patch = {};
    const username = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['User']);
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan']);
    const keyNow = inferAbsensiDateKey_(row);
    if (!row['Tanggal Key'] && keyNow) patch['Tanggal Key'] = keyNow;
    if (!row['ID Absensi']) patch['ID Absensi'] = makeAbsensiId_(username || nama || 'USER', patch['Tanggal Key'] || inferAbsensiDateKey_(row) || todayKey_());
    if (!row['Jam Masuk'] && isValidTime_(row['Masuk'])) patch['Jam Masuk'] = normalizeTime_(row['Masuk']);
    if (!row['Jam Pulang'] && isValidTime_(row['Pulang'])) patch['Jam Pulang'] = normalizeTime_(row['Pulang']);
    if (!row['Username'] && username) patch['Username'] = username;
    if (!row['Nama'] && nama) patch['Nama'] = nama;

    const rowUser = getUserByUsernameOrName_(username, nama);
    const dateObj = dateFromKey_(keyNow || patch['Tanggal Key'] || todayKey_());
    const jadwal = rowUser ? getJadwalForDate_(rowUser, dateObj, firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], patch['Outlet'])) : defaultJadwal_('User baris lama tidak ditemukan saat repair.');
    const masuk = normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(patch['Jam Masuk'], row['Jam Masuk'], row['Masuk']));
    const pulang = normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(patch['Jam Pulang'], row['Jam Pulang'], row['Pulang']));
    const late = masuk ? calculateLateMinutes_(masuk, jadwal) : normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Terlambat Menit']);
    if (String(row['Terlambat Menit'] || '') !== String(late) || row['Terlambat Menit'] instanceof Date) patch['Terlambat Menit'] = late;

    if (masuk) {
      const workMasuk = calculateWorkMetrics_(masuk, '', jadwal);
      patch['Lembur Awal Menit'] = workMasuk.lemburAwalMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Aktual Menit'] = workMasuk.lemburAwalAktualMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Menit'] = workMasuk.totalLemburMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Aktual Menit'] = workMasuk.totalLemburAktualMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Jam'] = workMasuk.lemburAwalJam;
      patch['Total Lembur Jam'] = workMasuk.totalLemburJam;
      if (!row['Shift'] && jadwal.shift) patch['Shift'] = jadwal.shift;
      if (!row['Jadwal Masuk'] && jadwal.jamMasuk) patch['Jadwal Masuk'] = jadwal.jamMasuk;
      if (!row['Jadwal Pulang'] && jadwal.jamPulang) patch['Jadwal Pulang'] = jadwal.jamPulang;
      patch['Istirahat Menit'] = Number(jadwal.istirahatMenit || 0);
    }

    if (masuk && pulang) {
      const work = calculateWorkMetrics_(masuk, pulang, jadwal);
      patch['Lembur Awal Menit'] = work.lemburAwalMenit;
      patch['Lembur Akhir Menit'] = work.lemburAkhirMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Menit'] = work.totalLemburMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Aktual Menit'] = work.lemburAwalAktualMenit;
      patch['Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit'] = work.lemburAkhirAktualMenit;
      patch['Total Lembur Aktual Menit'] = work.totalLemburAktualMenit;
      patch['Lembur Awal Jam'] = work.lemburAwalJam;
      patch['Lembur Akhir Jam'] = work.lemburAkhirJam;
      patch['Total Lembur Jam'] = work.totalLemburJam;
      patch['Total Kerja Menit'] = work.totalKerjaMenit;
      patch['Istirahat Menit'] = work.istirahatMenit;
      patch['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] = work.totalKerjaBersihMenit;
      patch['Total Kerja Bersih'] = work.totalKerjaBersih;
    }

    if (Object.keys(patch).length) {
      updateRecordByRow_(sh, r, patch);
      repaired++;
    }
  }
  const rekap = refreshRekapAbsensiV132({ silent: true });
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Repair Absensi V132 selesai dan rekap diperbarui.', repaired: repaired, rekap: rekap, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

    coreSpreadsheet: coreSS_().getName(),
    hrSpreadsheet: ss.getName(),

      users: getActiveUsers_().length,

      rekapBulanan: Math.max((ss.getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN) || { getLastRow: function(){ return 1; } }).getLastRow() - 1, 0)
    }
  };
}

// =============================================================================
// V133 - REKAP ABSENSI PAGE DATA + ROLE ACCESS
// =============================================================================
function getRekapAbsensiV133(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(currentUser);
  const isAdmin = isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(currentUser);
  const startKey = inferDateKey_(payload.tanggalAwal || payload.startDate || payload.dari) || firstDayOfMonthKeyV133_();
  const endKey = inferDateKey_(payload.tanggalAkhir || payload.endDate || payload.sampai) || todayKey_();
  const outletFilter = normKey_(payload.outlet || payload.outletFilter || '');
  const statusFilter = normKey_(payload.status || payload.statusFilter || '');
  const userFilterRaw = normText_(payload.userFilter || payload.usernameFilter || payload.namaFilter || '');
  const userFilterKey = normKey_(userFilterRaw);
  const limit = Math.min(Math.max(Number(payload.limit || 1000), 1), 5000);
  const users = getActiveUsers_(true);
  const rows = readTable_(absensiSheet_()).rows;

  let filtered = rows.map(function(row) {
    const tanggalKey = inferAbsensiDateKey_(row);
    if (!tanggalKey) return null;
    const riwayat = recordToRiwayat_(row);
    const username = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['User']);
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan']);
    const statusGabungan = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Status Masuk'], '') + ' ' + firstNonEmpty_(row['Status Pulang'], '')).trim();
    return {
      idAbsensi: row['ID Absensi'] || '',
      tanggalKey: tanggalKey,
      tanggal: riwayat.tanggal || displayDate_(row['Tanggal']),
      username: username || '',
      nama: nama || '',
      level: row['Level'] || '',
      outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], ''),
      shift: row['Shift'] || '',
      jadwalMasuk: normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Masuk']),
      jadwalPulang: normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Pulang']),
      jamMasuk: normalizeTime_(row['Jam Masuk']),
      jamPulang: normalizeTime_(row['Jam Pulang']),
      statusMasuk: row['Status Masuk'] || '',
      statusPulang: row['Status Pulang'] || '',
      status: statusGabungan,
      terlambatMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Terlambat Menit']),
      totalKerjaMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Menit']),
      totalKerjaBersihMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit']),
      totalKerjaBersih: row['Total Kerja Bersih'] || minutesToDurationText_(normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit'])),
      totalLemburJam: number_(row['Total Lembur Jam']),
      totalLemburLabel: hoursToTextZeroV131_(number_(row['Total Lembur Jam'])),
      fotoMasuk: photoValueToUrl_(row['Foto Masuk']),
      fotoPulang: photoValueToUrl_(row['Foto Pulang']),
      updatedAt: row['Updated At'] || row['Created At'] || ''
    };
  }).filter(Boolean).filter(function(r) {
    if (r.tanggalKey < startKey || r.tanggalKey > endKey) return false;
    if (!isAdmin) {
      const uKey = normKey_(currentUser.username);
      const nKey = normKey_(currentUser.nama);
      if (normKey_(r.username) !== uKey && normKey_(r.nama) !== nKey) return false;
    } else if (userFilterKey) {
      if (normKey_(r.username) !== userFilterKey && normKey_(r.nama) !== userFilterKey) return false;
    }
    if (outletFilter && normKey_(r.outlet) !== outletFilter) return false;
    if (statusFilter) {
      const combined = normKey_(String(r.statusMasuk || '') + ' ' + String(r.statusPulang || ''));
      if (statusFilter === 'tidakcheckout') {
        if (!(r.jamMasuk && !r.jamPulang)) return false;
      } else if (combined.indexOf(statusFilter) < 0) return false;
    }
    return true;
  }).sort(function(a,b){
    return String(a.tanggalKey).localeCompare(String(b.tanggalKey)) || String(a.nama).localeCompare(String(b.nama)) || String(a.jamMasuk).localeCompare(String(b.jamMasuk));
  });

  const summary = buildRekapAbsensiSummaryV133_(filtered);
  const shown = filtered.slice(0, limit);
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Rekap Absensi V133 berhasil dimuat.',
    isAdmin: isAdmin,
    scope: isAdmin ? 'ALL' : 'SELF',
    scopeText: isAdmin ? 'Mode admin: semua karyawan' : 'Mode pribadi: data sendiri',
    tanggalAwal: startKey,
    tanggalAkhir: endKey,
    user: publicUser_(currentUser),
    users: isAdmin ? users.map(publicUser_) : [publicUser_(currentUser)],
    outlets: getActiveOutlets_().map(publicOutlet_),
    rows: shown,
    totalRows: filtered.length,
    summary: summary,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(user) {
  const level = String(user && user.level || '').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/\s+/g, '');
  if (isBypassUser_(user)) return true;
  return level === 'SUPERVISOR';
}

function firstDayOfMonthKeyV133_() {
  const d = new Date();
  return formatDate_(new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), 1), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
}

function buildRekapAbsensiSummaryV133_(rows) {
  const hadirDates = {};
  let hadir = 0, terlambat = 0, tidakCheckout = 0, totalLemburJam = 0, totalKerjaMenit = 0;
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    if (r.jamMasuk) hadir += 1;
    if (Number(r.terlambatMenit || 0) > 0) terlambat += 1;
    if (r.jamMasuk && !r.jamPulang) tidakCheckout += 1;
    totalLemburJam += Number(r.totalLemburJam || 0);
    totalKerjaMenit += Number(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || r.totalKerjaMenit || 0);
  });
  return {
    totalRows: (rows || []).length,
    hadir: hadir,
    terlambat: terlambat,
    tidakCheckout: tidakCheckout,
    totalLemburJam: Math.round(totalLemburJam * 100) / 100,
    totalKerjaMenit: Math.round(totalKerjaMenit)
  };
}

// =============================================================================
// V137 - ABSENSI BOOTSTRAP SAFE FORMAT + FALLBACK FIX
// =============================================================================
// Tujuan:
// 1) Bootstrap Absensi tidak boleh gagal hanya karena Google Sheets menolak format kolom.
// 2) Setup/repair/refresh tetap jalan meskipun file sheet sedang terbuka/aktif diketik.
// 3) Error format teknis tidak dikirim ke frontend saat karyawan membuka halaman Absensi.

function safeConsoleV137_(label, err) {
  try { console.log(String(label || 'V137') + ': ' + errorMessage_(err)); } catch (e) {}
}

function safeSetValuesV137_(range, values, label) {
  try {
    range.setValues(values);
    return true;
  } catch (err) {
    safeConsoleV137_(label || 'setValues dilewati', err);
    return false;
  }
}

function ensureHeadersV137_(sh, headers) {
  if (!sh) return false;
  headers = headers || [];
  if (!headers.length) return true;
  let existing = [];
  try { existing = getHeaders_(sh); } catch (err) { existing = []; }
  try {
    if (!existing.length || existing.every(function(h){ return !h; })) {
      safeSetValuesV137_(sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length), [headers], 'header awal ' + sh.getName());
    } else {
      const missing = headers.filter(function(h){ return existing.indexOf(h) < 0; });
      if (missing.length) safeSetValuesV137_(sh.getRange(1, existing.length + 1, 1, missing.length), [missing], 'header tambahan ' + sh.getName());
    }
    try { sh.setFrozenRows(1); } catch (freezeErr) {}
    return true;
  } catch (err) {
    safeConsoleV137_('ensureHeaders ' + sh.getName(), err);
    return false;
  }
}

// Override util global lama supaya seluruh action lama juga aman.
function ensureHeaders_(sh, headers) { return ensureHeadersV137_(sh, headers); }
function formatAbsensiSheet_(sh) { return true; }
function formatRekapHarianSheetV131_(sh) { return true; }
function formatRekapBulananSheetV131_(sh) { return true; }
function safeSetValuesV131_(range, values, label) { return safeSetValuesV137_(range, values, label || 'setValues V131 safe'); }
function safeSetNumberFormatV131_(sh, headers, headerName, format) { return false; }
function safeRangeSetValuesV132_(range, values, label) { return safeSetValuesV137_(range, values, label || 'setValues V132 safe'); }
function safeRangeSetNumberFormatV132_(range, format, label) { return false; }
function safeSetNumberFormatV137_(range, format, label) { return false; }

function resetSheetWithHeadersV131_(sh, headers) {
  ensureHeadersV137_(sh, headers);
  clearDataRowsOnlyV131_(sh, headers.length);
}

function setupAbsensiSheetsV137(showResult) {
  const ss = hrSS_();
  const absensi = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI);
  ensureHeadersV137_(absensi, APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129);

  const rekapHarian = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN);
  ensureHeadersV137_(rekapHarian, APJ_REKAP_HARIAN_HEADERS_V131);

  const rekapBulanan = getOrCreateSheet_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN);
  ensureHeadersV137_(rekapBulanan, APJ_REKAP_BULANAN_HEADERS_V131);

  let legacyHidden = [];
  try { legacyHidden = hideLegacyRekapSheetsV129_(ss); } catch (err) { safeConsoleV137_('hide legacy rekap', err); }

  let rekap = null;
  if (showResult !== false) {
    try { rekap = refreshRekapAbsensiV137({ silent: true }); } catch (err) { rekap = { sukses:false, success:false, pesan:errorMessage_(err) }; }
  }

  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Setup Absensi V137 selesai. Header aman tanpa memaksa format kolom.',
    sheet: ss.getName(),
    legacyHidden: legacyHidden,
    rekap: rekap,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function refreshRekapAbsensiV137(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const res = refreshRekapAbsensiV131(Object.assign({}, payload, { noLock: payload.noLock }));
  return Object.assign({}, res || {}, { pesan: 'Rekap Absensi V137 selesai diperbarui.', version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION });
}
function refreshRekapAbsensiV136(payload) { return refreshRekapAbsensiV137(payload || {}); }
function refreshRekapAbsensiV135(payload) { return refreshRekapAbsensiV137(payload || {}); }
function refreshRekapAbsensiV134(payload) { return refreshRekapAbsensiV137(payload || {}); }
function refreshRekapAbsensiV133(payload) { return refreshRekapAbsensiV137(payload || {}); }
function refreshRekapAbsensiV132(payload) { return refreshRekapAbsensiV137(payload || {}); }
function refreshRekapAbsensiV131(payload) {
  // V137 copy ringan dari refresh lama, memakai helper format-safe yang sudah dioverride.
  payload = payload || {};
  const useLock = payload.noLock !== true;
  const lock = useLock ? LockService.getScriptLock() : null;
  let locked = false;
  try {
    if (lock) {
      locked = lock.tryLock(30000);
      if (!locked) return { sukses:false, success:false, pesan:'Rekap sedang diproses oleh proses lain. Coba lagi beberapa detik.', version:APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
    }
    const ss = hrSS_();
    const harian = rebuildRekapHarianV131_(ss);
    const bulanan = rebuildRekapBulananV131_(ss);
    return { sukses:true, success:true, pesan:'Rekap Absensi V137 selesai diperbarui.', harian:harian, bulanan:bulanan, version:APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
  } finally {
    if (lock && locked) { try { lock.releaseLock(); } catch (err) {} }
  }
}
