// =============================================================================
// V138 - ABSENSI OUTLET ACCESS FROM ID_JADWAL
// =============================================================================
// Prinsip V138:
// USER dipakai untuk identitas/login/role/status aktif.
// ID_JADWAL dipakai untuk jadwal kerja sekaligus akses outlet absensi.
// Jika kolom Outlet di ID_JADWAL bernilai ALL, karyawan boleh absen di outlet aktif mana pun selama masih dalam radius.
// Jika kolom Outlet berisi outlet tertentu, karyawan hanya boleh absen di outlet tersebut.

function getJadwalForDate_(user, dateObj, preferredOutlet) {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL);
  if (!sh) return defaultJadwal_('Jadwal kerja belum tersedia. Hubungi admin.');
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  const day = String(Number(formatDate_(dateObj, 'd')));
  const monthName = monthNameId_(dateObj);
  const year = String(dateObj.getFullYear());
  const nameKey = normKey_(user.nama);
  const preferredKey = normKey_(preferredOutlet || '');

  const candidates = table.rows.filter(row => {
    const rowName = normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], row['NAMA'], row['Nama']));
    const rowMonth = normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Bulan'], row['BULAN']));
    const rowYear = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Tahun'], row['TAHUN']) || '').trim();
    return rowName === nameKey && rowMonth === normKey_(monthName) && rowYear === year;
  });

  if (!candidates.length) return defaultJadwal_('Jadwal kerja bulan ini belum ditemukan. Hubungi admin.');

  let row = candidates[0];
  if (preferredKey) {
    row = candidates.find(r => normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(r['Outlet'], r['OUTLET'])) === preferredKey)
       || candidates.find(r => isAllOutletToken_(firstNonEmpty_(r['Outlet'], r['OUTLET'])))
       || row;
  }

  const jadwalOutlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']) || '';
  const shiftName = firstNonEmpty_(row[day], row[String(day).padStart(2, '0')]);
  if (!shiftName) return defaultJadwal_('Jadwal tanggal ' + day + ' belum diisi. Hubungi admin.');

  if (normKey_(shiftName) === 'libur') {
    return {
      found: true,
      isLibur: true,
      shift: 'LIBUR',
      outlet: jadwalOutlet || preferredOutlet || '',
      jadwalOutlet: jadwalOutlet || '',
      aksesOutletAbsensi: jadwalOutlet || '',
      aksesAbsensiSumber: 'ID_JADWAL',
      jamMasuk: '',
      jamPulang: '',
      toleransiMenit: 0,
      istirahatMenit: 0,
      hitungLemburAwal: true,
      hitungLemburAkhir: false,
      minimalLemburMenit: 60,
      pembulatanLemburMenit: 60,
      metodePembulatanLembur: 'TURUN',
      catatan: 'Hari libur'
    };
  }

  const shift = getShiftByName_(shiftName, jadwalOutlet || preferredOutlet || '');
  if (!shift) {
    return {
      found: true,
      isLibur: false,
      shift: shiftName,
      outlet: jadwalOutlet || '',
      jadwalOutlet: jadwalOutlet || '',
      aksesOutletAbsensi: jadwalOutlet || '',
      aksesAbsensiSumber: 'ID_JADWAL',
      jamMasuk: '',
      jamPulang: '',
      toleransiMenit: 0,
      istirahatMenit: 0,
      hitungLemburAwal: true,
      hitungLemburAkhir: false,
      minimalLemburMenit: 60,
      pembulatanLemburMenit: 60,
      metodePembulatanLembur: 'TURUN',
      catatan: 'Shift belum tersedia. Hubungi admin.'
    };
  }

  return {
    found: true,
    isLibur: false,
    shift: shift.namaShift,
    outlet: shift.outlet || jadwalOutlet || preferredOutlet || '',
    jadwalOutlet: jadwalOutlet || '',
    aksesOutletAbsensi: jadwalOutlet || shift.outlet || '',
    aksesAbsensiSumber: 'ID_JADWAL',
    jamMasuk: shift.jamMasuk,
    jamPulang: shift.jamPulang,
    toleransiMenit: shift.toleransiMenit,
    istirahatMenit: shift.istirahatMenit,
    hitungLemburAwal: shift.hitungLemburAwal,
    hitungLemburAkhir: shift.hitungLemburAkhir,
    minimalLemburMenit: shift.minimalLemburMenit,
    pembulatanLemburMenit: shift.pembulatanLemburMenit,
    metodePembulatanLembur: shift.metodePembulatanLembur,
    catatan: ''
  };
}

function getShiftByName_(shiftName, outlet) {
  const sh = coreSS_().getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT);
  if (!sh) return null;
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  const shiftKey = normKey_(shiftName);
  const outletKey = normKey_(outlet);
  const rows = table.rows.map(row => ({
    namaShift: firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Shift'], row['Shift'], row['SHIFT']),
    outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']),
    jamMasuk: normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Masuk'], row['Masuk'])),
    jamPulang: normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Pulang'], row['Pulang'])),
    toleransiMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Toleransi Keterlambatan'], row['Tolerasi Keterlambatan'], row['Toleransi'], row['Telat'])),
    istirahatMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Istirahat'], row['Break'])),
    hitungLemburAwal: parseBool_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Hitung Lembur Awal'], row['Lembur Awal'], row['Auto Lembur Awal']), true),
    hitungLemburAkhir: parseBool_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Hitung Lembur Akhir'], row['Lembur Akhir'], row['Auto Lembur Akhir']), false),
    minimalLemburMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Minimal Lembur Menit'], row['Minimal Lembur'], row['Minimum Lembur'])) || 60,
    pembulatanLemburMenit: parseDurationMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Pembulatan Lembur Menit'], row['Pembulatan Lembur'], row['Kelipatan Lembur'])) || 60,
    metodePembulatanLembur: String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Metode Pembulatan Lembur'], row['Metode Lembur'], row['Pembulatan']) || 'TURUN').trim().toUpperCase()
  })).filter(s => normKey_(s.namaShift) === shiftKey);
  if (!rows.length) return null;
  if (outletKey) {
    return rows.find(s => normKey_(s.outlet) === outletKey)
        || rows.find(s => isAllOutletToken_(s.outlet))
        || rows[0];
  }
  return rows[0];
}

function defaultJadwal_(catatan) {
  return {
    found: false,
    isLibur: false,
    shift: '',
    outlet: '',
    jadwalOutlet: '',
    aksesOutletAbsensi: '',
    aksesAbsensiSumber: 'ID_JADWAL',
    jamMasuk: '',
    jamPulang: '',
    toleransiMenit: 0,
    istirahatMenit: 0,
    hitungLemburAwal: true,
    hitungLemburAkhir: false,
    minimalLemburMenit: 60,
    pembulatanLemburMenit: 60,
    metodePembulatanLembur: 'TURUN',
    catatan: catatan || ''
  };
}

function isAllOutletToken_(value) {
  const key = normKey_(value);
  return key === 'all' || key === 'semua' || key === 'semuaoutlet' || key === 'semua outlet';
}

function jadwalOutletTokens_(jadwal) {
  const raw = firstNonEmpty_(jadwal && jadwal.aksesOutletAbsensi, jadwal && jadwal.jadwalOutlet, jadwal && jadwal.outlet);
  return String(raw || '').split(/[;,|]/).map(normKey_).filter(Boolean);
}

function jadwalHasOutletAccess_(jadwal, outlet) {
  if (!jadwal || !jadwal.found) return false;
  const tokens = jadwalOutletTokens_(jadwal);
  if (!tokens.length) return false;
  if (tokens.some(isAllOutletToken_)) return true;
  const aliases = [outlet && outlet.namaOutlet, outlet && outlet.kodeOutlet].map(normKey_).filter(Boolean);
  return tokens.some(t => aliases.indexOf(t) >= 0);
}

function validateUserOutletRadius_(user, outlet, lat, lng, mode, jadwal) {
  if (!outlet) throw new Error('Outlet tidak ditemukan.');
  const jarak = Math.round(distanceMeters_(lat, lng, outlet.latitude, outlet.longitude));
  const radius = Number(outlet.radius || 300);
  const bypass = isBypassUser_(user);
  if (bypass) return { ok: true, bypass: true, reason: user.level || user.username, jarak: jarak, radius: radius };
  if (!jadwalHasOutletAccess_(jadwal, outlet)) {
    const akses = jadwalOutletTokens_(jadwal).join(', ') || '-';
    throw new Error('Outlet tidak sesuai jadwal absensi. Jadwal: ' + akses + ', Outlet GPS: ' + outlet.namaOutlet + '.');
  }
  if (jarak > radius) throw new Error('Di luar radius outlet ' + outlet.namaOutlet + '. Jarak: ' + jarak + ' meter, Radius: ' + radius + ' meter.');
  return { ok: true, bypass: false, reason: '', jarak: jarak, radius: radius };
}

function checkin(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV138(false);
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(user);

  const existing = findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, todayKey_());
  if (existing && isValidTime_(existing.record['Jam Masuk'])) {
    const data = recordToRiwayat_(existing.record);
    data.jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, existing.record['Outlet']);
    return { sukses: false, success: false, already: true, pesan: 'Sudah Check In hari ini.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true };
  }

  const lat = number_(payload.latitude || payload.lat);
  const lng = number_(payload.longitude || payload.lng || payload.lon);
  if (!lat || !lng) throw new Error('GPS belum terbaca. Refresh lokasi terlebih dahulu.');

  const outlets = getActiveOutlets_();
  const outlet = nearestOutlet_(lat, lng, outlets);
  if (!outlet) throw new Error('Data outlet aktif tidak ditemukan.');

  const jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, outlet.namaOutlet);
  const validation = validateUserOutletRadius_(user, outlet, lat, lng, 'MASUK', jadwal);
  const now = new Date();
  const jamMasuk = formatDate_(now, 'HH:mm:ss');
  const tanggal = formatDate_(now, 'dd/MM/yyyy');
  const dateKey = formatDate_(now, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const terlambat = calculateLateMinutes_(jamMasuk, jadwal);
  const overtime = calculateWorkMetrics_(jamMasuk, '', jadwal);
  const statusMasuk = getStatusMasuk_(jadwal, terlambat);
  const fotoUrl = savePhoto_(payload.foto, user.username + '_CheckIn_' + dateKey + '_' + compactTime_(jamMasuk) + '.jpg');

  const record = {
    'ID Absensi': makeAbsensiId_(user.username, dateKey),
    'Tanggal Key': dateKey,
    'Username': user.username,
    'Level': user.level,
    'Shift': jadwal.shift || '',
    'Jadwal Masuk': jadwal.jamMasuk || '',
    'Jadwal Pulang': jadwal.jamPulang || '',
    'Status Masuk': statusMasuk,
    'Status Pulang': '',
    'Latitude Masuk': lat,
    'Longitude Masuk': lng,
    'Latitude Pulang': '',
    'Longitude Pulang': '',
    'Jarak Masuk': validation.jarak,
    'Jarak Pulang': '',
    'Radius': validation.radius,
    'Device': String(payload.device || ''),
    'Catatan': validation.bypass ? 'Bypass radius: ' + validation.reason : 'Akses outlet dari jadwal absensi',
    'Created At': now,
    'Updated At': now,
    'Tanggal': tanggal,
    'Nama': user.nama,
    'Outlet': outlet.namaOutlet,
    'Jam Masuk': jamMasuk,
    'Jam Pulang': '',
    'Foto Masuk': makePhotoLinkFormula_(fotoUrl, 'Foto Cek In'),
    'Foto Pulang': '',
    'Terlambat Menit': terlambat,
    'Lembur Awal Menit': overtime.lemburAwalMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Menit': 0,
    'Total Lembur Menit': overtime.totalLemburMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Aktual Menit': overtime.lemburAwalAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit': 0,
    'Total Lembur Aktual Menit': overtime.totalLemburAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Jam': overtime.lemburAwalJam,
    'Lembur Akhir Jam': 0,
    'Total Lembur Jam': overtime.totalLemburJam,
    'Total Kerja Menit': 0,
    'Istirahat Menit': Number(jadwal.istirahatMenit || 0),
    'Total Kerja Bersih Menit': 0,
    'Total Kerja Bersih': ''
  };

  if (existing) updateRecordByRow_(absensiSheet_(), existing.row, record);
  else appendRecord_(absensiSheet_(), APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129, record);
  try { refreshRekapAbsensiV138({ silent: true }); } catch (rekapErr) { console.log('Refresh rekap V138 gagal: ' + errorMessage_(rekapErr)); }

  const data = recordToRiwayat_(record);
  data.fotoMasuk = fotoUrl;
  data.jadwal = jadwal;
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Check In berhasil.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function checkout(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV138(false);
  const user = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(user);

  const found = findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, todayKey_());
  if (!found || !isValidTime_(found.record['Jam Masuk'])) throw new Error('Data Check In hari ini belum ditemukan.');
  if (isValidTime_(found.record['Jam Pulang'])) {
    const data = recordToRiwayat_(found.record);
    data.jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, found.record['Outlet']);
    return { sukses: false, success: false, already: true, pesan: 'Sudah Check Out hari ini.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true };
  }

  const lat = number_(payload.latitude || payload.lat);
  const lng = number_(payload.longitude || payload.lng || payload.lon);
  if (!lat || !lng) throw new Error('GPS belum terbaca. Refresh lokasi terlebih dahulu.');

  const outletName = found.record['Outlet'];
  const outlet = getOutletByName_(outletName) || nearestOutlet_(lat, lng, getActiveOutlets_());
  const jadwal = getTodayJadwalForUser_(user, outletName);
  const validation = validateUserOutletRadius_(user, outlet, lat, lng, 'PULANG', jadwal);
  const now = new Date();
  const jamPulang = formatDate_(now, 'HH:mm:ss');
  const fotoUrl = savePhoto_(payload.foto, user.username + '_CheckOut_' + todayKey_() + '_' + compactTime_(jamPulang) + '.jpg');
  const statusPulang = getStatusPulang_(jamPulang, jadwal);
  const work = calculateWorkMetrics_(found.record['Jam Masuk'], jamPulang, jadwal);

  const patch = {
    'Status Pulang': statusPulang,
    'Latitude Pulang': lat,
    'Longitude Pulang': lng,
    'Jarak Pulang': validation.jarak,
    'Jam Pulang': jamPulang,
    'Foto Pulang': makePhotoLinkFormula_(fotoUrl, 'Foto Cek Out'),
    'Updated At': now,
    'Lembur Awal Menit': work.lemburAwalMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Menit': work.lemburAkhirMenit,
    'Total Lembur Menit': work.totalLemburMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Aktual Menit': work.lemburAwalAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Akhir Aktual Menit': work.lemburAkhirAktualMenit,
    'Total Lembur Aktual Menit': work.totalLemburAktualMenit,
    'Lembur Awal Jam': work.lemburAwalJam,
    'Lembur Akhir Jam': work.lemburAkhirJam,
    'Total Lembur Jam': work.totalLemburJam,
    'Total Kerja Menit': work.totalKerjaMenit,
    'Istirahat Menit': work.istirahatMenit,
    'Total Kerja Bersih Menit': work.totalKerjaBersihMenit,
    'Total Kerja Bersih': work.totalKerjaBersih
  };
  updateRecordByRow_(absensiSheet_(), found.row, patch);
  try { refreshRekapAbsensiV138({ silent: true }); } catch (rekapErr) { console.log('Refresh rekap V138 gagal: ' + errorMessage_(rekapErr)); }

  const updated = Object.assign({}, found.record, patch);
  const data = recordToRiwayat_(updated);
  data.fotoPulang = fotoUrl;
  data.jadwal = jadwal;
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Check Out berhasil.', riwayat: data, data: data, exists: true, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function repairFotoAbsensiLinkV141() {
  const sh = absensiSheet_();
  ensureHeaders_(sh, APJ_ABSENSI_HEADERS_V129);
  const headers = getHeaders_(sh);
  const colMasuk = headers.indexOf('Foto Masuk') + 1;
  const colPulang = headers.indexOf('Foto Pulang') + 1;
  const lastRow = sh.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return { sukses: true, success: true, repaired: 0, pesan: 'Tidak ada data foto untuk diperbaiki.' };
  let repaired = 0;
  function repairCol(col, label) {
    if (col <= 0) return;
    const range = sh.getRange(2, col, lastRow - 1, 1);
    const values = range.getValues();
    const formulas = range.getFormulas();
    for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
      const raw = formulas[i][0] || values[i][0];
      const url = photoValueToUrl_(raw);
      if (/^https?:\/\//i.test(url)) {
        const formula = makePhotoLinkFormula_(url, label);
        if (formulas[i][0] !== formula) {
          sh.getRange(i + 2, col).setFormula(formula);
          repaired++;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  repairCol(colMasuk, 'Foto Cek In');
  repairCol(colPulang, 'Foto Cek Out');
  try { refreshRekapAbsensiV141({ silent: true }); } catch (err) {}
  return { sukses: true, success: true, repaired: repaired, pesan: 'Perbaikan foto hyperlink V141 selesai.', version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function hapusImportLegacyTriggersV141() {
  const handlers = [
    'continueImportAbsensiLegacyJuniBatchV140',
    'continueImportAbsensiLegacyJuniBatchV139',
    'startImportAbsensiLegacyJuniBatchV140'
  ];
  const deleted = [];
  ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers().forEach(function(t) {
    const h = t.getHandlerFunction && t.getHandlerFunction();
    if (handlers.indexOf(h) >= 0) {
      ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(t);
      deleted.push(h);
    }
  });
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Trigger import legacy sudah dibersihkan.', deleted: deleted, version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function exportRekapAbsensiPdfV142(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV141(false);
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(currentUser);
  const isAdmin = isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(currentUser);
  let userFilter = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.userFilter, payload.usernameFilter, payload.karyawan, payload.usernameExport));
  if (!isAdmin) userFilter = currentUser.username || currentUser.nama;
  if (!userFilter) throw new Error('Pilih karyawan terlebih dahulu sebelum export PDF.');

  const ctx = buildAbsensiExportContextV142_(payload, currentUser, { exportAll: false, userFilter: userFilter });
  if (!ctx.groups.length) throw new Error('Data absensi karyawan pada periode tersebut belum ada.');
  const file = createAbsensiPdfFileV142_(ctx.groups[0], ctx);
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Export PDF Absensi berhasil dibuat.',
    file: file,
    files: [file],
    folderName: ctx.folderName,
    folderUrl: ctx.folder.getUrl(),
    periode: ctx.periodLabel,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function exportSemuaRekapAbsensiPdfV142(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV141(false);
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(currentUser);
  if (!isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(currentUser)) throw new Error('Export semua karyawan hanya dapat dilakukan oleh Owner, SuperAdmin, atau Supervisor.');

  const ctx = buildAbsensiExportContextV142_(payload, currentUser, { exportAll: true });
  if (!ctx.groups.length) throw new Error('Tidak ada data absensi pada periode tersebut untuk diexport.');
  const files = [];
  ctx.groups.forEach(function(group) {
    files.push(createAbsensiPdfFileV142_(group, ctx));
  });
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Export PDF semua karyawan selesai. Total file: ' + files.length + '.',
    files: files,
    count: files.length,
    folderName: ctx.folderName,
    folderUrl: ctx.folder.getUrl(),
    periode: ctx.periodLabel,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function buildAbsensiExportContextV142_(payload, currentUser, options) {
  payload = payload || {};
  options = options || {};
  const isAdmin = isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(currentUser);
  let startKey = inferDateKey_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.tanggalAwal, payload.startDate, payload.dari)) || firstDayOfMonthKeyV133_();
  let endKey = inferDateKey_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.tanggalAkhir, payload.endDate, payload.sampai)) || todayKey_();
  if (startKey > endKey) { const tmp = startKey; startKey = endKey; endKey = tmp; }
  const outletFilter = normKey_(payload.outlet || payload.outletFilter || '');
  const statusFilter = normKey_(payload.status || payload.statusFilter || '');
  const userFilterKey = normKey_(options.userFilter || payload.userFilter || payload.usernameFilter || '');
  const rows = readTable_(absensiSheet_()).rows.map(function(row) {
    return rekapRowForExportV142_(row);
  }).filter(Boolean).filter(function(r) {
    if (r.tanggalKey < startKey || r.tanggalKey > endKey) return false;
    if (!isAdmin) {
      const uKey = normKey_(currentUser.username);
      const nKey = normKey_(currentUser.nama);
      if (normKey_(r.username) !== uKey && normKey_(r.nama) !== nKey) return false;
    }
    if (!options.exportAll && userFilterKey) {
      if (normKey_(r.username) !== userFilterKey && normKey_(r.nama) !== userFilterKey) return false;
    }
    if (outletFilter && normKey_(r.outlet) !== outletFilter) return false;
    if (statusFilter) {
      const combined = normKey_(String(r.statusMasuk || '') + ' ' + String(r.statusPulang || ''));
      if (statusFilter === 'tidakcheckout') {
        if (!(r.jamMasuk && !r.jamPulang)) return false;
      } else if (combined.indexOf(statusFilter) < 0) return false;
    }
    return true;
  }).sort(function(a, b) {
    return String(a.nama).localeCompare(String(b.nama)) || String(a.tanggalKey).localeCompare(String(b.tanggalKey));
  });

  const grouped = {};
  rows.forEach(function(r) {
    const key = normKey_(r.username || r.nama || 'user');
    if (!grouped[key]) grouped[key] = { username: r.username, nama: r.nama || r.username || 'Karyawan', outlet: r.outlet || '', rows: [] };
    grouped[key].rows.push(r);
  });
  const groups = Object.keys(grouped).map(function(k){ return grouped[k]; }).sort(function(a,b){ return String(a.nama).localeCompare(String(b.nama)); });
  const periodLabel = periodLabelV142_(startKey, endKey);
  const folderName = periodLabel;
  const root = DriveApp.getFolderById(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.ABSENSI_EXPORT_FOLDER_ID);
  const folder = getOrCreateFolder_(root, folderName);
  return { currentUser: currentUser, startKey: startKey, endKey: endKey, periodLabel: periodLabel, folderName: folderName, folder: folder, rows: rows, groups: groups, outletFilter: outletFilter, statusFilter: statusFilter };
}

function rekapRowForExportV142_(row) {
  const tanggalKey = inferAbsensiDateKey_(row);
  if (!tanggalKey) return null;
  const riwayat = recordToRiwayat_(row);
  const username = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['User']);
  const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan']);
  return {
    idAbsensi: row['ID Absensi'] || '',
    tanggalKey: tanggalKey,
    tanggal: riwayat.tanggal || displayDate_(row['Tanggal']),
    username: username || '',
    nama: nama || '',
    outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], ''),
    shift: row['Shift'] || '',
    jadwalMasuk: normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Masuk']),
    jadwalPulang: normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Pulang']),
    jamMasuk: normalizeTime_(row['Jam Masuk']),
    jamPulang: normalizeTime_(row['Jam Pulang']),
    statusMasuk: row['Status Masuk'] || '',
    statusPulang: row['Status Pulang'] || '',
    status: String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Status Masuk'], '') + ' ' + firstNonEmpty_(row['Status Pulang'], '')).trim(),
    terlambatMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Terlambat Menit']),
    totalKerjaBersihMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit']),
    totalKerjaBersih: row['Total Kerja Bersih'] || minutesToDurationText_(normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit'])),
    totalLemburJam: number_(row['Total Lembur Jam']),
    totalLemburLabel: hoursToTextZeroV131_(number_(row['Total Lembur Jam']))
  };
}

function createAbsensiPdfFileV142_(group, ctx) {
  const summary = buildExportGroupSummaryV142_(group.rows);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  deleteExistingFileByNameV142_(ctx.folder, fileName);
  const html = buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV142_(group, ctx, summary);
  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(html, 'text/html', fileName.replace(/\.pdf$/i, '.html')).getAs(MimeType.PDF).setName(fileName);
  const file = ctx.folder.createFile(blob);
  return {
    nama: group.nama,
    username: group.username || '',
    rows: group.rows.length,
    fileName: fileName,
    fileId: file.getId(),
    url: file.getUrl()
  };
}

function buildExportGroupSummaryV142_(rows) {
  let hadir = 0, terlambat = 0, tidakCheckout = 0, totalLemburJam = 0, totalKerjaMenit = 0;
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    if (r.jamMasuk) hadir++;
    if (Number(r.terlambatMenit || 0) > 0) terlambat++;
    if (r.jamMasuk && !r.jamPulang) tidakCheckout++;
    totalLemburJam += Number(r.totalLemburJam || 0);
    totalKerjaMenit += Number(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0);
  });
  return { totalRows: (rows || []).length, hadir: hadir, terlambat: terlambat, tidakCheckout: tidakCheckout, totalLemburJam: Math.round(totalLemburJam * 100) / 100, totalKerjaMenit: totalKerjaMenit };
}

function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV142_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const status = combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.outlet || '-') + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.shift || '-') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '-') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '-') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '-') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '-') + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="right">' + htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0)) + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="right">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0)) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="12" class="empty">Tidak ada data absensi pada periode ini.</td></tr>';
  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 landscape;margin:12mm;}body{font-family:Arial,sans-serif;color:#0f172a;font-size:10px;}h1{font-size:20px;margin:0 0 4px;}h2{font-size:14px;margin:0;color:#334155}.head{display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;border-bottom:2px solid #0f172a;padding-bottom:10px;margin-bottom:12px}.brand{font-weight:900;letter-spacing:.08em;color:#0f172a}.muted{color:#64748b}.meta{font-size:10px;line-height:1.5;text-align:right}.info{display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:8px;margin:10px 0 12px}.card{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:10px;padding:8px;background:#f8fafc}.card small{display:block;color:#64748b;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:8px;letter-spacing:.06em}.card strong{display:block;font-size:13px;margin-top:3px}.employee{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:10px;padding:9px 10px;margin-bottom:10px}.employee b{font-size:13px}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;}th,td{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;padding:5px 5px;vertical-align:middle;}th{background:#e2e8f0;font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.04em;}td{font-size:9px}.center{text-align:center}.right{text-align:right}.empty{text-align:center;padding:18px;color:#64748b}.foot{margin-top:12px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;color:#64748b;font-size:9px}.sign{margin-top:24px;display:flex;justify-content:flex-end}.signbox{width:190px;text-align:center}.signline{border-bottom:1px solid #0f172a;height:38px;margin-bottom:5px}' +
    '</style></head><body>' +
    '<div class="head"><div><div class="brand">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><h1>Rekap Absensi Karyawan</h1><h2>Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</h2></div><div class="meta"><b>Dibuat</b><br>' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '<br><span class="muted">Sistem APJ HR Absensi</span></div></div>' +
    '<div class="employee"><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.nama || '-') + '</b><br><span class="muted">Username: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.username || '-') + ' • Tanggal: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.startKey)) + ' s/d ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.endKey)) + '</span></div>' +
    '<div class="info"><div class="card"><small>Total Data</small><strong>' + summary.totalRows + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Hadir</small><strong>' + summary.hadir + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Terlambat</small><strong>' + summary.terlambat + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Tidak Checkout</small><strong>' + summary.tidakCheckout + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Total Lembur</small><strong>' + htmlEscapeV142_(hoursToTextZeroV131_(summary.totalLemburJam)) + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Total Kerja</small><strong>' + htmlEscapeV142_(minutesToDurationText_(summary.totalKerjaMenit)) + '</strong></div></div>' +
    '<table><thead><tr><th>No</th><th>Tanggal</th><th>Outlet</th><th>Shift</th><th>Jadwal Masuk</th><th>Jadwal Pulang</th><th>Masuk</th><th>Pulang</th><th>Status</th><th>Terlambat<br>(Menit)</th><th>Total Kerja</th><th>Lembur</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rowsHtml + '</tbody></table>' +
    '<div class="foot"><span>Dokumen dibuat otomatis oleh APJ HR Absensi.</span><span>File: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf')) + '</span></div>' +
    '<div class="sign"><div class="signbox"><div>Mengetahui,</div><div class="signline"></div><div>Owner / Supervisor</div></div></div>' +
    '</body></html>';
}

function combinedStatusTextV142_(row) {
  const a = row.statusMasuk || '';
  const b = row.statusPulang || '';
  if (a && b) return a + ' / ' + b;
  return a || b || row.status || '-';
}

function periodLabelV142_(startKey, endKey) {
  const start = dateFromKey_(startKey);
  const end = dateFromKey_(endKey);
  const startLabel = monthNameId_(start) + ' ' + start.getFullYear();
  const endLabel = monthNameId_(end) + ' ' + end.getFullYear();
  return startLabel === endLabel ? startLabel : startLabel + ' - ' + endLabel;
}

function displayDateKeyV142_(key) {
  return formatDate_(dateFromKey_(key), 'dd/MM/yyyy');
}

function safeFileNameV142_(name) {
  return String(name || 'Absensi.pdf').replace(/[\\/:*?"<>|]+/g, ' ').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
}

function htmlEscapeV142_(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value).replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(c) {
    return ({ '&':'&amp;', '<':'&lt;', '>':'&gt;', '"':'&quot;', "'":'&#39;' })[c];
  });
}

function deleteExistingFileByNameV142_(folder, fileName) {
  try {
    const files = folder.getFilesByName(fileName);
    while (files.hasNext()) files.next().setTrashed(true);
  } catch (err) {}
}


// =============================================================================
// V143 - REKAP ABSENSI EXPORT PDF TEMPLATE KOSONG
// =============================================================================
// Perubahan V143:
// 1) Export PDF satu karyawan tetap membuat file meskipun periode belum ada data.
// 2) Export Semua membuat PDF untuk semua karyawan aktif, termasuk yang belum punya data.
// 3) PDF kosong menampilkan template tanggal, shift/jadwal bila tersedia, dan kolom absensi kosong.

function setupAbsensiSheetsV143(showResult) {
  const res = setupAbsensiSheetsV142(showResult);
  return Object.assign({}, res || {}, {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Setup Absensi V143 selesai. Export PDF tetap membuat template kosong bila data belum ada.',
    exportFolderId: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.ABSENSI_EXPORT_FOLDER_ID,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  });
}

function repairAbsensiLegacyRowsV143() {
  const res = repairAbsensiLegacyRowsV142();
  return Object.assign({}, res || {}, { pesan: 'Repair Absensi V143 selesai.', version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION });
}

function refreshRekapAbsensiV143(payload) {
  const res = refreshRekapAbsensiV142(payload || {});
  return Object.assign({}, res || {}, { pesan: 'Rekap Absensi V143 selesai diperbarui.', version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION });
}

function cekAbsensiConfigV143(payload) { return cekAbsensiConfigV142(payload || {}); }
function debugAbsensiV143(payload) { return debugAbsensiV142(payload || {}); }
function cekJadwalShiftV143(payload) { return cekJadwalShiftV142(payload || {}); }
function installAbsensiRekapTriggerV143() { return installAbsensiRekapTriggerV142(); }
function listAbsensiRekapTriggerV143() { return listAbsensiRekapTriggerV142(); }
function hapusAbsensiRekapTriggerV143() { return hapusAbsensiRekapTriggerV142(); }
function deleteAbsensiRekapTriggerV143() { return hapusAbsensiRekapTriggerV143(); }

function exportRekapAbsensiPdfV143(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV142(false);
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(currentUser);
  const isAdmin = isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(currentUser);
  let userFilter = normText_(firstNonEmpty_(payload.userFilter, payload.usernameFilter, payload.karyawan, payload.usernameExport));
  if (!isAdmin) userFilter = currentUser.username || currentUser.nama;
  if (!userFilter) throw new Error('Pilih karyawan terlebih dahulu sebelum export PDF.');

  const ctx = buildAbsensiExportContextV142_(payload, currentUser, { exportAll: false, userFilter: userFilter });
  let group = ctx.groups[0] || null;
  let isTemplate = false;
  if (!group) {
    const user = isAdmin ? findExportUserV143_(userFilter) : currentUser;
    if (!user) throw new Error('Karyawan tidak ditemukan di USER: ' + userFilter);
    group = buildEmptyExportGroupV143_(user, ctx);
    isTemplate = true;
  }
  const file = createAbsensiPdfFileV143_(group, ctx);
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: isTemplate ? 'Export PDF template kosong berhasil dibuat.' : 'Export PDF Absensi berhasil dibuat.',
    file: file,
    files: [file],
    templateKosong: isTemplate,
    folderName: ctx.folderName,
    folderUrl: ctx.folder.getUrl(),
    periode: ctx.periodLabel,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

function exportSemuaRekapAbsensiPdfV143(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  setupAbsensiSheetsV142(false);
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(currentUser);
  if (!isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(currentUser)) throw new Error('Export semua karyawan hanya dapat dilakukan oleh Owner, SuperAdmin, atau Supervisor.');

  const ctx = buildAbsensiExportContextV142_(payload, currentUser, { exportAll: true });
  const groups = completeExportGroupsForAllUsersV143_(ctx.groups, ctx);
  if (!groups.length) throw new Error('Data karyawan aktif belum ditemukan untuk dibuatkan PDF.');
  const files = [];
  let templateCount = 0;
  groups.forEach(function(group) {
    if (group.templateKosong) templateCount++;
    files.push(createAbsensiPdfFileV143_(group, ctx));
  });
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Export PDF semua karyawan selesai. Total file: ' + files.length + (templateCount ? ', template kosong: ' + templateCount + '.' : '.'),
    files: files,
    count: files.length,
    templateKosong: templateCount,
    folderName: ctx.folderName,
    folderUrl: ctx.folder.getUrl(),
    periode: ctx.periodLabel,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}

// Backward-compatible override: tombol lama/action V142 otomatis memakai perilaku V143.
function exportRekapAbsensiPdfV142(payload) { return exportRekapAbsensiPdfV143(payload || {}); }
function exportSemuaRekapAbsensiPdfV142(payload) { return exportSemuaRekapAbsensiPdfV143(payload || {}); }

function findExportUserV143_(userFilter) {
  const key = normKey_(userFilter);
  if (!key) return null;
  const users = getActiveUsers_(true);
  return users.find(function(u) {
    return normKey_(u.username) === key || normKey_(u.nama) === key;
  }) || null;
}

function completeExportGroupsForAllUsersV143_(groups, ctx) {
  const list = (groups || []).slice();
  const existing = {};
  list.forEach(function(g) {
    existing[normKey_(g.username || g.nama)] = true;
  });
  getActiveUsers_().forEach(function(u) {
    const key = normKey_(u.username || u.nama);
    if (!key || existing[key]) return;
    list.push(buildEmptyExportGroupV143_(u, ctx));
    existing[key] = true;
  });
  return list.sort(function(a, b) { return String(a.nama).localeCompare(String(b.nama)); });
}

function buildEmptyExportGroupV143_(user, ctx) {
  return {
    username: user.username || '',
    nama: user.nama || user.username || 'Karyawan',
    outlet: user.outletUtama || '',
    rows: buildEmptyExportRowsV143_(user, ctx),
    templateKosong: true
  };
}

function buildEmptyExportRowsV143_(user, ctx) {
  const rows = [];
  let d = dateFromKey_(ctx.startKey);
  const end = dateFromKey_(ctx.endKey);
  let guard = 0;
  while (d <= end && guard < 370) {
    const key = formatDate_(d, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    let jadwal = null;
    try { jadwal = getJadwalForDate_(user, d, user.outletUtama || ''); } catch (err) { jadwal = defaultJadwal_(''); }
    rows.push({
      idAbsensi: '',
      tanggalKey: key,
      tanggal: formatDate_(d, 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
      username: user.username || '',
      nama: user.nama || user.username || 'Karyawan',
      outlet: exportRowOutletFromJadwalV143_(jadwal, user),
      shift: jadwal && jadwal.shift ? jadwal.shift : '',
      jadwalMasuk: jadwal && jadwal.jamMasuk ? jadwal.jamMasuk : '',
      jadwalPulang: jadwal && jadwal.jamPulang ? jadwal.jamPulang : '',
      jamMasuk: '',
      jamPulang: '',
      statusMasuk: '',
      statusPulang: '',
      status: '',
      terlambatMenit: '',
      totalKerjaBersihMenit: 0,
      totalKerjaBersih: '',
      totalLemburJam: 0,
      totalLemburLabel: '',
      isTemplate: true
    });
    d = new Date(d.getFullYear(), d.getMonth(), d.getDate() + 1);
    guard++;
  }
  return rows;
}

function exportRowOutletFromJadwalV143_(jadwal, user) {
  const raw = firstNonEmpty_(jadwal && jadwal.jadwalOutlet, jadwal && jadwal.aksesOutletAbsensi, jadwal && jadwal.outlet, user && user.outletUtama, '');
  return isAllOutletToken_(raw) ? 'ALL' : raw;
}

function createAbsensiPdfFileV143_(group, ctx) {
  const summary = buildExportGroupSummaryV143_(group.rows);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  deleteExistingFileByNameV142_(ctx.folder, fileName);
  const html = buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary);
  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(html, 'text/html', fileName.replace(/\.pdf$/i, '.html')).getAs(MimeType.PDF).setName(fileName);
  const file = ctx.folder.createFile(blob);
  return {
    nama: group.nama,
    username: group.username || '',
    rows: (group.rows || []).filter(function(r){ return !r.isTemplate; }).length,
    templateKosong: !!group.templateKosong,
    fileName: fileName,
    fileId: file.getId(),
    url: file.getUrl()
  };
}

function buildExportGroupSummaryV143_(rows) {
  const realRows = (rows || []).filter(function(r){ return !r.isTemplate; });
  return buildExportGroupSummaryV142_(realRows);
}

function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const note = isTemplate
    ? '<div class="template-note">Template kosong: belum ada data absensi pada periode ini. Kolom Masuk, Pulang, Status, Terlambat, Total Kerja, dan Lembur dikosongkan.</div>'
    : '';
  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr' + (template ? ' class="template-row"' : '') + '>' +
      '<td class="center">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.outlet || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.shift || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="right">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td>' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="right">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="12" class="empty">Template kosong. Belum ada data absensi pada periode ini.</td></tr>';
  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 landscape;margin:12mm;}body{font-family:Arial,sans-serif;color:#0f172a;font-size:10px;}h1{font-size:20px;margin:0 0 4px;}h2{font-size:14px;margin:0;color:#334155}.head{display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;border-bottom:2px solid #0f172a;padding-bottom:10px;margin-bottom:12px}.brand{font-weight:900;letter-spacing:.08em;color:#0f172a}.muted{color:#64748b}.meta{font-size:10px;line-height:1.5;text-align:right}.info{display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:8px;margin:10px 0 12px}.card{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:10px;padding:8px;background:#f8fafc}.card small{display:block;color:#64748b;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:8px;letter-spacing:.06em}.card strong{display:block;font-size:13px;margin-top:3px}.employee{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;border-radius:10px;padding:9px 10px;margin-bottom:10px}.employee b{font-size:13px}.template-note{border:1px solid #fbbf24;background:#fffbeb;color:#92400e;border-radius:10px;padding:8px 10px;margin:0 0 10px;font-weight:700}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;}th,td{border:1px solid #cbd5e1;padding:5px 5px;vertical-align:middle;}th{background:#e2e8f0;font-size:8px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.04em;}td{font-size:9px;height:18px}.center{text-align:center}.right{text-align:right}.empty{text-align:center;padding:18px;color:#64748b}.template-row td{color:#334155}.foot{margin-top:12px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;color:#64748b;font-size:9px}.sign{margin-top:24px;display:flex;justify-content:flex-end}.signbox{width:190px;text-align:center}.signline{border-bottom:1px solid #0f172a;height:38px;margin-bottom:5px}' +
    '</style></head><body>' +
    '<div class="head"><div><div class="brand">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><h1>Rekap Absensi Karyawan</h1><h2>Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</h2></div><div class="meta"><b>Dibuat</b><br>' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '<br><span class="muted">Sistem APJ HR Absensi</span></div></div>' +
    '<div class="employee"><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.nama || '-') + '</b><br><span class="muted">Username: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.username || '-') + ' • Tanggal: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.startKey)) + ' s/d ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.endKey)) + '</span></div>' +
    note +
    '<div class="info"><div class="card"><small>Total Data</small><strong>' + summary.totalRows + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Hadir</small><strong>' + summary.hadir + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Terlambat</small><strong>' + summary.terlambat + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Tidak Checkout</small><strong>' + summary.tidakCheckout + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Total Lembur</small><strong>' + htmlEscapeV142_(hoursToTextZeroV131_(summary.totalLemburJam)) + '</strong></div><div class="card"><small>Total Kerja</small><strong>' + htmlEscapeV142_(minutesToDurationText_(summary.totalKerjaMenit)) + '</strong></div></div>' +
    '<table><thead><tr><th>No</th><th>Tanggal</th><th>Outlet</th><th>Shift</th><th>Jadwal Masuk</th><th>Jadwal Pulang</th><th>Masuk</th><th>Pulang</th><th>Status</th><th>Terlambat<br>(Menit)</th><th>Total Kerja</th><th>Lembur</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rowsHtml + '</tbody></table>' +
    '<div class="foot"><span>Dokumen dibuat otomatis oleh APJ HR Absensi.</span><span>File: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf')) + '</span></div>' +
    '<div class="sign"><div class="signbox"><div>Mengetahui,</div><div class="signline"></div><div>Owner / Supervisor</div></div></div>' +
    '</body></html>';
}

// Override HTML PDF V143 agar semua action lama (V142/V143) otomatis memakai layout formal V144.
function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  const note = isTemplate
    ? '<div class="notice"><b>Keterangan:</b> Belum terdapat catatan absensi pada periode laporan ini. Dokumen diterbitkan sebagai format rekap kosong; kolom realisasi absensi dikosongkan.</div>'
    : '';
  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center col-no">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-date">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-day">' + htmlEscapeV142_(dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(r.tanggalKey)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="col-outlet">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.outlet || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="col-shift">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.shift || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="col-status">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="right col-num">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="col-work">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="right col-lembur">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="13" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 landscape;margin:10mm;}*{box-sizing:border-box;}body{font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;color:#111827;font-size:9px;line-height:1.35;margin:0;}h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0}.doc-header{border:1px solid #111827;border-bottom:3px solid #111827;padding:10px 12px;margin-bottom:10px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start}.company{font-size:12px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.08em;text-transform:uppercase}.subtitle{font-size:8px;color:#4b5563;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;margin-top:2px}.title{text-align:center;flex:1;padding-top:2px}.title h1{font-size:18px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.04em}.title h2{font-size:11px;margin-top:3px;color:#374151;font-weight:700}.doc-meta{width:190px}.doc-meta table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse}.doc-meta td{border:none;padding:1px 0;font-size:8px}.doc-meta td:first-child{color:#4b5563;width:68px}.section-title{font-size:10px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.06em;margin:8px 0 4px;font-weight:800;color:#111827}.identity,.summary{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:8px}.identity th,.identity td,.summary th,.summary td{border:1px solid #9ca3af;padding:5px 6px}.identity th,.summary th{background:#f3f4f6;text-align:left;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:7.5px;letter-spacing:.05em;color:#374151}.summary td{font-weight:700;font-size:10px}.notice{border:1px solid #9ca3af;background:#f9fafb;color:#374151;padding:6px 8px;margin:6px 0 8px;font-size:9px}.main-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed}.main-table th,.main-table td{border:1px solid #9ca3af;padding:4px 4px;vertical-align:middle}.main-table th{background:#e5e7eb;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:7px;line-height:1.15;letter-spacing:.03em;text-align:center;color:#111827}.main-table td{height:18px;font-size:8px}.center{text-align:center}.right{text-align:right}.empty{text-align:center;padding:18px;color:#4b5563}.col-no{width:24px}.col-date{width:62px}.col-day{width:45px}.col-outlet{width:70px}.col-shift{width:90px}.col-time{width:55px}.col-status{width:80px}.col-num{width:54px}.col-work{width:78px}.col-lembur{width:55px}.footer{margin-top:10px;border-top:1px solid #9ca3af;padding-top:6px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;color:#4b5563;font-size:8px}.signatures{margin-top:18px;display:flex;justify-content:flex-end;gap:34px}.sig{width:160px;text-align:center;font-size:9px}.sig-title{font-weight:700;margin-bottom:34px}.sig-line{border-top:1px solid #111827;padding-top:4px}.muted{color:#4b5563}.nowrap{white-space:nowrap}' +
    '</style></head><body>' +
    '<div class="doc-header"><div style="width:190px"><div class="company">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><div class="subtitle">Dokumen Internal HR & Operasional</div></div><div class="title"><h1>Laporan Rekapitulasi Absensi Karyawan</h1><h2>Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</h2></div><div class="doc-meta"><table><tr><td>No. Dokumen</td><td>: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(docNo) + '</td></tr><tr><td>Tanggal Cetak</td><td>: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '</td></tr><tr><td>Sumber</td><td>: APJ HR Absensi</td></tr></table></div></div>' +
    '<div class="section-title">A. Identitas Karyawan</div>' +
    '<table class="identity"><tr><th>Nama Karyawan</th><th>Username</th><th>Periode Tanggal</th><th>Status Dokumen</th></tr><tr><td><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.nama || '-') + '</b></td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.username || '-') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.startKey)) + ' s/d ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.endKey)) + '</td><td>' + (isTemplate ? 'Format rekap kosong' : 'Rekap absensi tercatat') + '</td></tr></table>' +
    note +
    '<div class="section-title">B. Ringkasan Absensi</div>' +
    '<table class="summary"><tr><th>Total Data</th><th>Hadir</th><th>Terlambat</th><th>Tidak Checkout</th><th>Total Lembur</th><th>Total Kerja</th></tr><tr><td>' + summary.totalRows + '</td><td>' + summary.hadir + '</td><td>' + summary.terlambat + '</td><td>' + summary.tidakCheckout + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(hoursToTextZeroV131_(summary.totalLemburJam)) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(minutesToDurationText_(summary.totalKerjaMenit)) + '</td></tr></table>' +
    '<div class="section-title">C. Rincian Absensi Harian</div>' +
    '<table class="main-table"><thead><tr><th>No</th><th>Tanggal</th><th>Hari</th><th>Outlet</th><th>Shift</th><th>Jadwal<br>Masuk</th><th>Jadwal<br>Pulang</th><th>Masuk</th><th>Pulang</th><th>Status</th><th>Terlambat<br>(Menit)</th><th>Total Kerja</th><th>Lembur</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rowsHtml + '</tbody></table>' +
    '<div class="footer"><span>Dokumen ini dibuat otomatis oleh Sistem APJ HR Absensi dan digunakan untuk kebutuhan administrasi internal.</span><span class="nowrap">File: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</span></div>' +
    '<div class="signatures"><div class="sig"><div class="sig-title">Diperiksa oleh,</div><div class="sig-line">HR / Admin</div></div><div class="sig"><div class="sig-title">Disetujui oleh,</div><div class="sig-line">Owner / Supervisor</div></div></div>' +
    '</body></html>';
}

function dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(key) {
  if (!key) return '';
  const d = dateFromKey_(key);
  return ['Minggu','Senin','Selasa','Rabu','Kamis','Jumat','Sabtu'][d.getDay()] || '';
}

function uniqueLabelFromRowsV146_(rows, fieldName) {
  const seen = {};
  const list = [];
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const value = String(r && r[fieldName] || '').trim();
    const key = normKey_(value);
    if (value && !seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; list.push(value); }
  });
  if (!list.length) return '-';
  if (list.length <= 3) return list.join(', ');
  return 'Beberapa ' + (fieldName === 'outlet' ? 'Outlet' : 'Shift');
}

// Override HTML PDF terakhir: semua export lama otomatis memakai tampilan V146.
function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  const outletLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV146_(group.rows, 'outlet');
  const shiftLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV146_(group.rows, 'shift');
  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center col-no">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-date">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-day">' + htmlEscapeV142_(dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(r.tanggalKey)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-status">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-num">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-work">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-lembur">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 portrait;margin:2.54cm;}*{box-sizing:border-box;}body{font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;color:#111827;font-size:7.3px;line-height:1.18;margin:0;}h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0}.doc-header{border:1px solid #111827;border-bottom:2px solid #111827;padding:5px 6px;margin-bottom:5px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start}.company{font-size:8.2px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.05em;text-transform:uppercase}.subtitle{font-size:5.4px;color:#4b5563;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.035em;margin-top:1px}.title{text-align:center;flex:1;padding-top:0}.title h1{font-size:10.2px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.025em}.title h2{font-size:7px;margin-top:1px;color:#374151;font-weight:700}.doc-meta{width:105px}.doc-meta table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse}.doc-meta td{border:none;padding:0;font-size:5.1px;line-height:1.15}.doc-meta td:first-child{color:#4b5563;width:43px}.section-title{text-align:center;font-size:7.4px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.05em;margin:4px 0 2px;font-weight:800;color:#111827}.identity,.summary{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-bottom:4px;table-layout:fixed}.identity th,.identity td,.summary th,.summary td{border:1px solid #9ca3af;padding:2px 3px;text-align:center}.identity th,.summary th{background:#f3f4f6;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:5.4px;letter-spacing:.035em;color:#374151;text-align:center}.identity td,.summary td{font-size:6.4px}.summary td{font-weight:700}.main-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed}.main-table th,.main-table td{border:1px solid #9ca3af;padding:1.1px 1.5px;vertical-align:middle;overflow:hidden}.main-table th{background:#e5e7eb;text-transform:uppercase;font-size:5.15px;line-height:1.0;letter-spacing:.01em;text-align:center;color:#111827}.main-table td{height:9.9px;font-size:5.75px;line-height:1.03}.center{text-align:center}.right{text-align:right}.empty{text-align:center;padding:12px;color:#4b5563}.col-no{width:5%;}.col-date{width:12%;}.col-day{width:9%;}.col-time{width:9%;}.col-status{width:13%;}.col-num{width:10%;}.col-work{width:12%;}.col-lembur{width:8%;}.footer{margin-top:5px;border-top:1px solid #9ca3af;padding-top:4px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;gap:8px;color:#4b5563;font-size:5.5px}.muted{color:#4b5563}.nowrap{white-space:nowrap}.page-compact{page-break-inside:avoid}' +
    '</style></head><body><div class="page-compact">' +
    '<div class="doc-header"><div style="width:118px"><div class="company">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><div class="subtitle">Dokumen Internal HR & Operasional</div></div><div class="title"><h1>Laporan Rekapitulasi Absensi Karyawan</h1><h2>Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</h2></div><div class="doc-meta"><table><tr><td>No. Dokumen</td><td>: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(docNo) + '</td></tr><tr><td>Tanggal Cetak</td><td>: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '</td></tr><tr><td>Sumber</td><td>: APJ HR Absensi</td></tr></table></div></div>' +
    '<div class="section-title">A. Identitas Karyawan</div>' +
    '<table class="identity"><tr><th>Nama Karyawan</th><th>Username</th><th>Outlet</th><th>Shift</th></tr><tr><td><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.nama || '-') + '</b></td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.username || '-') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(outletLabel) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(shiftLabel) + '</td></tr><tr><th>Periode Tanggal</th><th colspan="2">Status Dokumen</th><th>File</th></tr><tr><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.startKey)) + ' s/d ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.endKey)) + '</td><td colspan="2">' + (isTemplate ? 'Format rekap kosong' : 'Rekap absensi tercatat') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</td></tr></table>' +
    '<div class="section-title">B. Ringkasan Absensi</div>' +
    '<table class="summary"><tr><th>Total Data</th><th>Hadir</th><th>Terlambat</th><th>Tidak Checkout</th><th>Total Lembur</th><th>Total Kerja</th></tr><tr><td>' + summary.totalRows + '</td><td>' + summary.hadir + '</td><td>' + summary.terlambat + '</td><td>' + summary.tidakCheckout + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(hoursToTextZeroV131_(summary.totalLemburJam)) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(minutesToDurationText_(summary.totalKerjaMenit)) + '</td></tr></table>' +

// 1) Export PDF memakai A4 potret penuh dengan margin formal 2,54 cm semua sisi.
// 2) Kontainer laporan dipaksa memakai 100% area cetak; tidak ada max-width, zoom,
//    transform, atau width kecil yang membuat tabel terlihat mengumpul.
// 3) Outlet dan Shift hanya tampil di bagian A. Identitas Karyawan.
// 4) Rincian Absensi Harian tidak lagi memuat kolom Outlet dan Shift.
// 5) Lebar kolom rincian harian diatur ulang dengan colgroup agar proporsional.

    exportFolderId: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.ABSENSI_EXPORT_FOLDER_ID,

}

function uniqueLabelFromRowsV147_(rows, fieldName) {
  const seen = {};
  const list = [];
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const value = String(r && r[fieldName] || '').trim();
    const key = normKey_(value);
    if (value && !seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; list.push(value); }
  });
  if (!list.length) return '-';
  if (list.length <= 4) return list.join(', ');
  return 'Beberapa ' + (fieldName === 'outlet' ? 'Outlet' : 'Shift');
}

function cssEscapeV147_(value) {
  return htmlEscapeV142_(value);
}

// Override paling akhir: create PDF V143 tetap dipakai, tetapi HTML final memakai desain V147.
function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  const outletLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV147_(group.rows, 'outlet');
  const shiftLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV147_(group.rows, 'shift');

  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center nowrap">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(r.tanggalKey)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  const detailColgroup = '<colgroup>' +
    '<col style="width:4.8%">' +
    '<col style="width:12.2%">' +
    '<col style="width:8.5%">' +
    '<col style="width:9.4%">' +
    '<col style="width:9.4%">' +
    '<col style="width:8.7%">' +
    '<col style="width:8.7%">' +
    '<col style="width:14.7%">' +
    '<col style="width:8.4%">' +
    '<col style="width:8.6%">' +
    '<col style="width:6.6%">' +
    '</colgroup>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 portrait;margin:2.54cm;}' +
    'html,body{width:100%;min-width:0;margin:0;padding:0;background:#fff;color:#111827;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;-webkit-print-color-adjust:exact;print-color-adjust:exact;}' +
    '*{box-sizing:border-box;}' +
    'body{font-size:8px;line-height:1.2;}' +
    'h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0;padding:0;}' +
    '.page{display:block;width:100%;max-width:none;min-width:0;margin:0;padding:0;transform:none;zoom:1;}' +
    '.doc-header{width:100%;border:1px solid #111827;border-bottom:2px solid #111827;margin:0 0 5mm 0;padding:3mm 3.2mm;}' +
    '.header-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;}' +
    '.header-table td{border:none;padding:0;vertical-align:top;}' +
    '.brand-cell{width:27%;}.title-cell{width:46%;text-align:center;}.meta-cell{width:27%;}' +
    '.company{font-size:9.2px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.06em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.15;}' +
    '.subtitle{font-size:6.2px;color:#4b5563;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.04em;margin-top:1mm;line-height:1.2;}' +
    '.title h1{font-size:12.2px;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.025em;font-weight:800;line-height:1.15;}' +
    '.title h2{font-size:8px;margin-top:1mm;color:#374151;font-weight:700;line-height:1.15;}' +
    '.meta-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;}' +
    '.meta-table td{border:none;padding:0 0 .7mm 0;font-size:6.1px;line-height:1.12;word-break:break-word;}' +
    '.meta-table td:first-child{width:42%;color:#4b5563;}' +
    '.section{width:100%;max-width:none;margin:0 0 3.2mm 0;padding:0;}' +
    '.section-title{width:100%;margin:0 0 1.5mm 0;padding:1.6mm 2mm;border:1px solid #cbd5e1;background:#f3f4f6;text-align:center;font-size:8.4px;line-height:1.1;font-weight:800;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.05em;color:#111827;}' +
    'table{width:100%;max-width:none;min-width:0;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;margin:0;}' +
    'th,td{border:1px solid #9ca3af;padding:1.8mm 1.5mm;vertical-align:middle;white-space:normal;overflow-wrap:anywhere;word-break:break-word;}' +
    'th{background:#e5e7eb;text-align:center;font-size:6.6px;line-height:1.05;font-weight:800;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.018em;color:#111827;}' +
    'td{font-size:7.1px;line-height:1.12;}' +
    '.identity th,.identity td{padding:1.7mm 1.6mm;}' +

    '.identity td{font-size:7.4px;}' +
    '.summary th,.summary td{padding:1.55mm 1.4mm;}' +
    '.summary th{font-size:6.2px;background:#f3f4f6;color:#374151;}' +

    '.signature,.ttd,.template-note,.empty-template-note,.keterangan-template{display:none!important;}' +
    'tr,.section{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +
    '</style></head><body><div class="page">' +
    '<div class="doc-header"><table class="header-table"><tr><td class="brand-cell"><div class="company">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><div class="subtitle">Dokumen Internal HR & Operasional</div></td><td class="title-cell title"><h1>Laporan Rekapitulasi Absensi Karyawan</h1><h2>Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</h2></td><td class="meta-cell"><table class="meta-table"><tr><td>No. Dokumen</td><td>: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(docNo) + '</td></tr><tr><td>Tanggal Cetak</td><td>: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '</td></tr><tr><td>Sumber</td><td>: APJ HR Absensi</td></tr></table></td></tr></table></div>' +

function uniqueLabelFromRowsV148_(rows, fieldName) {
  const seen = {};
  const list = [];
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const value = String(r && r[fieldName] || '').trim();
    const key = normKey_(value);
    if (value && !seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; list.push(value); }
  });
  if (!list.length) return '-';
  if (list.length <= 3) return list.join(', ');
  return 'Beberapa ' + (fieldName === 'outlet' ? 'Outlet' : 'Shift');
}

// Override HTML PDF terakhir: semua export lama otomatis memakai tampilan V148.
function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  const outletLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV148_(group.rows, 'outlet');
  const shiftLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV148_(group.rows, 'shift');
  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center col-no">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-date">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-day">' + htmlEscapeV142_(dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(r.tanggalKey)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-status">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-num">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-work">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-lembur">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 portrait;margin:2.54cm;}' +
    '*{box-sizing:border-box;-webkit-print-color-adjust:exact;print-color-adjust:exact;}' +
    'html,body{width:100%;margin:0;padding:0;background:#fff;color:#000;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;}' +
    'body{font-size:5.2px;line-height:1.02;}' +
    'h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0;}' +
    '.sheet{width:100%;margin:0;padding:0;page-break-before:avoid;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +
    '.doc-header{width:100%;border:1px solid #000;padding:2.2px 3.2px;margin:0 0 3px 0;}' +
    '.head-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;}' +
    '.head-table td{border:none;padding:0;vertical-align:top;color:#000;}' +
    '.head-left{width:27%;}' +
    '.head-center{width:46%;text-align:center;padding:0 4px;}' +
    '.head-right{width:27%;text-align:right;}' +
    '.company{font-size:6.4px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:.03em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.1;}' +
    '.subtitle{font-size:4.6px;line-height:1.1;margin-top:1px;}' +
    '.report-title{font-size:7.6px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:.02em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.05;}' +
    '.report-subtitle{font-size:5.3px;line-height:1.05;margin-top:1px;}' +
    '.meta-line{font-size:4.5px;line-height:1.14;}' +
    '.section-title{width:100%;margin:0 0 1.5px 0;padding:1.4px 2px;border:1px solid #000;background:#f2f2f2;text-align:center;font-size:5.6px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.02em;color:#000;}' +
    '.identity,.summary,.main-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;margin:0 0 3px 0;}' +
    '.identity th,.identity td,.summary th,.summary td,.main-table th,.main-table td{border:1px solid #000;padding:1px 1.4px;vertical-align:middle;color:#000;word-break:break-word;overflow-wrap:anywhere;}' +
    '.identity th,.summary th,.main-table th{background:#f2f2f2;font-weight:700;text-align:center;}' +
    '.identity th{font-size:4.8px;line-height:1.0;}' +
    '.identity td{font-size:5.4px;line-height:1.02;text-align:center;}' +
    '.summary th{font-size:4.6px;line-height:1.0;}' +
    '.summary td{font-size:5.2px;line-height:1.02;text-align:center;font-weight:700;}' +
    '.main-table th{font-size:4.25px;line-height:0.98;text-align:center;}' +
    '.main-table td{font-size:4.8px;line-height:0.98;height:11.4px;text-align:center;}' +
    '.center{text-align:center;}' +
    '.empty{text-align:center;padding:8px;color:#000;}' +
    '.col-no{width:5%;}.col-date{width:13%;}.col-day{width:10%;}.col-time{width:9%;}.col-status{width:11%;}.col-num{width:8%;}.col-work{width:10%;}.col-lembur{width:7%;}' +
    '.footer{margin-top:2px;border-top:1px solid #000;padding-top:2px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;gap:6px;color:#000;font-size:4.5px;line-height:1.1;}' +
    '.nowrap{white-space:nowrap;}' +
    '.template-note{display:none;}' +
    'tr{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +
    '</style></head><body><div class="sheet">' +
    '<div class="doc-header"><table class="head-table"><tr>' +
      '<td class="head-left"><div class="company">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><div class="subtitle">Dokumen Internal HR & Operasional</div></td>' +
      '<td class="head-center"><div class="report-title">Laporan Rekapitulasi Absensi Karyawan</div><div class="report-subtitle">Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</div></td>' +
      '<td class="head-right"><div class="meta-line"><b>No. Dokumen:</b> ' + htmlEscapeV142_(docNo) + '</div><div class="meta-line"><b>Tanggal Cetak:</b> ' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '</div><div class="meta-line"><b>Sumber:</b> APJ HR Absensi</div></td>' +
    '</tr></table></div>' +
    '<div class="section-title">A. Identitas Karyawan</div>' +
    '<table class="identity"><tr><th>Nama Karyawan</th><th>Username</th><th>Outlet</th><th>Shift</th></tr><tr><td><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.nama || '-') + '</b></td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.username || '-') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(outletLabel) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(shiftLabel) + '</td></tr><tr><th>Periode Tanggal</th><th colspan="2">Status Dokumen</th><th>Nama File</th></tr><tr><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.startKey)) + ' s/d ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.endKey)) + '</td><td colspan="2">' + (isTemplate ? 'Format rekap kosong' : 'Rekap absensi tercatat') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</td></tr></table>' +
    '<div class="section-title">B. Ringkasan Absensi</div>' +
    '<table class="summary"><tr><th>Total Data</th><th>Hadir</th><th>Terlambat</th><th>Tidak Checkout</th><th>Total Lembur</th><th>Total Kerja</th></tr><tr><td>' + summary.totalRows + '</td><td>' + summary.hadir + '</td><td>' + summary.terlambat + '</td><td>' + summary.tidakCheckout + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(hoursToTextZeroV131_(summary.totalLemburJam)) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(minutesToDurationText_(summary.totalKerjaMenit)) + '</td></tr></table>' +
    '<div class="section-title">C. Rincian Absensi Harian</div>' +
    '<table class="main-table"><colgroup><col class="col-no"><col class="col-date"><col class="col-day"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-status"><col class="col-num"><col class="col-work"><col class="col-lembur"></colgroup><thead><tr><th>No</th><th>Tanggal</th><th>Hari</th><th>Jadwal<br>Masuk</th><th>Jadwal<br>Pulang</th><th>Masuk</th><th>Pulang</th><th>Status</th><th>Terlambat<br>(Menit)</th><th>Total Kerja</th><th>Lembur</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rowsHtml + '</tbody></table>' +
    '<div class="footer"><span>Dokumen dibuat otomatis oleh Sistem APJ HR Absensi.</span><span class="nowrap">File: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</span></div>' +
    '</div></body></html>';
}


// =============================================================================
// V149 - REKAP ABSENSI PDF A4 POTRET ONE PAGE BALANCED
// =============================================================================
// Perubahan V149:
// 1) Tetap A4 potret satu lembar dengan margin 2,54 cm.
// 2) Tampilan tidak lagi terlalu kecil/kerempeng: font, header, dan tinggi baris dinaikkan.
// 3) Kolom tabel C diatur ulang supaya lebar lebih proporsional dan nyaman dibaca.
// 4) Semua garis tabel tetap hitam.
// 5) Isi tabel A. Identitas Karyawan tetap center semua.

function setupAbsensiSheetsV149(showResult) {
  const res = setupAbsensiSheetsV148(showResult);
  return Object.assign({}, res || {}, {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Setup Absensi V149 selesai. PDF satu lembar A4 potret dibuat lebih seimbang: baris lebih tinggi, kolom proporsional, garis hitam.',
    exportFolderId: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.ABSENSI_EXPORT_FOLDER_ID,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  });
}

function uniqueLabelFromRowsV149_(rows, fieldName) {
  const seen = {};
  const list = [];
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const value = String(r && r[fieldName] || '').trim();
    const key = normKey_(value);
    if (value && !seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; list.push(value); }
  });
  if (!list.length) return '-';
  if (list.length <= 3) return list.join(', ');
  return 'Beberapa ' + (fieldName === 'outlet' ? 'Outlet' : 'Shift');
}

function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);

  const outletLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV149_(group.rows, 'outlet');
  const shiftLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV149_(group.rows, 'shift');

  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center col-no">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-date">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-day">' + htmlEscapeV142_(dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(r.tanggalKey)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-status">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-late">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-work">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-overtime">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 portrait;margin:2.54cm;}' +
    '*{box-sizing:border-box;-webkit-print-color-adjust:exact;print-color-adjust:exact;}' +
    'html,body{width:100%;height:auto;margin:0;padding:0;background:#fff;color:#000;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;}' +

    'h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0;}' +
    '.sheet{width:100%;margin:0;padding:0;page-break-before:avoid;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +

    /* Header dibuat lebih besar tapi tetap hemat tinggi */
    '.doc-header{width:100%;border:1px solid #000;padding:3px 4px;margin:0 0 4px 0;}' +
