    '.head-table td{border:none;padding:0;vertical-align:middle;color:#000;}' +
    '.head-left{width:27%;}' +
    '.head-center{width:46%;text-align:center;padding:0 4px;}' +
    '.head-right{width:27%;text-align:right;}' +
    '.company{font-size:7.2px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.03em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.12;}' +
    '.subtitle{font-size:5.2px;line-height:1.12;margin-top:1px;}' +
    '.report-title{font-size:8.8px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.02em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.08;}' +
    '.report-subtitle{font-size:6.2px;line-height:1.1;margin-top:1px;font-weight:700;}' +
    '.meta-line{font-size:5.1px;line-height:1.18;}' +

    /* Judul section hitam, rapi, tidak tinggi berlebihan */
    '.section-title{width:100%;margin:0 0 2px 0;padding:2px 2px;border:1px solid #000;background:#f2f2f2;text-align:center;font-size:6.3px;font-weight:800;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.02em;color:#000;}' +

    /* Semua tabel full lebar, garis hitam */
    '.identity,.summary,.main-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;margin:0 0 4px 0;}' +
    '.identity th,.identity td,.summary th,.summary td,.main-table th,.main-table td{border:1px solid #000;padding:1.8px 2.1px;vertical-align:middle;color:#000;word-break:break-word;overflow-wrap:anywhere;}' +
    '.identity th,.summary th,.main-table th{background:#f2f2f2;font-weight:800;text-align:center;}' +

    /* Tabel A center semua */
    '.identity th{font-size:5.6px;line-height:1.06;}' +
    '.identity td{font-size:6.3px;line-height:1.08;text-align:center;height:16px;}' +

    /* Tabel B dibuat jelas tapi pendek */
    '.summary th{font-size:5.3px;line-height:1.05;}' +
    '.summary td{font-size:6.2px;line-height:1.08;text-align:center;font-weight:800;height:15px;}' +

    /* Tabel C: baris dinaikkan supaya tidak kerempeng, masih aman satu halaman */
    '.main-table th{font-size:5.05px;line-height:1.05;text-align:center;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;}' +
    '.main-table td{font-size:5.85px;line-height:1.06;height:14.8px;text-align:center;padding-top:1.6px;padding-bottom:1.6px;}' +

    '.center{text-align:center;}' +
    '.empty{text-align:center;padding:10px;color:#000;}' +

    /* Proporsi kolom total 100%.
       Kolom waktu dipadatkan, tanggal/hari/status dibuat lebih enak dibaca. */
    '.col-no{width:4.5%;}' +
    '.col-date{width:13.2%;}' +
    '.col-day{width:9.5%;}' +
    '.col-time{width:8.6%;}' +
    '.col-status{width:11.8%;}' +
    '.col-late{width:8.4%;}' +
    '.col-work{width:10.3%;}' +
    '.col-overtime{width:8.3%;}' +

    '.footer{margin-top:3px;border-top:1px solid #000;padding-top:2.5px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;gap:6px;color:#000;font-size:5.1px;line-height:1.12;}' +
    '.nowrap{white-space:nowrap;}' +
    'tr{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +
    '</style></head><body><div class="sheet">' +

    '<div class="doc-header"><table class="head-table"><tr>' +
      '<td class="head-left"><div class="company">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><div class="subtitle">Dokumen Internal HR & Operasional</div></td>' +
      '<td class="head-center"><div class="report-title">Laporan Rekapitulasi Absensi Karyawan</div><div class="report-subtitle">Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</div></td>' +
      '<td class="head-right"><div class="meta-line"><b>No. Dokumen:</b> ' + htmlEscapeV142_(docNo) + '</div><div class="meta-line"><b>Tanggal Cetak:</b> ' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '</div><div class="meta-line"><b>Sumber:</b> APJ HR Absensi</div></td>' +
    '</tr></table></div>' +

    '<div class="section-title">A. Identitas Karyawan</div>' +
    '<table class="identity"><tr><th>Nama Karyawan</th><th>Username</th><th>Outlet</th><th>Shift</th></tr><tr><td><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.nama || '-') + '</b></td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.username || '-') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(outletLabel) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(shiftLabel) + '</td></tr><tr><th>Periode Tanggal</th><th colspan="2">Status Dokumen</th><th>Nama File</th></tr><tr><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.startKey)) + ' s/d ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.endKey)) + '</td><td colspan="2">' + (isTemplate ? 'Format rekap kosong' : 'Rekap absensi tercatat') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</td></tr></table>' +

    '<div class="section-title">B. Ringkasan Absensi</div>' +
    '<table class="summary"><tr><th>Total Data</th><th>Hadir</th><th>Terlambat</th><th>Tidak Checkout</th><th>Total Lembur</th><th>Total Kerja</th></tr><tr><td>' + summary.totalRows + '</td><td>' + summary.hadir + '</td><td>' + summary.terlambat + '</td><td>' + summary.tidakCheckout + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(hoursToTextZeroV131_(summary.totalLemburJam)) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(minutesToDurationText_(summary.totalKerjaMenit)) + '</td></tr></table>' +

    '<div class="section-title">C. Rincian Absensi Harian</div>' +
    '<table class="main-table"><colgroup><col class="col-no"><col class="col-date"><col class="col-day"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-status"><col class="col-late"><col class="col-work"><col class="col-overtime"></colgroup><thead><tr><th>No</th><th>Tanggal</th><th>Hari</th><th>Jadwal<br>Masuk</th><th>Jadwal<br>Pulang</th><th>Masuk</th><th>Pulang</th><th>Status</th><th>Terlambat<br>(Menit)</th><th>Total Kerja</th><th>Lembur</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rowsHtml + '</tbody></table>' +

    '<div class="footer"><span>Dokumen dibuat otomatis oleh Sistem APJ HR Absensi.</span><span class="nowrap">File: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</span></div>' +
    '</div></body></html>';
}

function uniqueLabelFromRowsV151_(rows, fieldName) {
  const seen = {};
  const list = [];
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const value = String(r && r[fieldName] || '').trim();
    const key = normKey_(value);
    if (value && !seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; list.push(value); }
  });
  if (!list.length) return '-';
  if (list.length <= 3) return list.join(', ');
  return 'Beberapa ' + (fieldName === 'outlet' ? 'Outlet' : 'Shift');
}

// Override HTML PDF terakhir: versi ini memperbesar tampilan V150 tanpa mengubah struktur.
function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  const outletLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV151_(group.rows, 'outlet');
  const shiftLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV151_(group.rows, 'shift');

  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center col-no">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-date">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-day">' + htmlEscapeV142_(dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(r.tanggalKey)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-status">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-late">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-work">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-overtime">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 portrait;margin:2.54cm;}' +
    '*{box-sizing:border-box;-webkit-print-color-adjust:exact;print-color-adjust:exact;}' +
    'html,body{width:100%;height:auto;margin:0;padding:0;background:#fff;color:#000;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;}' +
    'body{font-size:7.05px;line-height:1.16;}' +
    'h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0;}' +
    '.sheet{width:100%;margin:0;padding:0;page-break-before:avoid;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +

    '.doc-header{width:100%;border:1px solid #000;padding:4.2px 5px;margin:0 0 5px 0;}' +
    '.head-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;}' +
    '.head-table td{border:none;padding:0;vertical-align:middle;color:#000;}' +
    '.head-left{width:27%;}' +
    '.head-center{width:46%;text-align:center;padding:0 4px;}' +
    '.head-right{width:27%;text-align:right;}' +
    '.company{font-size:8.2px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.03em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.14;}' +
    '.subtitle{font-size:5.95px;line-height:1.14;margin-top:1px;}' +
    '.report-title{font-size:10px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.02em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.1;}' +
    '.report-subtitle{font-size:7.2px;line-height:1.12;margin-top:1px;font-weight:700;}' +
    '.meta-line{font-size:5.85px;line-height:1.2;}' +

    '.section-title{width:100%;margin:0 0 2.4px 0;padding:2.7px 2px;border:1px solid #000;background:#f2f2f2;text-align:center;font-size:7.05px;font-weight:800;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.02em;color:#000;}' +

    '.identity,.summary,.main-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;margin:0 0 5px 0;}' +
    '.identity th,.identity td,.summary th,.summary td,.main-table th,.main-table td{border:1px solid #000;padding:2.25px 2.6px;vertical-align:middle;color:#000;word-break:break-word;overflow-wrap:anywhere;}' +
    '.identity th,.summary th,.main-table th{background:#f2f2f2;font-weight:800;text-align:center;}' +

    '.identity th{font-size:6.25px;line-height:1.08;}' +
    '.identity td{font-size:7.05px;line-height:1.1;text-align:center;height:19px;}' +

    '.summary th{font-size:6px;line-height:1.08;}' +
    '.summary td{font-size:7px;line-height:1.1;text-align:center;font-weight:800;height:18px;}' +

    '.main-table th{font-size:5.75px;line-height:1.08;text-align:center;padding-top:2.6px;padding-bottom:2.6px;}' +
    '.main-table td{font-size:6.65px;line-height:1.08;height:20px;text-align:center;padding-top:2px;padding-bottom:2px;}' +

    '.center{text-align:center;}' +
    '.empty{text-align:center;padding:12px;color:#000;}' +

    '.col-no{width:4.5%;}' +
    '.col-date{width:13.2%;}' +
    '.col-day{width:9.5%;}' +
    '.col-time{width:8.6%;}' +
    '.col-status{width:11.8%;}' +
    '.col-late{width:8.4%;}' +
    '.col-work{width:10.3%;}' +
    '.col-overtime{width:8.3%;}' +

    '.footer{margin-top:4px;border-top:1px solid #000;padding-top:3px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;gap:6px;color:#000;font-size:5.8px;line-height:1.14;}' +
    '.nowrap{white-space:nowrap;}' +
    'tr{page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +
    '</style></head><body><div class="sheet">' +

    '<div class="doc-header"><table class="head-table"><tr>' +
      '<td class="head-left"><div class="company">AMPERA PAK JENGGOT</div><div class="subtitle">Dokumen Internal HR & Operasional</div></td>' +
      '<td class="head-center"><div class="report-title">Laporan Rekapitulasi Absensi Karyawan</div><div class="report-subtitle">Periode ' + htmlEscapeV142_(ctx.periodLabel) + '</div></td>' +
      '<td class="head-right"><div class="meta-line"><b>No. Dokumen:</b> ' + htmlEscapeV142_(docNo) + '</div><div class="meta-line"><b>Tanggal Cetak:</b> ' + htmlEscapeV142_(generated) + '</div><div class="meta-line"><b>Sumber:</b> APJ HR Absensi</div></td>' +
    '</tr></table></div>' +

    '<div class="section-title">A. Identitas Karyawan</div>' +
    '<table class="identity"><tr><th>Nama Karyawan</th><th>Username</th><th>Outlet</th><th>Shift</th></tr><tr><td><b>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.nama || '-') + '</b></td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(group.username || '-') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(outletLabel) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(shiftLabel) + '</td></tr><tr><th>Periode Tanggal</th><th colspan="2">Status Dokumen</th><th>Nama File</th></tr><tr><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.startKey)) + ' s/d ' + htmlEscapeV142_(displayDateKeyV142_(ctx.endKey)) + '</td><td colspan="2">' + (isTemplate ? 'Format rekap kosong' : 'Rekap absensi tercatat') + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</td></tr></table>' +

    '<div class="section-title">B. Ringkasan Absensi</div>' +
    '<table class="summary"><tr><th>Total Data</th><th>Hadir</th><th>Terlambat</th><th>Tidak Checkout</th><th>Total Lembur</th><th>Total Kerja</th></tr><tr><td>' + summary.totalRows + '</td><td>' + summary.hadir + '</td><td>' + summary.terlambat + '</td><td>' + summary.tidakCheckout + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(hoursToTextZeroV131_(summary.totalLemburJam)) + '</td><td>' + htmlEscapeV142_(minutesToDurationText_(summary.totalKerjaMenit)) + '</td></tr></table>' +

    '<div class="section-title">C. Rincian Absensi Harian</div>' +
    '<table class="main-table"><colgroup><col class="col-no"><col class="col-date"><col class="col-day"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-time"><col class="col-status"><col class="col-late"><col class="col-work"><col class="col-overtime"></colgroup><thead><tr><th>No</th><th>Tanggal</th><th>Hari</th><th>Jadwal<br>Masuk</th><th>Jadwal<br>Pulang</th><th>Masuk</th><th>Pulang</th><th>Status</th><th>Terlambat<br>(Menit)</th><th>Total Kerja</th><th>Lembur</th></tr></thead><tbody>' + rowsHtml + '</tbody></table>' +

    '<div class="footer"><span>Dokumen dibuat otomatis oleh Sistem APJ HR Absensi.</span><span class="nowrap">File: ' + htmlEscapeV142_(fileName) + '</span></div>' +
    '</div></body></html>';
}

    const value = String(r && r[fieldName] || '').trim();
    const key = normKey_(value);
    if (value && !seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; list.push(value); }

// Override HTML PDF terakhir: versi ini membesarkan V151 sedikit lagi.
function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);

  const outletLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV152_(group.rows, 'outlet');
  const shiftLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV152_(group.rows, 'shift');

  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center col-no">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-date">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-day">' + htmlEscapeV142_(dayNameFromDateKeyV144_(r.tanggalKey)) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jadwalPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamMasuk || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-status">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-late">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-work">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-overtime">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalLemburLabel || hoursToTextZeroV131_(r.totalLemburJam || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +
    '@page{size:A4 portrait;margin:2.54cm;}' +
    '*{box-sizing:border-box;-webkit-print-color-adjust:exact;print-color-adjust:exact;}' +
    'html,body{width:100%;height:auto;margin:0;padding:0;background:#fff;color:#000;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;}' +
    'body{font-size:7.35px;line-height:1.17;}' +
    'h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0;}' +
    '.sheet{width:100%;margin:0;padding:0;page-break-before:avoid;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +

function uniqueLabelFromRowsV153_(rows, fieldName) {
  const seen = {};
  const list = [];
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const value = String(r && r[fieldName] || '').trim();
    const key = normKey_(value);
    if (value && !seen[key]) { seen[key] = true; list.push(value); }
  });
  if (!list.length) return '-';
  if (list.length <= 3) return list.join(', ');
  return 'Beberapa ' + (fieldName === 'outlet' ? 'Outlet' : 'Shift');
}

// Override HTML PDF terakhir: versi ini membesarkan V152 sedikit lagi.
function buildAbsensiPdfHtmlV143_(group, ctx, summary) {
  const generated = formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss');
  const isTemplate = !!group.templateKosong;
  const docNo = 'APJ-HR-ABS-' + String(ctx.startKey || '').replace(/-/g, '').slice(0, 6) + '-' + String(group.username || group.nama || 'KRY').toUpperCase().replace(/[^A-Z0-9]+/g, '').slice(0, 10);
  const fileName = safeFileNameV142_(String(group.nama || 'Karyawan') + '-Absensi-' + ctx.periodLabel + '.pdf');
  const outletLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV153_(group.rows, 'outlet');
  const shiftLabel = uniqueLabelFromRowsV153_(group.rows, 'shift');

  const rowsHtml = (group.rows || []).map(function(r, i) {
    const template = !!r.isTemplate;
    const status = template ? '' : combinedStatusTextV142_(r);
    return '<tr>' +
      '<td class="center col-no">' + (i + 1) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-date">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.tanggal || r.tanggalKey || '') + '</td>' +

      '<td class="center col-time">' + htmlEscapeV142_(r.jamPulang || '') + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-status">' + htmlEscapeV142_(status) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-late">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(String(r.terlambatMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +
      '<td class="center col-work">' + (template ? '' : htmlEscapeV142_(r.totalKerjaBersih || minutesToDurationText_(r.totalKerjaBersihMenit || 0))) + '</td>' +

      '</tr>';
  }).join('') || '<tr><td colspan="11" class="empty">Belum terdapat data absensi pada periode laporan.</td></tr>';

  return '<!doctype html><html><head><meta charset="utf-8"><style>' +

    'h1,h2,h3,p{margin:0;}' +
    '.sheet{width:100%;margin:0;padding:0;page-break-before:avoid;page-break-after:avoid;page-break-inside:avoid;break-inside:avoid;}' +

    '.doc-header{width:100%;border:1px solid #000;padding:4.8px 5.4px;margin:0 0 5.2px 0;}' +
    '.head-table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;table-layout:fixed;}' +
    '.head-table td{border:none;padding:0;vertical-align:middle;color:#000;}' +
    '.head-left{width:27%;}' +
    '.head-center{width:46%;text-align:center;padding:0 4px;}' +
    '.head-right{width:27%;text-align:right;}' +
    '.company{font-size:8.85px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.03em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.14;}' +
    '.subtitle{font-size:6.4px;line-height:1.14;margin-top:1px;}' +
    '.report-title{font-size:10.8px;font-weight:800;letter-spacing:.02em;text-transform:uppercase;line-height:1.1;}' +
    '.report-subtitle{font-size:7.75px;line-height:1.12;margin-top:1px;font-weight:700;}' +

// =============================================================================
// DASHBOARD ABSENSI V168 - REAL SUMMARY DATA
// =============================================================================
function getDashboardAbsensiV168(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const isCalendarOnly = payload.calendarOnly === true || String(payload.calendarOnly || '').toLowerCase() === 'true';
  if (!isCalendarOnly) setupAbsensiSheetsV131(false);
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  const isAdmin = isHrKaryawanAdminV157_(currentUser);
  const today = inferDateKey_(payload.tanggal || payload.date || payload.tanggalKey) || todayKey_();
  const todayDate = dateFromKey_(today);
  const todayDay = Number(formatDate_(todayDate, 'd'));
  const bulan = monthNameId_(todayDate);
  const tahun = formatDate_(todayDate, 'yyyy');
  const nowMinutes = Number(formatDate_(new Date(), 'H')) * 60 + Number(formatDate_(new Date(), 'm'));

  const allUsers = getHrKaryawanUsersV157_();
  const activeUsersAll = allUsers.filter(function(u) { return normKey_(u.status || 'AKTIF') === 'aktif'; });
  const users = isAdmin ? activeUsersAll : activeUsersAll.filter(function(u) {
    return normKey_(u.username) === normKey_(currentUser.username) || normKey_(u.nama) === normKey_(currentUser.nama);
  });

  // APP-V.4.6_FIX4: request kalender tidak perlu menghitung rekap absensi penuh.
  // Ini mempercepat Dashboard Utama/kalender saat hanya butuh libur nasional, ulang tahun, dan pesanan.
  if (isCalendarOnly) {
    return {
      sukses: true,
      success: true,
      version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
      calendarOnly: true,
      tanggal: today,
      todayLabel: formatDate_(todayDate, 'EEEE, dd MMMM yyyy'),
      syncAt: formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss'),
      user: publicUser_(currentUser),
      kpi: {},
      outletAccuracy: [],
      detailAbsensi: [],
      belumAbsen: [],
      belumCheckout: [],
      lokasiAbsen: [],
      topLembur: [],
      topTerlambat: [],
      karyawanLibur: [],
      karyawanIzin: [],
      karyawanAlpa: [],
      calendar: buildAbsensiCalendarV168_(todayDate, activeUsersAll),
      pesan: 'Kalender Dashboard berhasil dimuat.'
    };
  }

  const userMap = buildDashboardUserMapV168_(users);
  const outlets = getHrKaryawanOutletsV157_();
  const shifts = getHrKaryawanShiftsV157_();
  const shiftMap = buildDashboardShiftMapV168_(shifts);
  const jadwalRows = getHrKaryawanJadwalV157_(shifts).filter(function(r) {
    const p = parseHrJadwalDateV167_(r.hari || r.tanggal);
    if (Number(p.day || 0) !== todayDay || normKey_(p.bulan) !== normKey_(bulan) || String(p.tahun || '') !== tahun) return false;
    if (isAdmin) return true;
    return normKey_(r.username) === normKey_(currentUser.username) || normKey_(r.nama) === normKey_(currentUser.nama);
  }).map(function(r) {
    const u = findDashboardUserForRowV168_(r, users) || {};
    const shift = shiftMap[normKey_(r.shift)] || {};
    return {
      nama: r.nama || u.nama || '-',
      username: r.username || u.username || '',
      outlet: r.outlet || shift.outlet || u.outletUtama || '-',
      shift: r.shift || '',
      jam: r.jam || (shift.jamMasuk || shift.jamPulang ? [shift.jamMasuk || '', shift.jamPulang || ''].filter(Boolean).join(' - ') : ''),
      jamMasukJadwal: shift.jamMasuk || '',
      jamPulangJadwal: shift.jamPulang || '',
      status: r.status || 'AKTIF'
    };
  });

  const absRows = readDashboardAbsensiRowsV168_(today, isAdmin, currentUser);
  const absMap = {};
  absRows.forEach(function(a) {
    const key = normKey_(a.username || a.nama);
    if (key && !absMap[key]) absMap[key] = a;
  });

  const lists = { belumAbsen: [], belumCheckout: [], libur: [], izin: [], alpa: [] };
  const outletMap = {};
  outlets.forEach(function(o) { if (o.namaOutlet) outletMap[normKey_(o.namaOutlet)] = { outlet: o.namaOutlet, target: 0, hadir: 0, belumCheckout: 0, capaian: 0 }; });

  jadwalRows.forEach(function(j) {
    const statusKey = normKey_(j.shift);
    const personKey = normKey_(j.username || j.nama);
    const absen = absMap[personKey];
    const outletName = j.outlet || (absen && absen.outlet) || '-';
    const outletKey = normKey_(outletName);
    if (!outletMap[outletKey]) outletMap[outletKey] = { outlet: outletName, target: 0, hadir: 0, belumCheckout: 0, capaian: 0 };

    if (statusKey === 'libur') { lists.libur.push({ nama: j.nama, username: j.username, outlet: outletName, shift: 'LIBUR' }); return; }
    if (statusKey === 'izin') { lists.izin.push({ nama: j.nama, username: j.username, outlet: outletName, shift: 'IZIN' }); return; }
    if (statusKey === 'alpa') { lists.alpa.push({ nama: j.nama, username: j.username, outlet: outletName, shift: 'ALPA' }); return; }

    outletMap[outletKey].target += 1;
    if (absen && absen.jamMasuk) {
      outletMap[outletKey].hadir += 1;
      if (!absen.jamPulang) {
        outletMap[outletKey].belumCheckout += 1;
        lists.belumCheckout.push({ nama: absen.nama || j.nama, username: absen.username || j.username, outlet: outletName, jamMasuk: absen.jamMasuk });
      }
    } else {
      const endMinutes = timeToMinutesV168_(j.jamPulangJadwal || parseEndTimeFromJamV168_(j.jam));
      if (endMinutes && nowMinutes > endMinutes) lists.alpa.push({ nama: j.nama, username: j.username, outlet: outletName, shift: j.shift || 'ALPA' });
      else lists.belumAbsen.push({ nama: j.nama, username: j.username, outlet: outletName, shift: j.shift || '-' });
    }
  });

  const detailAbsensi = absRows.map(function(a) {
    return { nama: a.nama || a.username || '-', username: a.username || '', outlet: a.outlet || '-', jamMasuk: a.jamMasuk || '-', jamPulang: a.jamPulang || '-', jamKeluar: a.jamPulang || '-' };
  });
  const lokasiAbsen = absRows.filter(function(a) { return a.jamMasuk; }).map(function(a) {
    return { nama: a.nama || a.username || '-', username: a.username || '', outlet: a.outlet || a.lokasi || '-', lokasi: a.outlet || a.lokasi || '-' };
  });
  const topLembur = absRows.filter(function(a) { return Number(a.totalLembur || 0) > 0; }).sort(function(a,b){ return Number(b.totalLembur || 0) - Number(a.totalLembur || 0); }).slice(0, 8).map(function(a){ return { nama: a.nama || a.username || '-', outlet: a.outlet || '-', totalLembur: Number(a.totalLembur || 0), menit: Number(a.totalLembur || 0) }; });
  const topTerlambat = absRows.filter(function(a) { return Number(a.terlambatMenit || 0) > 0; }).sort(function(a,b){ return Number(b.terlambatMenit || 0) - Number(a.terlambatMenit || 0); }).slice(0, 8).map(function(a){ return { nama: a.nama || a.username || '-', outlet: a.outlet || '-', menit: Number(a.terlambatMenit || 0), terlambatMenit: Number(a.terlambatMenit || 0) }; });

  const outletAccuracy = Object.keys(outletMap).map(function(k) {
    const o = outletMap[k];
    o.capaian = o.target ? Math.round((Number(o.hadir || 0) / Number(o.target || 1)) * 100) : 0;
    return o;
  }).filter(function(o) { return o.target || o.hadir || o.belumCheckout; }).sort(function(a,b){ return String(a.outlet).localeCompare(String(b.outlet)); });

  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    tanggal: today,
    todayLabel: formatDate_(todayDate, 'EEEE, dd MMMM yyyy'),
    syncAt: formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss'),
    user: publicUser_(currentUser),
    kpi: {
      totalKaryawan: users.length,
      hadir: detailAbsensi.length,
      belumAbsen: lists.belumAbsen.length,
      alpa: lists.alpa.length,
      libur: lists.libur.length,
      izin: lists.izin.length
    },
    outletAccuracy: outletAccuracy,
    detailAbsensi: detailAbsensi,
    belumAbsen: lists.belumAbsen,
    belumCheckout: lists.belumCheckout,
    lokasiAbsen: lokasiAbsen,
    topLembur: topLembur,
    topTerlambat: topTerlambat,
    karyawanLibur: lists.libur,
    karyawanIzin: lists.izin,
    karyawanAlpa: lists.alpa,
    calendar: buildAbsensiCalendarV168_(todayDate, users),
    pesan: 'Dashboard Absensi berhasil dimuat.'
  };
}

function readDashboardAbsensiRowsV168_(dateKey, isAdmin, currentUser) {
  let sh;
  try { sh = absensiSheet_(); } catch (err) { return []; }
  if (!sh) return [];
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  return table.rows.map(function(row) {
    const tanggalKey = inferAbsensiDateKey_(row) || inferDateKey_(row['Tanggal Key'] || row['Tanggal']);
    if (tanggalKey !== dateKey) return null;
    const username = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['USER'], row['User']);
    const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], username);
    if (!isAdmin) {
      if (normKey_(username) !== normKey_(currentUser.username) && normKey_(nama) !== normKey_(currentUser.nama)) return null;
    }
    return {
      username: username || '',
      nama: nama || '',
      outlet: firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['Lokasi'], row['OUTLET']),
      lokasi: firstNonEmpty_(row['Lokasi'], row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']),
      jamMasuk: normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Masuk'], row['Masuk'])),
      jamPulang: normalizeTime_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Jam Pulang'], row['Jam Keluar'], row['Pulang'])),
      terlambatMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Terlambat Menit'], row['Telat Menit'], row['Keterlambatan Menit'])),
      totalLembur: normalizeLateMinutes_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Total Lembur Aktual Menit'], row['Total Lembur Menit'], row['Lembur Menit'], row['Total Lembur Jam']))
    };
  }).filter(Boolean);
}

function buildDashboardUserMapV168_(users) {
  const map = {};
  (users || []).forEach(function(u) {
    if (u.username) map[normKey_(u.username)] = u;
    if (u.nama) map[normKey_(u.nama)] = u;
  });
  return map;
}

function buildDashboardShiftMapV168_(shifts) {
  const map = {};
  (shifts || []).forEach(function(s) {
    [s.namaShift, s.nama, s.kodeShift, s.kode].forEach(function(k) { if (k) map[normKey_(k)] = s; });
  });
  return map;
}

function findDashboardUserForRowV168_(row, users) {
  return (users || []).find(function(u) {
    return (row.username && normKey_(u.username) === normKey_(row.username)) || (row.nama && normKey_(u.nama) === normKey_(row.nama));
  });
}

function parseEndTimeFromJamV168_(jam) {
  const parts = String(jam || '').split('-');
  return parts.length > 1 ? parts[1].trim() : '';
}

function timeToMinutesV168_(time) {
  const m = String(time || '').match(/(\d{1,2})[:.](\d{2})/);
  if (!m) return 0;
  return Number(m[1]) * 60 + Number(m[2]);
}

function buildAbsensiCalendarV168_(dateObj, users) {
  const year = dateObj.getFullYear();
  const month = dateObj.getMonth();
  const days = new Date(year, month + 1, 0).getDate();
  const tanggalMerah = [];
  const redMap = {};
  function addRed_(day, label, tipe, tanggal) {
    day = Number(day || 0);
    if (!day) return;
    const dt = tanggal ? dateFromKey_(tanggal) : new Date(year, month, day);
    const dateKey = dt && dt.getFullYear ? formatDate_(dt, 'yyyy-MM-dd') : String(tanggal || '');
    const key = String(day);
    if (!redMap[key]) redMap[key] = [];
    const item = { day: day, tanggal: dateKey, date: dateKey, month: month + 1, year: year, label: label || 'Tanggal merah', tipe: tipe || 'tanggal_merah' };
    redMap[key].push(item);
    tanggalMerah.push(item);
  }
  for (let d = 1; d <= days; d++) {
    const dt = new Date(year, month, d);
    if (dt.getDay() === 0) addRed_(d, 'Minggu', 'minggu', formatDate_(dt, 'yyyy-MM-dd'));
  }
  getIndonesiaNationalCalendarV170_(year).forEach(function(h) {
    const dt = dateFromKey_(h.tanggal);
    if (dt && dt.getMonth && dt.getMonth() === month) addRed_(dt.getDate(), h.nama, h.tipe || 'libur_nasional', h.tanggal);
  });
  const ulangTahun = [];
  (users || []).forEach(function(u) {
    const raw = u.raw || {};
    const v = firstNonEmpty_(raw['Tanggal Lahir'], raw['TANGGAL_LAHIR'], raw['Tgl Lahir'], raw['TTL'], raw['Ulang Tahun'], raw['ULTAH']);
    const d = dashboardBirthdayDayV168_(v, month + 1);
    if (d) {
      const bDate = new Date(year, month, d);
      const bKey = formatDate_(bDate, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
      ulangTahun.push({ day: d, tanggal: bKey, date: bKey, month: month + 1, year: year, username: u.username || '', nama: u.nama || u.username || '-' });
    }
  });
  const pesanan = readDashboardPesananV168_(dateObj);
  return { tanggalMerah: tanggalMerah, ulangTahun: ulangTahun, pesanan: pesanan, viewKey: String(year) + '-' + String(month + 1).padStart(2, '0'), year: year, month: month + 1 };
}


function getIndonesiaNationalCalendarV170_(year) {
  year = Number(year || 0);
  if (!year || year < 1900 || year > 2200) return [];

  const cacheKey = 'APJ_ID_HOLIDAYS_' + year;
  try {
    const cached = CacheService.getScriptCache().get(cacheKey);
    if (cached) {
      const parsed = JSON.parse(cached);
      if (Array.isArray(parsed)) return parsed;
    }
  } catch (ignore) {}

  let rows = [];
  try {
    const url = 'https://date.nager.at/api/v3/PublicHolidays/' + year + '/ID';
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, {
      method: 'get',
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      followRedirects: true,
      headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json' }
    });
    const code = Number(response.getResponseCode && response.getResponseCode() || 0);
    if (code >= 200 && code < 300) {
      const data = JSON.parse(response.getContentText() || '[]');
      if (Array.isArray(data)) {
        rows = data.map(function(h) {
          const tanggal = String(h.date || '').trim();
          if (!/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(tanggal)) return null;
          if (Number(tanggal.slice(0, 4)) !== year) return null;
          const types = Array.isArray(h.types) ? h.types.join(',') : String(h.types || '');
          return {
            tanggal: tanggal,
            date: tanggal,
            nama: String(h.localName || h.name || 'Libur nasional').trim(),
            label: String(h.localName || h.name || 'Libur nasional').trim(),
            tipe: /optional|observance/i.test(types) ? 'peringatan_nasional' : 'libur_nasional',
            sumber: 'API_NAGER_DATE'
          };
        }).filter(Boolean);
      }
    }
  } catch (err) {
    // Jika API tidak bisa diakses, fallback fixed holiday tetap menjaga tanggal nasional utama.
  }

  if (!rows.length) rows = getIndonesiaNationalCalendarFallbackV170_(year);

  rows = dedupeIndonesiaHolidayRowsV170_(rows);
  try { CacheService.getScriptCache().put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(rows), 21600); } catch (ignore) {}
  return rows;
}

function getIndonesiaNationalCalendarFallbackV170_(year) {
  year = Number(year || 0);
  const rows = [];
  function add(mmdd, nama) {
    rows.push({
      tanggal: year + '-' + mmdd,
      date: year + '-' + mmdd,
      nama: nama,
      label: nama,
      tipe: 'libur_nasional',
      sumber: 'FALLBACK_FIXED'
    });
  }
  // Fallback hanya untuk libur nasional yang tanggalnya tetap setiap tahun.
  add('01-01', 'Tahun Baru Masehi');
  add('05-01', 'Hari Buruh Internasional');
  add('06-01', 'Hari Lahir Pancasila');
  add('08-17', 'Hari Kemerdekaan Republik Indonesia');
  add('12-25', 'Hari Raya Natal');
  return rows;
}

function dedupeIndonesiaHolidayRowsV170_(rows) {
  const seen = {};
  const out = [];
  (rows || []).forEach(function(r) {
    const tanggal = String(r && (r.tanggal || r.date) || '').trim();
    if (!tanggal) return;
    const key = tanggal + '|' + normKey_(r.nama || r.label || 'libur nasional');
    if (seen[key]) return;
    seen[key] = true;
    out.push({
      tanggal: tanggal,
      date: tanggal,
      nama: r.nama || r.label || 'Libur nasional',
      label: r.label || r.nama || 'Libur nasional',
      tipe: r.tipe || 'libur_nasional',
      sumber: r.sumber || 'AUTO'
    });
  });
  return out.sort(function(a, b) { return String(a.tanggal || '').localeCompare(String(b.tanggal || '')); });
}

function dashboardBirthdayDayV168_(value, targetMonth) {
  if (!value) return 0;
  if (value instanceof Date) return (value.getMonth() + 1) === targetMonth ? value.getDate() : 0;
  const s = String(value).trim();
  const m1 = s.match(/(\d{1,2})[\/\-](\d{1,2})(?:[\/\-]\d{2,4})?/);
  if (m1) return Number(m1[2]) === targetMonth ? Number(m1[1]) : 0;
  return 0;
}

function readDashboardPesananV168_(dateObj) {
  const out = [];
  let ss;
  try { ss = inventorySS_(); } catch (err) { return out; }
  const main = ss.getSheetByName('PESANAN_OUTLET');
  if (!main) return out;

  const detailMap = buildPesananOutletDetailMapV170_(ss);
  const table = readTable_(main);
  const mainValues = main.getDataRange().getValues().slice(1).filter(function(row) {
    return row.some(function(v) { return String(v || '').trim() !== ''; });
  });
  const targetYear = formatDate_(dateObj, 'yyyy');
  const targetMonth = formatDate_(dateObj, 'MM');
  const todayKey = formatDate_(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const nowMinutes = Number(formatDate_(new Date(), 'H')) * 60 + Number(formatDate_(new Date(), 'm'));

  table.rows.forEach(function(row, rowIndex) {
    const rawValues = mainValues[rowIndex] || [];
    const jamKolomN = rawValues.length >= 14 ? rawValues[13] : ''; // Kolom N = Jam Pesanan
    const noPesanan = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['No Pesanan'], row['NO PESANAN'], row['Nomor Pesanan'], row['No. Pesanan']) || '').trim();
    const key = inferDateKey_(firstNonEmpty_(row['Tanggal Pesanan'], row['TANGGAL PESANAN'], row['Tanggal'], row['Tanggal Ambil'], row['Tanggal Pengambilan']));
    if (!key) return;
    const dt = dateFromKey_(key);
    if (formatDate_(dt, 'yyyy') !== targetYear || formatDate_(dt, 'MM') !== targetMonth) return;
    if (key < todayKey) return;

    const jam = normalizePesananJamV191_(firstNonEmpty_(jamKolomN, row['Jam Pesanan'], row['Jam'], row['JAM'], row['Waktu'], row['Waktu Ambil']));
    if (key === todayKey && jam && timeToMinutesV168_(jam) && timeToMinutesV168_(jam) < nowMinutes) return;

    const status = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Status Pesanan'], row['STATUS PESANAN'], row['Status'], row['STATUS']) || '').trim();
    const statusKey = normKey_(status);
    if (/batal|cancel|void|hapus/i.test(statusKey)) return;

    const outlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET']) || '';
    const namaPesanan = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Pesanan'], row['Nama Pemesan'], row['Penerima'], row['Customer'], row['Pelanggan'], noPesanan || 'Pesanan');
    const jenisAmbil = firstNonEmpty_(row['Jenis Pengambilan'], row['Jenis Ambil'], row['Pengambilan']) || '';
    const detail = detailMap[normKey_(noPesanan)] || '';
    const labelParts = [];
    if (jam) labelParts.push(jam);
    if (outlet) labelParts.push(outlet);
    if (namaPesanan) labelParts.push(namaPesanan);
    if (detail) labelParts.push(detail);
    out.push({
      day: Number(formatDate_(dt, 'd')),
      tanggal: key,
      jam: jam || '',
      outlet: outlet,
      noPesanan: noPesanan,
      nama: namaPesanan || 'Pesanan',
      jenisPengambilan: jenisAmbil,
      status: status,
      detail: detail,
      label: labelParts.join(' • ')
    });
  });
  return out.sort(function(a,b) {
    const ak = String(a.tanggal || '') + ' ' + String(a.jam || '99:99');
    const bk = String(b.tanggal || '') + ' ' + String(b.jam || '99:99');
    return ak.localeCompare(bk);
  }).slice(0, 24);
}


function normalizePesananJamV191_(value) {
  if (value === undefined || value === null || String(value).trim() === '') return '';
  if (value instanceof Date) return formatDate_(value, 'HH:mm');
  if (typeof value === 'number' && isFinite(value)) {
    const totalMinutes = Math.round(Number(value) * 24 * 60);
    if (totalMinutes >= 0 && totalMinutes < 24 * 60) {
      const h = Math.floor(totalMinutes / 60);
      const m = totalMinutes % 60;
      return String(h).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(m).padStart(2, '0');
    }
  }
  const t = normalizeTime_(value);
  const m = String(t || '').match(/(\d{1,2})[:.](\d{2})/);
  return m ? String(m[1]).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(m[2]).padStart(2, '0') : t;
}

function buildPesananOutletDetailMapV170_(ss) {
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName('PESANAN_OUTLET_DETAIL');
  const map = {};
  if (!sh) return map;
  const table = readTable_(sh);
  table.rows.forEach(function(row) {
    const noPesanan = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['No Pesanan'], row['NO PESANAN'], row['Nomor Pesanan'], row['No. Pesanan']) || '').trim();
    if (!noPesanan) return;
    const namaLauk = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama Lauk'], row['NAMA LAUK'], row['Nama Item'], row['Item'], row['Jenis Pesanan']) || '';
    const qtyLauk = firstNonEmpty_(row['Qty Lauk'], row['QTY LAUK'], row['Qty Pesanan'], row['QTY'], row['Jumlah']) || '';
    const label = [qtyLauk, namaLauk].filter(Boolean).join('x ');
    const k = normKey_(noPesanan);
    if (!map[k]) map[k] = [];
    if (label) map[k].push(label);
  });
  Object.keys(map).forEach(function(k) {
    const arr = map[k];
    map[k] = arr.slice(0, 2).join(', ') + (arr.length > 2 ? ' +' + (arr.length - 2) + ' item' : '');
  });
  return map;
}


// =============================================================================
// APP-V.4.3 HR SHEET SYNC FIX - ABSENSI & REKAP READ FROM ID_ABSENSI
// =============================================================================
// Tujuan:
// 1) Absensi hari ini dan Rekap Absensi membaca sumber yang sama: sheet ID_ABSENSI.
// 2) Filter tanggal/nama/username/outlet lebih toleran untuk data lama dan data baru.
// 3) Tidak mengubah frontend, action API, payload, response utama, sheet, CSS, sidebar, dashboard.

function normalizeOutletKeyV43_(value) {
  let s = String(value || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  s = s.replace(/^outlet\s+/i, '').replace(/\boutlet\b/gi, '');
  return s.replace(/\s+/g, '').replace(/[_-]+/g, '');
}

function normalizeFilterKeyV43_(value) {
  const key = normKey_(value);
  if (!key || key === 'semua' || key === 'all' || key === 'semuakaryawan' || key === 'semuaoutlet' || key === 'semuastatus') return '';
  if (key === '-' || key === 'null' || key === 'undefined') return '';
  return key;
}

function parseIndonesianDateKeyV43_(value) {
  if (!value) return '';
  if (value instanceof Date) return formatDate_(value, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  const s = String(value || '').trim();
  if (!s) return '';
  const direct = inferDateKey_(s);
  if (direct) return direct;

  const monthMap = {
    jan: 1, januari: 1, january: 1,
    feb: 2, februari: 2, february: 2,
    mar: 3, maret: 3, march: 3,
    apr: 4, april: 4,
    mei: 5, may: 5,
    jun: 6, juni: 6, june: 6,
    jul: 7, juli: 7, july: 7,
    agu: 8, ags: 8, agust: 8, agustus: 8, aug: 8, august: 8,
    sep: 9, sept: 9, september: 9,
    okt: 10, oktober: 10, oct: 10, october: 10,
    nov: 11, november: 11,
    des: 12, desember: 12, dec: 12, december: 12
  };

  const m = s.match(/(\d{1,2})\s+([A-Za-zÀ-ÿ]+)\s+(\d{4})/i);
  if (m) {
    const d = Number(m[1]);
    const monName = String(m[2] || '').toLowerCase();
    const y = Number(m[3]);
    const mon = monthMap[monName] || monthMap[monName.slice(0, 3)] || 0;
    if (d && mon && y) return String(y) + '-' + String(mon).padStart(2, '0') + '-' + String(d).padStart(2, '0');
  }

  const parsed = new Date(s);
  if (!isNaN(parsed.getTime())) return formatDate_(parsed, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  return '';
}

function inferAbsensiDateKeyV43_(record) {
  record = record || {};
  let key = parseIndonesianDateKeyV43_(firstNonEmpty_(record['Tanggal Key'], record['Tanggal'], record['Created At'], record['Updated At']));
  if (key) return key;

  const id = String(firstNonEmpty_(record['ID Absensi'], record['ID_ABSENSI'], record['ID']) || '');
  const m = id.match(/(20\d{2})(\d{2})(\d{2})/);
  if (m) return m[1] + '-' + m[2] + '-' + m[3];
  return '';
}

function inferAbsensiDateKey_(record) {
  return inferAbsensiDateKeyV43_(record);
}

function rowAbsensiUserKeysV43_(record) {
  record = record || {};
  return {
    username: normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(record['Username'], record['User'], record['USERNAME'], record['Petugas Username'])),
    nama: normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(record['Nama'], record['Nama Lengkap'], record['Nama Karyawan'], record['NAMA'], record['Petugas'])),
    idAbsensi: normKey_(firstNonEmpty_(record['ID Absensi'], record['ID_ABSENSI'], record['ID']))
  };
}

function userMatchesAbsensiRowV43_(record, userOrFilter) {
  record = record || {};
  userOrFilter = userOrFilter || {};
  const keys = rowAbsensiUserKeysV43_(record);
  const username = normKey_(userOrFilter.username || userOrFilter.user || '');
  const nama = normKey_(userOrFilter.nama || userOrFilter.name || userOrFilter.namaLengkap || '');
  const raw = normKey_(userOrFilter.raw || userOrFilter.filter || '');
  if (username && keys.username && keys.username === username) return true;
  if (nama && keys.nama && keys.nama === nama) return true;
  if (raw) {
    if (keys.username && keys.username === raw) return true;
    if (keys.nama && keys.nama === raw) return true;
    if (keys.idAbsensi && keys.idAbsensi.indexOf(raw) >= 0) return true;
  }
  return false;
}

function absensiRowHasDataV43_(record) {
  record = record || {};
  return !!(
    normalizeTime_(record['Jam Masuk']) ||
    normalizeTime_(record['Jam Pulang']) ||
    firstNonEmpty_(record['ID Absensi'], record['ID_ABSENSI'])
  );
}

function readAbsensiRowsFromSheetV43_() {
  const table = readTable_(absensiSheet_());
  return (table.rows || []).map(function(row, idx) {
    return { rowNumber: idx + 2, record: row, tanggalKey: inferAbsensiDateKeyV43_(row) };
  }).filter(function(item) {
    return item.tanggalKey && absensiRowHasDataV43_(item.record);
  });
}

function findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, dateKey) {
  dateKey = inferDateKey_(dateKey) || dateKey || todayKey_();
  const rows = readAbsensiRowsFromSheetV43_();
  for (let i = rows.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    const item = rows[i];
    if (item.tanggalKey !== dateKey) continue;
    if (userMatchesAbsensiRowV43_(item.record, user)) return { row: item.rowNumber, record: item.record };
  }
  return null;
}

function readAbsensiHariIni_(user) {
  const found = findAbsensiRowForUser_(user, todayKey_());
  if (!found) {
    return {
      exists: false,
      tanggal: formatDate_(new Date(), 'dd/MM/yyyy'),
      tanggalKey: todayKey_(),
      username: user && user.username || '',
      nama: user && user.nama || '',
      outlet: user && user.outletUtama || '',
      jamMasuk: '',
      jamPulang: '',
      masuk: '',
      pulang: '',
      status: 'Belum Absen',
      statusMasuk: '',
      statusPulang: '',
      terlambatMenit: 0
    };
  }
  const data = recordToRiwayat_(found.record);
  if (!data.tanggalKey) data.tanggalKey = inferAbsensiDateKeyV43_(found.record);
  if (!data.username) data.username = firstNonEmpty_(found.record['Username'], user && user.username);
  if (!data.nama) data.nama = firstNonEmpty_(found.record['Nama'], found.record['Nama Lengkap'], user && user.nama);
  return data;
}

function rowToRekapAbsensiV43_(row) {
  row = row || {};
  const tanggalKey = inferAbsensiDateKeyV43_(row);
  const riwayat = recordToRiwayat_(row);
  const username = firstNonEmpty_(row['Username'], row['User'], row['USERNAME']);
  const nama = firstNonEmpty_(row['Nama'], row['Nama Lengkap'], row['Nama Karyawan'], row['NAMA']);
  const outlet = firstNonEmpty_(row['Outlet'], row['OUTLET'], row['Nama Outlet']);
  const jamMasuk = normalizeTime_(row['Jam Masuk']);
  const jamPulang = normalizeTime_(row['Jam Pulang']);
  const statusGabungan = String(firstNonEmpty_(row['Status Masuk'], '') + ' ' + firstNonEmpty_(row['Status Pulang'], '')).trim();
  return {
    idAbsensi: row['ID Absensi'] || row['ID_ABSENSI'] || '',
    tanggalKey: tanggalKey,
    tanggal: riwayat.tanggal || displayDate_(row['Tanggal']),
    username: username || '',
    nama: nama || '',
    level: row['Level'] || '',
    outlet: outlet || '',
    shift: row['Shift'] || '',
    jadwalMasuk: normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Masuk']),
    jadwalPulang: normalizeTime_(row['Jadwal Pulang']),
    jamMasuk: jamMasuk,
    jamPulang: jamPulang,
    statusMasuk: row['Status Masuk'] || '',
    statusPulang: row['Status Pulang'] || '',
    status: statusGabungan || (jamMasuk ? (jamPulang ? 'Selesai' : 'Sudah Check In') : 'Belum Absen'),
    terlambatMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Terlambat Menit']),
    totalKerjaMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Menit']),
    totalKerjaBersihMenit: normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit']),
    totalKerjaBersih: row['Total Kerja Bersih'] || minutesToDurationText_(normalizeLateMinutes_(row['Total Kerja Bersih Menit'] || row['Total Kerja Menit'])),
    totalLemburJam: number_(row['Total Lembur Jam']),
    totalLemburLabel: hoursToTextZeroV131_(number_(row['Total Lembur Jam'])),
    fotoMasuk: photoValueToUrl_(row['Foto Masuk']),
    fotoPulang: photoValueToUrl_(row['Foto Pulang']),
    updatedAt: row['Updated At'] || row['Created At'] || ''
  };
}

function isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(user) {
  const level = String(user && user.level || '').trim().toUpperCase().replace(/[\s_-]+/g, '');
  if (isBypassUser_(user)) return true;
  return ['OWNER', 'SUPERADMIN', 'SUPERVISOR', 'HR'].indexOf(level) >= 0;
}

function getRekapAbsensiV133(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const currentUser = getCurrentUser_(payload);
  assertUserActive_(currentUser);
  const isAdmin = isRekapAbsensiAdminV133_(currentUser);
  const startKey = inferDateKey_(payload.tanggalAwal || payload.startDate || payload.dari || payload.start) || firstDayOfMonthKeyV133_();
  const endKey = inferDateKey_(payload.tanggalAkhir || payload.endDate || payload.sampai || payload.end) || todayKey_();
  const outletFilter = normalizeFilterKeyV43_(payload.outlet || payload.outletFilter || payload.namaOutlet || '');
  const outletFilterClean = normalizeOutletKeyV43_(payload.outlet || payload.outletFilter || payload.namaOutlet || '');
  const statusFilter = normalizeFilterKeyV43_(payload.status || payload.statusFilter || '');
  const userFilterRaw = normText_(payload.userFilter || payload.usernameFilter || payload.namaFilter || payload.karyawan || payload.karyawanFilter || payload.usernameKaryawan || payload.namaKaryawan || '');
  const userFilterKey = normalizeFilterKeyV43_(userFilterRaw);
  const limit = Math.min(Math.max(Number(payload.limit || 1000), 1), 5000);
  const users = getActiveUsers_(true);
  const source = readAbsensiRowsFromSheetV43_();

  let scanned = 0;
  let dateMatched = 0;
  let userMatched = 0;
  let outletMatched = 0;
  let statusMatched = 0;

  let filtered = source.map(function(item) {
    scanned += 1;
    return rowToRekapAbsensiV43_(item.record);
  }).filter(function(r) {
    if (!r || !r.tanggalKey) return false;
    if (r.tanggalKey < startKey || r.tanggalKey > endKey) return false;
    dateMatched += 1;

    if (!isAdmin) {
      if (!userMatchesAbsensiRowV43_(r, currentUser)) return false;
    } else if (userFilterKey) {
      if (!userMatchesAbsensiRowV43_(r, { raw: userFilterKey })) return false;
    }
    userMatched += 1;

    if (outletFilter || outletFilterClean) {
      const rowOutlet = normalizeOutletKeyV43_(r.outlet);
      if (rowOutlet && outletFilterClean && rowOutlet !== outletFilterClean) return false;
      // Data lama yang outlet-nya kosong tetap ditampilkan jika tanggal/user cocok.
    }
    outletMatched += 1;

    if (statusFilter) {
      const combined = normKey_(String(r.statusMasuk || '') + ' ' + String(r.statusPulang || '') + ' ' + String(r.status || ''));
      if (statusFilter === 'tidakcheckout') {
        if (!(r.jamMasuk && !r.jamPulang)) return false;
      } else if (statusFilter === 'hadir') {
        if (!r.jamMasuk) return false;
      } else if (statusFilter === 'terlambat') {
        if (Number(r.terlambatMenit || 0) <= 0 && combined.indexOf('terlambat') < 0) return false;
      } else if (combined.indexOf(statusFilter) < 0) return false;
    }
    statusMatched += 1;
    return true;
  }).sort(function(a,b){
    return String(a.tanggalKey).localeCompare(String(b.tanggalKey)) || String(a.nama).localeCompare(String(b.nama)) || String(a.jamMasuk).localeCompare(String(b.jamMasuk));
  });

  const summary = buildRekapAbsensiSummaryV133_(filtered);
  const shown = filtered.slice(0, limit);
  return {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    pesan: 'Rekap Absensi APP-V.4.3 HR Sheet Sync berhasil dimuat dari ID_ABSENSI.',
    isAdmin: isAdmin,
    scope: isAdmin ? 'ALL' : 'SELF',
    scopeText: isAdmin ? 'Mode admin: semua karyawan' : 'Mode pribadi: data sendiri',
    tanggalAwal: startKey,
    tanggalAkhir: endKey,
    user: publicUser_(currentUser),
    users: isAdmin ? users.map(publicUser_) : [publicUser_(currentUser)],
    outlets: getActiveOutlets_().map(publicOutlet_),
    rows: shown,
    totalRows: filtered.length,
    summary: summary,
    debugRekapV43SheetSync: {
      sourceSheet: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI,
      scannedRows: scanned,
      dateMatched: dateMatched,
      userMatched: userMatched,
      outletMatched: outletMatched,
      statusMatched: statusMatched,
      startKey: startKey,
      endKey: endKey,
      userFilter: userFilterRaw || '',
      outletFilter: payload.outlet || payload.outletFilter || '',
      statusFilter: payload.status || payload.statusFilter || '',
      securityMode: currentUser.securityMode || ''
    },
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION
  };
}



// =============================================================================
// APP-V.4.5 OBSERVABILITY: AUDIT LOG, ERROR LOG, HEALTH CHECK
// Fail-safe: kegagalan log tidak boleh memutus absensi/transaksi utama.
// =============================================================================
const APJ_HR_AUDIT_HEADERS_V45 = ['Timestamp','App','Username','Nama','Role','Modul','Action','Target ID','Status','Message','Data Ringkas'];
const APJ_HR_ERROR_HEADERS_V45 = ['Timestamp','App','Username','Modul','Action','Message','Stack','Payload Ringkas','User Agent'];
const APJ_HR_HEALTH_HEADERS_V45 = ['Timestamp','App','Status','Message','Spreadsheet ID','Spreadsheet Name','Data Ringkas'];

function isObservabilityPublicActionHrV45_(action) {
  return ['ping','healthCheck','healthCheckV45','logClientError','logClientErrorV45'].indexOf(String(action || '')) !== -1;
}

function setupObservabilityHrV45(payload) {
  const ss = hrSS_();
  ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.AUDIT_LOG || 'AUDIT_LOG', APJ_HR_AUDIT_HEADERS_V45);
  ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ERROR_LOG || 'ERROR_LOG', APJ_HR_ERROR_HEADERS_V45);
  ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.HEALTH_CHECK || 'HEALTH_CHECK', APJ_HR_HEALTH_HEADERS_V45);
  appendHealthHrV45_({ status: 'READY', message: 'Observability HR Absensi siap.', data: { sheets: ['AUDIT_LOG','ERROR_LOG','HEALTH_CHECK'] } });
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Observability HR Absensi siap: AUDIT_LOG, ERROR_LOG, dan HEALTH_CHECK.', sheets: ['AUDIT_LOG','ERROR_LOG','HEALTH_CHECK'], version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function healthCheckHrV45(payload) {
  const hr = hrSS_();
  const core = coreSS_();
  const hrRequired = [APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ABSENSI, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_HARIAN, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.REKAP_BULANAN];
  const coreRequired = [APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.USER, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.OUTLET, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.SHIFT, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.JADWAL];
  const hrSheets = hrRequired.map(function(name) {
    const sh = hr.getSheetByName(name);
    return { name: name, exists: !!sh, rows: sh ? sh.getLastRow() : 0, cols: sh ? sh.getLastColumn() : 0 };
  });
  const coreSheets = coreRequired.map(function(name) {
    const sh = core.getSheetByName(name);
    return { name: name, exists: !!sh, rows: sh ? sh.getLastRow() : 0, cols: sh ? sh.getLastColumn() : 0 };
  });
  const audit = hr.getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.AUDIT_LOG || 'AUDIT_LOG');
  const error = hr.getSheetByName(APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ERROR_LOG || 'ERROR_LOG');
  const health = ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(hr, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.HEALTH_CHECK || 'HEALTH_CHECK', APJ_HR_HEALTH_HEADERS_V45);
  const missing = hrSheets.concat(coreSheets).filter(function(x) { return !x.exists; }).map(function(x) { return x.name; });
  const status = missing.length ? 'WARNING' : 'OK';
  const response = {
    sukses: true,
    success: true,
    app: 'APJ_HR_ABSENSI',
    version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION,
    serverTime: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'),
    spreadsheets: {
      hr: { id: hr.getId(), name: hr.getName(), sheets: hrSheets },
      core: { id: core.getId(), name: core.getName(), sheets: coreSheets }
    },
    observability: {
      auditLog: !!audit,
      errorLog: !!error,
      healthCheck: !!health,
      auditRows: audit ? Math.max(0, audit.getLastRow() - 1) : 0,
      errorRows: error ? Math.max(0, error.getLastRow() - 1) : 0,
      healthRows: health ? Math.max(0, health.getLastRow() - 1) : 0
    },
    status: status,
    message: missing.length ? ('Sheet hilang: ' + missing.join(', ')) : 'Health check HR Absensi OK'
  };
  appendHealthHrV45_({ status: status, message: response.message, data: { hrSheets: hrSheets, coreSheets: coreSheets, observability: response.observability } });
  return response;
}

function appendHealthHrV45_(info) {
  try {
    const ss = hrSS_();
    const sh = ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(ss, APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.HEALTH_CHECK || 'HEALTH_CHECK', APJ_HR_HEALTH_HEADERS_V45);
    sh.appendRow([Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'), 'APJ_HR_ABSENSI', normText_(info.status || 'OK'), normText_(info.message || ''), ss.getId(), ss.getName(), compactJsonHrV45_(info.data)]);
  } catch (ignore) {}
}

function logClientErrorHrV45(payload) {
  appendErrorHrV45_({
    username: payload.username || payload.user || '',
    modul: payload.page || payload.modul || 'FRONTEND',
    action: payload.actionName || payload.sourceAction || 'CLIENT_ERROR',
    message: payload.message || payload.error || 'Client error',
    stack: payload.stack || '',
    payload: payload,
    userAgent: payload.userAgent || ''
  });
  return { sukses: true, success: true, pesan: 'Client error dicatat.', version: APJ_HR_ABSENSI.VERSION };
}

function auditHrActionV45_(action, payload, result) {
  try {
    if (!isHrWriteActionV45_(action)) return;
    if (!result || result.success === false || result.sukses === false) return;
    const auth = payload && payload._auth && payload._auth.user ? payload._auth.user : {};
    const target = result.id || result.idAbsensi || result.absensiId || result.fileId || payload.id || payload.username || payload.nama || '';
    appendAuditHrV45_({
      username: auth.username || payload.username || '',
      nama: auth.nama || payload.nama || '',
      role: auth.level || payload.level || '',
      modul: 'HR_ABSENSI',
      action: action,
      targetId: target,
      status: 'SUCCESS',
      message: result.pesan || result.message || 'OK',
      data: summarizePayloadHrV45_(payload)
    });
  } catch (ignore) {}
}

function isHrWriteActionV45_(action) {
  const a = String(action || '');
  return /^(checkin|checkout|absenMasuk|absenPulang|save|export|setup|repair|refresh|install|hapus|delete)/i.test(a);
}

function logServerErrorHrV45_(err, payload) {
  appendErrorHrV45_({
    username: payload && payload.username,
    modul: 'HR_ABSENSI',
    action: payload && payload.action,
    message: err && err.message ? err.message : errorMessage_(err),
    stack: err && err.stack ? err.stack : '',
    payload: payload || {},
    userAgent: payload && payload.userAgent
  });
}

function appendAuditHrV45_(info) {
  try {
    const sh = ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(hrSS_(), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.AUDIT_LOG || 'AUDIT_LOG', APJ_HR_AUDIT_HEADERS_V45);
    sh.appendRow([nowHrV45_(), 'APJ_HR_ABSENSI', textHrV45_(info.username), textHrV45_(info.nama), textHrV45_(info.role), textHrV45_(info.modul), textHrV45_(info.action), textHrV45_(info.targetId), textHrV45_(info.status), textHrV45_(info.message), compactJsonHrV45_(info.data)]);
  } catch (ignore) {}
}

function appendErrorHrV45_(info) {
  try {
    const sh = ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(hrSS_(), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.SHEETS.ERROR_LOG || 'ERROR_LOG', APJ_HR_ERROR_HEADERS_V45);
    sh.appendRow([nowHrV45_(), 'APJ_HR_ABSENSI', textHrV45_(info.username), textHrV45_(info.modul), textHrV45_(info.action), textHrV45_(info.message), textHrV45_(info.stack), compactJsonHrV45_(info.payload), textHrV45_(info.userAgent)]);
  } catch (ignore) {}
}

function ensureSheetWithHeadersHrV45_(ss, name, headers) {
  let sh = ss.getSheetByName(name);
  if (!sh) sh = ss.insertSheet(name);
  if (sh.getLastRow() < 1) sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  return sh;
}

function summarizePayloadHrV45_(payload) {
  const keep = {};
  ['action','tanggal','tanggalAwal','tanggalAkhir','username','nama','outlet','status','shift','id','idAbsensi'].forEach(function(k) {
    if (payload && payload[k] !== undefined) keep[k] = payload[k];
  });
  return keep;
}

function nowHrV45_() { return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), APJ_HR_ABSENSI.TIMEZONE, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss'); }
function textHrV45_(v) { return String(v == null ? '' : v).trim(); }
function compactJsonHrV45_(value) {
  try {
    const text = JSON.stringify(value || {});
    return text.length > 800 ? text.slice(0, 800) + '…' : text;
  } catch (err) { return ''; }
}
